bhavabhūteḥ sambandhādbhūdharabhūreva bhāratī bhāti etatkṛtakāruṇye kimanyathā roditi grāvā  govardhanaḥ yadyapyasya kaveritivṛttaṃ sākalyena na kvāpyupalabhyate tathāpyanena mahākavinā svavira eva kecinnāndyante sthāpaka ityevaṃ paṭhanti nanu prastāvanāyāḥ pūrva vahūni nāṭyāṅgāni santi tāni kimiti noktāni yadāha bharataḥ raṅgaprasādamadhuraiḥ ślokaiḥ kāvyārthasūcakaiḥ ṛtuṃ kaṃcidupādāya bhāratī vṛttimāśrayet bhedaiḥ prarocanāyuktairvārthiprahasanāmukhaiḥ sūtradhāro nahīṃ brūte māriṣaṃ vā vidūṣakam svakārya prastutākṣepi citroktyā yattadāmukham ata evāhaalamiti ayamāśayaḥ  pūrvoktānyāni na bhavanti kiṃntu pariṣadobhimukhīkaraṇāni sā cetsvayameva kṛtāvadhānā navanāṭakavilokanotkā ca mānamapi rasabhaṅgāya paraṃ bhavatīti kṛtaṃ tatpraṇayanena anyathā sabhāyā bhavediti niṣphalateti aye iti nipāto vyāsaṅgādinānākalitasyākalanena saṃbhramavācakaḥ akasmātsūryodayākalanāt  tataḥ ślokaṃ paṭhedekaṃ gambhīrasvarasaṃyutam devastotraṃ puraskṛtya yasya pūjā pravartate  iti bharatamatamanumasya māṅgalikatayā raṅgadvārapāṭhyaṃ ślokamutthāpayati  uditeti uditaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bahu yasya saḥ nekṣedāasya bahutarabhāga uditaḥ kiṃcidevodayāyāvaśiṣyata iti bhāvaḥ atra dityamudyantam iti niṣedhāduditabhūyiṣṭa ityuktam bhagaṃ jñānādisaṃpattistadvān bhatadanyatprayujyarasavicchedo alamalam puro prācīma sa eva nambaramaṇiḥ dīpaḥ  dīpaka tamu tadenamuprathamoṅkaḥ kalyāṇānāṃ tvamasi mahasāṃ bhājanaṃ viśvamūrte dhuryā lakṣmīmarthaṃ mayi bhṛśaṃ dhehi deva prasīda yadyatpāpaṃ pratijahi jagannātha namrasya tanme bhadraṃ bhadraṃ vitara bhagavanbhūyase maṅgalāya nepathyābhimukhamavalokya māriṣa suvihitāni raṅgamaṅgalāni saṃnipatitaśca bhagavataḥ kālapriyanāthasya yātrāprasaṅgena nānādigantavāstavyo mahājana samājaḥ ādiṣṭaścāsmi vidvajjanapariṣadā yathā kenacidapūrvaprakaraṇena vayaṃ vinodayitavyā iti tatkimityudāsate bharatāḥ gavānityarthaḥ upatiṣṭhe ślokeneti śeṣaḥ tadevāhakalyāṇānāmityādi bho viśvamūrte sarvamayadeva dīvyatīti devo dyutimāṃstādṛśa he kalyāṇānāṃ mahasāṃ māṅga likānāṃ tejasāṃ tvaṃ bhājanaṃ pātramasi ataḥ prasīda prasanno bhava mayi madviṣaye dhuryo nṛtyadhuraṃdharāṃ lakṣmīṃ saṃpattimapi bhṛśamatiśayena dhehyāropaya athaśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ dhehīti sthāne dehīti pāṭhe dadasvetyarthaḥ tathā he jagannātha bhuvanapate yadyatpāpamārabdhaviruddhaṃ namrasya mesti tatpratijahi nāśaya yadyaditi vīpsayā kāyikavācikamānasikarūpaṃ pāpatrayamuktam vīpsā tu na tacchavde kṛtā vīpsitasyaiva tacchabdena parāmarśāttathaiva vyutpatteḥ kvacidyatpada iva tatpadepi vīpsā yathā  yāṃ yāṃ priyāṃ praikṣata ityādau bhadramadoṣaṃ bhadramabhīṣṭaṃ vitara dehi yadvā bhadraṃ bhadramatiśayenābhīṣṭaṃ dehītyarthaḥ kimartham maṅgalāyāśaṃsanīyakarmārtham tādarthye caturthī maṅgalāya maṅgalaṃ kartumiti vā kīdṛśāya bhūyase pracurāya tadiha hariharādīnapāsya bhānorupasthānena prakaraṇanāyakasya brāhmaṇyaṃ sūcitam ata eva dehīti brāhmaṇocitā prārthanā sarvakṣudrasattvakṣayahetoḥ prabhātasyādareṇa prakaraṇakathābījasūcanamapi tathāhi yadyaditi vīpsayā śārdūlāghoraghaṇṭavimardasūcanam pāpapratighātānantaraṃ ca bhadraṃ bhadramiti vīpsayā svasya mālatīlābhena makarandasya ca madayantikālabheneṣṭasiddhiḥ sūcitā bhūyo maṅgalapadena kapālakuṇḍalāpakṛtamālatīlābho vidyālābhādikaṃ ca sūcitam nepathyota nepathyaṃ raṅgabhūmiḥ nepathyaṃ raṅgabhūmau syāt  iti viśvaḥ mānyo bhāveti vaktavyaḥ kiṃcinnyūnastu māriṣaḥ ityamaraḥmāriṣa eva marṣaṇānmārṣaḥ sūtradhāroktanirvāhasahiṣṇurityarthaḥ suvihitāni bhaktiśraddhākṛtāni raṅgo nṛtyaṃ tadartha maṅgalāni lokapālapūjāādīni raṅgo nṛtye raṇakṣitau iti viśvaḥsaṃnipatitaḥ sarvata āgatyaikatra militaḥ kālapriyanāthasya taddeśadeva tvamiha mahasāmīśiṣe tvaṃ vidhatse puṇyām iha samūhaḥ janaḥ tatkimi tyudāsate bharatāḥ ādiṣṭosmi vidvatpariṣadayathā  adya tvayāpūrvavastuprayogeṇa vayaṃ vinodayitavyā iti tatpariṣadaṃ nirdiṣṭaguṇaprabandhanopatiṣṭhāvaḥ mālatīmāghave praviśya pauripārśvikaḥ  bhāva pariṣannirdiṣṭaguṇaṃ prabandhaṃ nauvagacchāmaḥ sūtradhāra   māriṣa katame te guṇāstatra yānaidāharantyāryavidagdhamiśrā bhagavanto bhūmidevāśca naṭaḥbhūmnā rasānāṃ gahanāḥ prayogāḥ sauhārdahṛdyāni viceṣṭitāni auddhatyamāyojita kāmasūtraṃ citrāḥ kathā vāci vidagdhatā ca bhedasya yātrāprasaṅgeneti nṛtyakālasūcanam  idaṃ dhvajamahaḥ śrīmanmahendrasya pravartate ityabhidhānāt vāstavyo vāsī mahājanasamājo vigoṣṭhī udāsata udāsīnā bhavanti bharatā naṭāḥ pāripārśvikalakṣaṇaṃ bharate  sūtradhārasya pārśve yaḥ pravacankuruterthanām kāvyārthasūcanālāpaṃ sa bhavetpāripārśvikaḥ  iti bhāva mānyanaṭa pariṣadā prekṣakeṇa nirdiṣṭo guṇo yatra taṃ prabandhaṃ prakaraṇam prekṣakastuyastuṣṭe tuṣṭimāyāti śoke śokamupaiti ca kruddhaḥ kruddhe bhaye bhītaḥ sa nāṭye prekṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ  iti bharatoktaḥ pūjāvākyagarbha praśnamāha  katama iti gotraṃ nāma ca banīyātpūjāvākyaṃ ca sarvataḥ  iti bharataḥ katame kiyanta ityarthaḥ āryāḥ sukulādisaṃpannāḥ yadāha bharataḥ   kulaṃ śīlaṃ dayā dānaṃ dharmaḥ satyaṃ kṛtajñatā adroha iti yeṣvetattānāryānsaṃpracakṣate vidagdhāścatuḥṣaṣṭikala vedinaḥ miśrā vedāntavedinaḥ bhagavantaḥ smṛtidharāḥ yadāha  devāśca liṅginaścaiva nānāsmṛtidharāśca ye bhagavāniti te vācyāḥ puruṣāḥ striya eva ca iti yadvā ārādyātā dūraṃ gatāḥ grāmyatvādidoṣebhya ityāryāḥ vidagdhāḥ vaśamanasaḥ miśrāḥ pūjyāḥ pūjye miśrapadaṃ nityaṃ bahuvacanāntam marīcimiśrairdakṣeṇa  iti viṣṇupurāṇāt bhagavanto jñānādisaṃpannā bhūmidevā brāhmaṇāḥ iha tatroddhātakarūpā prastāvanā yadāha bharataḥ  supratītaṃ vismṛtaṃ vā yatra kārye prakāśyate taduddhātakamityāhuḥ praśnottaramanoharam  iti prabandhe guṇānāha  bhūmneti yatra prabandhe rasānāṃ śṛṅgārādīnāṃ bhūmnā prācuryeṇa gahanā gambhīrāḥ sahṛdayamātragrāhyāḥ prayogāḥ santi etenāsya rasamayatvamuktam yatra prabandhe vicoṣṭitāni mālatīmādhavādeḥ paraspavyāpārāḥ sauhārdena premṇā hṛdyāni manojñāni yatrauddhatyaṃ nāyakanāyikāsakhībhṛtyādiguṇamāhātmyamasti kīdṛśam āyojitaṃ vihitaṃ kāsasūtramanaṅgaprayogo yatra tat yadvā auddhatyaṃ nijotkarṣapuraḥsaramanyāvajñāviṣkaraṇam taccāyojitasya samantātkāryābhimukhīkṛtasya kāmasya manmathecchāyāḥ sūtraṃ sūcakam sūtraṃ saṃbhogaḥ paṭārambhastanturvā anenātra kākāvyarasanaṭaḥ  praviśya bhāva kaname te guṇayānudārahantyārthamiśrā bhagavanto bhūmidevāḥ sūtradhāraḥ  bhūnā i naṭaḥ  bhāva kasminprakaraṇe sūtraḥ  vicintya smṛtam asti dakṣiṇāpathe  i pāṭhāntaram nādhi anuvartante āryā vidvadvidagdhaprathamoṅkaḥ sūtradhāraḥ smṛtaṃ tarhi naṭaḥ  bhāva kimivai sūtradhāra  asti dakṣiṇāpathe vidarbheṣu padmapuraṃ nāma nagaram tatra kecittaittirīyiṇaiḥ kāśyapāścaraṇaguravaḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ pañcāgnayo ghṛtavratāḥ somapīthino udumbairanāmāno brahmavādinaḥ prativasarttiṃ te śrotriyāstattvaviniścayāya bhūri śrutaṃ śāśvatamādriyante iṣṭāya pūrtāya ca karmaṇerthāndārānapatyāya taporthamāyuḥ moddīpaka tayauddhatyaṃ guṇāya svābhāvikasya tasya bhūṣaṇatvamiti darśitam yatra citrāścaryajanikā kathā kalpitakathatvāt rasamayatvāccāścaryam vāci vacane vidagdhatā paripāko nirdoṣatvaṃ vakratā ca yatra etenānyanāṭakādasyādhika guṇavattvamuktam taṃ prabandhaṃ nartitamādiśanti miśrā iti śeṣaḥ naṭaḥ  kimiva kiṃ smṛtamityarthaḥ adhunā ruṇaddhi rodasī vāsya yāvatkīrtiranaśvarī tāvatkilāyamadhyāste sukṛtaṃ vaibudhaṃ padam  iti nijanāmādikathanaphalamanurudhya tadācarateastītyādi dakṣiṇadeśasya śṛṅgārarasavaśatayā taddeśajatvena svasya tadubhayarasavarṇanaśaktiruktā vidarbheṣvityanena vaidarbhīrītiparicayacāturī darśitā padmanagaraṃ padmāvatī nāma prasiddhau na tu nāmapadama bhidhānārtham tadā prakṛtyāditvāttṛtīyā syādityavadhayem taittirīyiṇaḥ taittirīyakanāmaśākhā viśeṣapāṭhina ityarthaḥ kāśyapāḥ kāśyapagotrāḥ caraṇagurava iti caraṇaśavdaḥ śākhāviśeṣādhyayanaparaikatāpannajanasaṅghavācī tatra samūhe te guravaḥ kriyāṃ kṛtvā vedādhyāpayitāraḥ sa gururyaḥ kriyāṃ kṛtvā vedamasmai prayacchati iti smateḥ yadvā caraṇaiḥ kalāpādibhirguravo mahāntaḥ paṅkṣipāvanāḥ pakau bhojanādigoṣṭayāṃ pāvanā agrabhojinaḥ pavitrā vetyarthaḥ yadvā yajuṣāṃ pārago yastu sāmnāṃ yaścāpi pāragaḥ atharvaśirasodhyetā brāhmaṇaḥ paṅkipāvanaḥ  iti lakṣitāḥ pañcāgnayo dakṣiṇagnigārhapatyāhavanīyasabhyāvasathyarūpāgnipañcakopāsakāḥ dhṛtavratāścāndrāyaṇādivratayoginaḥ somapīthinaḥ somo latāviśeṣo hutaśeṣo vā tatpāyinaḥ anena somayāgayā jitvamuktam ḍambaranāmāno ḍambaramutkarṣasūcakaṃ kulanāma yeṣāṃ te yadvā ḍambaraṃ prasiddhaṃ nāma yeṣāṃ te prasiddhau ḍambaraṃ viduḥ iti viśvaḥ brahmavādinaḥ vedajñā ityarthaḥ ta ityādi kathitarūpāḥ śrotriyāśchandodhyetāraḥ janmādisaṃpannā brāhmaṇā vā bhūri pracuram śāśvataṃ sārvakālikam śrutamadhyayanamā driyante śraddadhati yadvā śāśvataṃ nityāgamaṃ vedākhyamādriyante kīdṛśam bhūri śrutaṃ bahubhyo bahudhā bahubhiḥ sahābhyastam kimartham dharmasya kartavyākartavyarūpasya viniścayāya nirṇayāya vaidikakarmaṇi nirṇayādeva pra ka iva nagaraṃ taittirīyā pītinaḥ thino brāhmaṇāḥ ḍambara audu vasanti sma vinirṇayāyamālatīmādhave tedāmupyāyaṇasya tatrabhavataḥ sugṛhītanāmno bhaṭṭagopālasya pautraḥ pavitrakīrternīlakaṇṭhasyātmaisaṃbhavo bhaṭṭaśrīkaṇṭhapadalāñchano bhavabhūtirnāma jātūkarṇīputraḥ kavirnisargasaudena bharateṣu svakṛtimevaprāya guṇabhūyasīmasmākamarpitavān yartre khalviyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ ye nāma kecidiha naḥ prathayantyavajñāṃ jānanti te kimapi tānprati naiṣa yatnaḥ utpatsyeṃtesti mama kopi samānadharmā kālo hyayaṃ niravadhirvipulā ca pṛthvī vṛtteriti bhāvaḥ śrotriyaśchandodhīte iti pāṇinisūtram janmanā brāhmaṇo jñeyaḥ saṃskārairdvija ucyate vidyayā yāti vipratvaṃ tribhiḥ śrotriya ucyate  iti smṛtiḥ śāśvatamityatra kālājaṃ bādhitvā śāśvate pratiṣedha iti bhāṣyavacanādaṇ tathā terthāndhanānyādriyante iṣṭāya karmaṇe yāgādikāryārtham pūrtāya karmaṇe khātādikāryārtham yāgādīnāṃ dhanasādhyatayā teṣāṃ tadādaro na tu bhogāyeti bhāvaḥ dārānpatnīrādriyante apatyāya saṃtatyarthaṃ na tu kāmāyetyarthaḥ ta āyurjīvitamādriyante taporthaṃ tapaścaraṇārthaṃ na tu vyasanārtham kleśabahulaṃ dharmya karma tapaḥ tadanena teṣāṃ sarvaguṇavatvaṃ darśitam bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhūyaśca bhūri ca ityamaraḥ atha ṛtukarmeṣṭaṃ pūrte khātādikarmaṇi puṃbhūmni dārāḥ iti ca viniścayāyetyādau tādarthye caturthī atra kule jāta āmuṣyāyaṇaḥ tatrabhavataḥ pūjyasya sugṛhītaṃ śobhanoccāraṇaṃ balikarṇādivanmaṅgalyaṃ nāma yasya bhaṭṭaścatuḥśākhābhijñaḥ pavitrā puṇyā kīrtiryasya tasyātmasaṃbhavaḥ putraḥ śrīḥ sarasvatī kaṇṭhe yasya sa śrīkaṇṭhaḥ tadvācakaṃ padaṃ lāñchanaṃ cihnaṃ yasya saḥ nāmnā śrīkaṇṭhaḥ prasiddhayā bhavabhūtirityarthaḥ śrīveṃśara canāśobhābhāratīsaraladruṣu iti medinīkaraḥ jatukarṇagotraprasūtaḥ jātūkarṇī tasyāḥ putraḥ nisargasauhṛdena sāhajikasauhārdena nanu hṛdbhagasindhvante pūrvapadasya ca ityubhayavṛddhayā sauhārdamiti syāt ucyate hṛdityādau pratipadoktasya grahaṇāt hṛdayasya hṛllekha   iti hṛdādeśasyādivṛddhiḥ yadvā saṃjñāpūrvako vidhiranityaḥ iti vacanādubhayapadavṛddheranityatvam yadvā suhṛdurhṛdau mitrāmitrayoḥ iti nipātasya suhṛcchabdasyāvayavo hṛcchabdastadantottarapadavṛddhirbhavati evaṃprāyaguṇabhūyasīṃ bhūmnā rasānām ityādiprāyairguṇairupacitāmarpitavānprayogatorthataśca saṃkramitavān khalu prasiddhau vākyabhūṣāyāṃ vā vācoyuktirvacanaracanam vāgdikpaśyadbhyo yuktidaṇḍahareṣu iti ṣaṣṭyaluka tyādi iha tāvatrividhāḥ saṃprati svakauśalabalena sagarvamāha ye nāmepuruṣāḥ kecidajñā eva kecidadvaitamatamagnamanasaḥ kāvyarasavirasāḥ itare sahṛdayahṛdayāmodikāvyabhavyarasabhararasikāḥ tatrādyā tatrā kīrtiḥ ātmajaḥ padavākyapramāṇajñaḥ bhava bhavabhūtināmā sauhārdena dena vartamānaḥ evaṃguṇa asmākaṃ haste tatra tasya kaveḥ syate caprathamoṅkaḥ e api ca yadvedādhyayanaṃ taṃthopaniṣadāṃ sāṃkhyasya yogasya ca jñānaṃ tatkathanena kiṃ nāha tataḥ kaścidguṇo nāṭake yatprauḍhitvamudāratā ca vacasāṃ yancārthato gauravaṃ taccedasti tatastadeva gamakaṃ pāṇḍityavaidagdhyayoḥ sa npratyāhaye kecidajñā nosmākamiha prabandhevajñāmavardhāraṇaṃ prathayanti khyāpayanti nāma saṃbhāvanāyām saṃbhāvyata iva na tu vāstavamityarthaḥ te kimapi kiṃcidalpaṃ jānanti tānprati tākṣīkṛtya mama naiṣa yatnaḥ na hi badhire gīyate yadvā kiṃśabda ākṣepe te kiṃ jānanti kiṃtu na jānantītyarthaḥ dvitīyānpratyāha  ye nāma niścaye vaiṣayikasukhavimukhā mumukṣava ihāvadhīraṇāmācaranti te kimapi vāḍmanasāgocaraṃ paraṃ brahma jānanti te namasyāstānprati mama naiṣa yatnaḥ na hi samrājamadhikṛtya kaupīnaṃ sūtryata iti bhāvaḥ antyānpratyāha sama taṃ pramānadharmā tulyaguṇaḥ kopi jana utpatsyate janmāpsyatyasti vidyate vā tyeṣa yatna iti bhāvaḥ ihālpajñatvena sādharmyamanauddhatyāya bahujñatvena sādharmya kadaryadurjanavivarjanāyetyubhayatra vivakṣā athedānīmanutpannasya kathamutpādotrānupalabdhasya vā kathamupalambha ityubhayayogyatāmāha  yataḥ kāloyaṃ niravadhirvigatāvasānaḥ vipulā mahatī ca pṛthvī bhūmiḥ tathā ca tasyedānīmanutpannasya kālāntara utpāda ihānupalabdhasya deśāntara upalambhaśca syāditi bhāvaḥ iha prathamārdhe bahutvena prayogo dvitīyārdha ekatvena prayogaśca na doṣaḥ bhinnavākyārthatvāt ekavākyārthatve tādṛkprayogasyāyogyatayā doṣatvāt tathaiva vyutpattarityavadheyam yadvā avajñāprathāvasarehaṃkāreṇātmano gauravāhutvaṃ nijasamatāvasare śāntyātmanyekatvam yadvā jātyabhiprāyamekavacanam adhunā nijaguṇagarimopadarśanena nijagranthe vidagdhādaramāha   yadetyādi yatra khalviyaṃ vācoyuktirityatrāpyanuṣajyate advaitapratipādako vedabhāga upaniṣattajjñānam yogaḥ pātañjalaśāstram tayoradhyayanajñānayoḥ kathanena kim api tu na kimapītyarthaḥ yatastato vedādhyayanādernāṭake kaścidguṇo nāsti teṣāṃ nāṭakenupayogāt tata iti lyavlope pañcamī tānprāpya nāṭake na kaścidruṇa ityarthaḥ vayaṃ sarvameva vidmaḥ anaṅga tayā punastadatra na nibaddhamiti bhāvaḥ tarhyatra kavervedādijñānajñāpanaṃ kimarthamata āhayaditi vacasāṃ yatprauḍhatvaṃ vākyārthe padaṃ padārthe vākyaṃ tatkṛtiḥ yathā na daivīyaṃ kiṃ tu mānuṣītyarthe nimeṣavatī guṇaiḥ satāṃ na mama ko guṇaḥ prakhyāpito bhavet yathārthanāmā bhagavānyasya jñānanidhiryaruḥ A asmātprāk  taducyantāṃ tatprakhyāpanāya sarve kuśīlavā yathā  svasaṃgītaka prayoga vārṇakāparigrahe ca tvaryatāmiti kavivarṇanāṃ prati tenaivamuktam  mālatīmādhave ato yadasmākamarpitaṃ priyasuhṛdā taṃtrabhavatā bhūyo bhūyaḥ savidhanagarīrathyayā paryaṭantaṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā bhavanavalabhītuṅgavātāyanasthā sākṣātkāmaṃ navamiva ratirmālatī mādhavaṃ ya gāḍhotkaṇṭhā lulitalulitairaṅga kaistāmyatīti śrobhau vañcanīyau tayoranyonyānurāgādeva pariṇayo vṛtto na mayā kārita iti vaktavyameveti bhāvaḥ sārvalaukika ityatra sarvalokān anyonyānurāgeṇa gāndharvavivāhopi sūcitaḥ bāharityādi vidvānsubuddhirekaḥ śreṣṭodvitīyo vā sakalaṃ janaṃ kapaṭairata bhi sandhāya vañcayitvā strānarthānsvaprayojanāni sampādayati maunamabhāṣaṇaṃ bhajate ca vidhiniṣedhaparaṃ vaco na vadatītyarthaḥ ataḥ eva taṭastha udāsīna ivānabhivyaktavyāpāra ityarthaḥ katham sarvākāreṇoṅgatādinā svabhāvasundaraṃ yathā bhavati tathā bahiḥ pragaṭaṃ vyavaharannatisūkṣmāṇyapi parābhyūhasthānāni parasya tarkasthānāni sthagayati pidadhāti apirmiṃnnakramaḥ atisandhirvaca nārthaḥ iti dhātusaṃgrahaḥ kevalaśreṣṭhayorekaḥ iti dharaṇiḥ avalokitā atropanyāso vyājena kāryodbhedaḥ rājamārgeṇetyanena sarvasādhāraṇyānmādhava syānauddha tyamadvitīyavedyatā ca sūcitā sañcāraṇaṃ ca taddarśanena mālatyā anurāgāyeti bhāvaḥ atra kāmandakyāvalokitāyāmevamanuktatvātkathaṃ tava vacanāditighaṭata iti na deśyam prāṇaistapobhirityādinā tadabhidhānāt kāmandakī dhātreyupamātṛsutā etena vālyātprabhṛti sakalaceṣṭāveditvaṃ dhvanitam tathā ca lavaṅgikā mālatīgataṃ yatkathayati tatpramāṇamevetyevakāravyamayam anenāsyāḥ sakhītvamapyuktam yadāha bharataḥ  kārusī ca dhātreyī prativeśyā ca śilpikā bālā pravrajitā ceti nāyikānāṃ sakhījanaḥ  iti na iti bahuvacanenātmani lavaṅgikāhṛdayajāgarūkabahumānena vañcakatānirāsaḥ sūcitaḥ bhūya ityādi mālatyaṅgakaistāmyati vidyata iti kathitameva lavadbhikayetyanvayaḥ aṅgakairityatrā pravaṇa abhisaṃ sannatara lalitaprathamoṅkaḥ ava  bāḍham tayāpyātmano vinodanimittaṃ mādhavapraticchandakamālikhitaṃ talluvaṅgikayā mandārikāyā hastedya nihitaṃ tāvat bāḍham taue vi attaṇo viṇodaṇimittaṃ māhavapaḍicchandaaṃ lihiaṃ taṃ lavabhiāe mandāriāe hatthe ṇihideṃ dāva lpārthe kan alpatā mṛdutvena bahuvacanātsarvāṅgamuktam tathā ca mṛdubhiḥ sarvāṅgai rityarthaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ taṃ mādhavaṃ dṛṣṭā dṛṣṭā punaḥ punaravalokya gāḍhotkaṇṭhayā dṛḍhākāḍṅkṣayā lulitalulitairatimlānakāntibhiḥ lalitalulitaiḥ iti pāṭhe pūrva lalite ramyairadhunā lulitaimlanairityarthaḥ kīdṛśam savidhanagarīrathyayā mālatīgṛhanikaṭarājamārgeṇa bhūyo bhūyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ paryaṭantaṃ gacchantam iha rājamārgopanyāsena mādhavasya niḥśaṅkaḥ sañcāro mālatyāñca taddarśanena paravitarkābhāvaḥ sūcitaḥ gamane paunaḥpunyena darśanaṃ prati dārḍhyamuktam darśane ca paunaḥpunyena tasyā utkaṇṭhātiśaya uktaḥ yadvā prathamavīpsayā darśanaṃ dṛṣṭvānuvṛttyā prathamaṃ ramyavastucamatkāreṇa tata udbhidyamānānurāganavāḍareṇa netraprītiryujyate dvitīyavīpsayā sahacarībhirapyajñātā nayanaprītiruktā nagarīpadena rathyāyā anekakautukādhāratoktā tathā cetastatonekakautukadarśanatarali na nira tatvena mādhavasya samyagdarśanasampādakanikaṭārthakasavidhapadanigarva uktaḥ ktvāpratyayena cānantarabhāvivihvalatāyā viṣayāntarasañcāreṇāpi vyavadhānasyāpādanādatyantānurāgodbhedaḥ kathamantaḥpurasthā sā dadarśetyata āha  bhavaneti bhavanasya prāsāsūcitaḥ dāderyā valabhyuparikuṭī tasyāḥ tuṅgamuccaṃ yadvātāyanaṃ gavākṣastatrasthā  tuṅgatayā yathākrāḍkṣaṃ darśanamuktam vātāyanetyanena vātasyāyanaṃ gamanaṃ yatreti vyutpattyā dharmādi tāpavatī gabhīrasamīrapariśīlanārtha yātīti praroheṇa nirargalamasyā gamanaṃ tatreti sūcitam yadyapi  saudhoparikuṭīṃ valabhī viduḥ iti bhavanapadamatra gatārtha tathā yuktipoṣālaṅkāradyotanārthaṃ bhavanapadam yadvā bhavanarūpā valabhī mālatīvasatiḥ saudhoparikuṭītyarthaḥ etenāsyā nijagṛhādvalabhīgamanaṃ kimarthamityanyāśaṅkāparihāro nirargalaṃ ca taddarśanaṃ bhavatīti dhvanitam yathā ratiḥ kāmakāntā navaṃ dāhānantaramutpannaṃ sākṣātpratyakṣaṃ kāmaṃ dṛṣṭvāḍgaistāmyati tathetyarthaḥ mālatī ratirmādhavaśca kāma iti tayorbahalalokasaḍkulepi pathi rāgasāgaronyonyaṃ vadha iti bhāvaḥ yadvā kāmonaṅgattayāpratyakṣo vṛddhaśca atrotprekṣā viśiṣṭasyaiva sākṣātpratyakṣaṃ navaṃ kāmamivetyarthaḥ tāmyatītyanenodvega uktaḥ yadāha bharataḥ cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddā hābhinayena ca ślathāṅgopāgaceṣṭābhisdvegābhinayo bhavet  iti  rathyāpratolī viśikhā  ityamaraḥ vātāyanaṃ gavākṣotha iti ca sākṣātpratyakṣatulyayoriti dharaṇiḥ avalokitā bāḍhamatitarāmanuraktā mālatītyarthaḥ vinodaḥ krīḍā harṣo vā praticchandakaṃ prati jado tāe tāe uvvea udvega viṇoaṇaṃ abhi ṇikkhittaṃ nikṣiptam mālatīmādhave kāma vicintya suvihitaṃ lavaṅgikayā yato mādhavānucaraḥ kalahaṃsakastāṃ vihāradāsīṃ mandārikāṃ kāmayate tadanena tīrthene ghaṭeta tatpraticchandakamupoddhātāya mādhavāntikamupeyādityabhiprāyaḥ ava  mādhavopi kautūhalamutpādya mayā pravṛttamadanamahotsarvaṃ makarandodyānamadya prabhātenupreṣitaḥ tatra kila mālatī gamiṣyati tatonyonyadarśanaṃ bhavatviti māhavo vi kodūhalaṃ uppādia mae pauttamaaṇamahūsavaṃ maarandujjāṇaṃ ajja pabhāde aṇuppesido tattha kila māladī gamissadi tado aṇṇodaṃsaṇaṃ hodu tti kāma  sādhu vatse sādhu anena matpriyābhiyogena smārayasi me pūrvaśiṣyāṃ saudāminīm ava   bhagavati sā saudāminyadhunā samāsāditāścaryamantrasiddhiprabhāvā śrīparvate kāpālikataṃ dhārayati bhaavadi sā sodāmiṇī ahuṇā samāsādidaaccariamantasiddhippahāvā sirīpavvade kāvāliavvadaṃ dhāredi kāma kutaḥ punariyaṃ vārtā ava  astyatra nagaryo mahāśmaśānapradeśe karālā nāma cāmuṇḍā asthi ettha ṇaarīe mahāmasāṇappadese karālo ṇāma cāmuṇḍā rūpakam tāvatpadena mandārikāhastanidhānasya prakṛtakāryopakramaḥ sūcitaḥ ata eva kāmandakyā suvihitamityuktam kāmandakī vihāraḥ saugatapravrājikānāmālayaḥ tatra vyāvṛtā dāsī vihāradāsī etena prakaraṇabāhyatvamuktam yadāha daṇḍī  śakāra kuhinī dāsī dharmaśāstrabahiṣkṛtāḥ viṭaceṣṭādayo nityaṃ bāhyāḥ prakaraṇe matāḥ tīrthena dvārā upāyena vā  tīrthamupāyadvāramantriṣu  iti viśvaḥ upoddhātena prasaṅgena abhi prāyastāvaditi vādinyāstaveti śeṣaḥ avalokitā  kautukaṃ tu kutūhalam  ityamaraḥmadanamahotsavena vasantakālaḥ sūcitaḥ tasya ca vaivāhikatvam yadāhaśarasagrāmaviṣaye vivāhe jyeṣṭamādhavau iti kila prasiddhau iti hetau anupreṣaṇe tatra kiletyāderhetutvam anyonyadarśanenobhayānurāge vivāhanirvāhaḥ priye prītiviṣaye kāryoṃbhiyoga āsaṅgaḥ atra kapālavrataṃ mahāvratam kṛta ityādinā śmaśānāṅkasūcanam haṃso nāma tīrthena tatḥ ghaṭate upoddhā tena ṭī  maaṇajjāṇaṃ madano  karālīkāma nāṃ pravādaḥ prathamoṅkaḥ asti yo kila vividhajīvopahārapriyeti sāhasikā  tatra khalu śrīparvatādāgatasya rātrivihāriṇo nātidūrāraṇya vāsinaḥ sādhakasya muṇḍadhāriṇoghoraghaṇṭanāmadheyasyāntevāsinī mahāprabhāvā kapālakuṇḍalā nāmānusandhyaṃ samāgacchati tata iyaṃ pravṛttiḥ tahiṃ kkhu sirīpavvadādo āadassa rattivihāriṇo ṇādidairāraṇṇavāsiṇo sāhaassa muṇḍariṇo aghoraghaṇṭaṇāmaheassa andevāsiṇī mahāppahāvā kavālakuṇḍalā ṇāma aṇusaṃjjhaṃ samācchadi  tado iaṃ pauttī kāma  sarve saudāminyāṃ sambhāvyate ava  alaṃ tāvadetena bhagavati sopi sahacaro mādhavasya bālamitraṃ makarando nandanasya bhaginīṃ madayantikāṃ yadi samudvahati tadapi mādhavasya dvitīyaṃ priyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati alaṃ dāva ediṇā bhaavadi so vi sahaaro māhavassa bālamittaṃ maarando ṇandaṇassa vahiṇiṃ madaantiaṃ jai samuvvahadi taṃ vi māhavassa dudīaṃ piaṃ kidaṃ hodi  niyuktaiva tatra mayā tatpriyasakhī buddharakṣitā ava  su vihitaṃ bhagavatyā suvihidaṃ bhaavadīe kāma vicintya taduttiṣṭha mādhavapravṛttimupalabhya mālatīkāma  meva paśyāvaḥ kāmandakī kila prasiddhau vividhā nānārūpā jīvā mānuṣādaya upahārā balayaḥ priyā yasyāḥ sā anena mālatyupahāraḥ sūcitaḥ ātmanirapekṣaṃ karma sāhasaṃ tena vartante te sāhasikāḥ pravādaḥ prasiddhiḥ iha priyetyasyānantaramiti padaṃ deyamanyathā pūrvāparānanvayāt tathā ca priyetyanenākāreṇa sāhasikānāṃ pravāda ityarthaḥ ata eva vākyārthakarmādāviteradhyāhāraḥ avalokitā iha khalu prasiddhau tasyāścāmuṇḍāyā nātidūreṇātyāsanne vastuṃ śīlaṃ yasya tasya etena devakulasya lokasaṅkulatayā kiṃcidviprakṛṣṭaṃ sādhakasaṃsthānamuktam sādhakasya yoginaḥ muṇḍadhāriṇaḥ kāpālikasya aghoraghaṇṭeti kāpālikāstu ghaṇṭāntanāmānaḥ samudāhṛtāḥ  iti bharataḥ aghorovimṛṣyakārīti nāmavyutpattiḥ anusandhyaṃ sandhyāyām pravṛttirvārtā sarvamaghoraghaṇṭanāśanamādhavarakṣaṇādikam atraitena kāpālikādeḥ kathanenālaṃ niṣphalamadhunānupayogāt avalokitā bālamiti bhāvapradhānam tena bālyānmitramityarthaḥ samuhati vivahati kāmandakī buddharakṣitetyanena bhikṣukītvaṃ sūcitam ata eva dautye niyuktā kāmandakī uttiṣṭhalyatrordhvakarmatvānna taṅ sā sādhakānāṃ ido nādidūramasāṇabā muṇḍamālādhā mahānubhāvā are samā sarve hi pāssa pārśva  mālatīmādhave ubhe uttiṣṭhataḥ kāma  vicintya atyudāraprakṛtirmālatī tannipuṇaṃ nisaṣṭārthadūtīkalpaḥ sūtrayitavyaiḥ sarvathā śarajjotsnā kāntaṃ kumudamiva taṃ nandayatu sā sujātaṃ kalyāṇī bhavatu kṛtakṛtyaḥ sa ca yuvā varīyānanyonyapraguṇaguṇanirmāṇanipuṇo vidhāturvyāpāraḥ phalatu ca manojñaśca bhavatu iti niṣkrānte viṣkambhakaḥ tataḥ praviśati gṛhītacitraphalakopakaraṇaḥ kalahaṃsaḥ kalahaṃsa  kutredānīṃ tulita makaradhvajāvaleparūpavibhramāvakṣiptamālatīhṛdayamāhātmyaṃ nāthamādhavaṃ prekṣiṣye parikramya pariśrāntosmi kāmandakī atyudāttā gabhīga pratipannārthāsaṃvādinī prakṛtiryasyāḥ sā tathā nisṛṣṭā rtheti nāyikāyā nāyakasya vā manorathaṃ jñātvā svamatyā kārya sādhayati sā nisṛṣṭārthā dūtī tasyāḥ kalpo vyāpāraḥ prastāvanīya ityarthaḥ dūtī ca vividhā yadāha  nisṛṣṭārthā mitārthā ca tathā śāsanahārikā sāmarthyotpāditāhīnā dūtī tu vividhā matā  iti śaradityādi sā mālatī taṃ mādhavaṃ nandayatu prīṇātu yathā śaraccandrikā kumudaṃ nandayati tathā candrikākumudayornityaṃ prītistathā tayorayastviti bhāvaḥ kīdṛśam kāntaṃ ramyam sujātaṃ śobhanajanmānam śobhanatā ca guṇavatvena yadvā kāntamanyastrībhogacihnaśūnyam yadāha bharataḥ  anyastrībhogasambhūtaṃ cihnaṃ yasya na vidyate dehe vāpyadhare vāpi sa kānta iti kīrtitaḥ  sā kīdṛśī kalyāṇī niravayā sa ca yuvā kalyāṇī vivāhakalyāṇayogī saṃstāṃ prāpya kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṛtārtho bhavatu yuvetyanena kanyāyāṃ madanamadoddīpakatāyogitvamuktam evaṃ sati vidhātuḥ prayatnaḥ saphalo bhavatu manoharaśca bhūpanandanāvirodhena sarvāvarjako stvityarthaḥ kīdṛśaḥ anyonyaṃ kāminoḥ praguṇā anurūpā ye guṇāsteṣāṃ nirmāṇe kuśalota eva varīyānśreṣṭho garīyāngururkhā yadvā anyonyaṃ praguṇā utkṛṣṭā ye guṇāsteṣāṃ nirmāṇe kuśalaḥ niṣkānte kāmandakyavalokite viṣkambhaka iti kutopi svecchayā prāptaḥ sambandhenobhayorapi viṣkambhakaḥ sa vijñeyo yastu kāvyārthasūcakaḥ viṣkambhastu dvidhā soyaṃ śuddha saṅkīrṇa eva ca śuddho madhyamapātreṇa saṅkīrṇo madhyamādhamaiḥ  iti bharataḥ upakaraṇamupaḍhaukanam kalahaṃsaḥ ityu mālatī nāma tantrayitavyaḥ garīyān miavi citropakaraṇaḥ gṛhītacitraphalakaḥ citraphalakahastaḥprathamoṅkaḥ yāvadasminnudyāne muhūrtaṃ viśramya makarandanandanaṃ nāthamādhavaṃ prekṣiṣye kahiṃ dāṇiṃ tulidamaaraddhaivalearūvavivbhamāvakkhittamāladīhiaamāhapaṃ ṇāhamāhavaṃ pekkhissaṃ parissanto hmi jāva imariṃsa ujjā muhuttaṃ vissamia maarandaṇandaṇaṃ ṇauhamāhavaṃ pekkhissaṃ iti praviśyopaviśati tataḥ praviśati makarandaḥ makarandaḥ kathitamavalokitayā madanodyānaṃ gato mādhava iti bhavatu tatraiva gacchāmi parikramyāvalokya ca diṣṭacāyaṃ vayasya ita evābhivartate nirūpya asya tu gamanamalasaṃ śūnyā dṛṣṭiḥ śarīramasauṣṭhavaṃ śvasitamadhikaṃ kiṃ nvaitatsyātkimarnyaditotha vā bhramati bhuvane kandarpājñā vikāri ca yauvanaṃ lalitamadhurāste te bhāvāḥ kṣipanti ca dhīratām atra tulito makaradhvajasya kāmasyāvalepo garvo yena rūpavibhrameṇa saundaryavilāsena tenāvakṣiptaṃ tiraskṛtaṃ mālatīhṛdayasya māhātmyaṃ gāmbhīrya yena tam avalepaḥ smṛto garvaḥ  iti śāśvataḥ makarandasya nandanaṃ harṣakam kalahaṃso rājahaṃsaḥ sa ca śaradi virājamānopi yoginīprabhāvādvasante milita iti nāmāmiprāyaḥ makarandaḥ diṣṭayetyavyayaṃ harṣe mādhavasya vasantasya makarandaḥ puṣparasaḥ sahacaro yujyata eva ita evātraiva iha śṛṅgāro dvividhaḥ yadāha bharataḥ sambhogo vipralambhava śṛṅgāro dvividho mataḥ  sambhogopi vipralambhapūrvaka eva svadate yadāha  na vinā vipralambhena sambhogaḥ puṣṭimarhati kaṣāyite hi vastrādau bhuyārāgobhijāyate sa ca daśārambhaḥ yadāha bharataḥ  aprāptaratibhogasya navastrīrāgajanmanaḥ daśa sthānāni kāmasya kāmamantarvisarpataḥ abhilāṣotra prathame dvitīye cintanaṃ tathā anusmṛtistṛtīye ca caturthe guṇakīrtanam udvegaḥ pañcame jñeyo vilāpaḥ ṣaṣṭa ucyate unmādaḥ saptame prokto bhavedvayā dhistathāṣṭame navame jaḍatā proktā daśame maraṇaṃ bhavet iti tadihānusmṛtyavastho mādhavo makarandena kathyate   gamanamiti asya gamanamalasaṃ mandaṃ na tu śarīram hastāderākuñcanaprasāraṇāt antarāntarā vilambasyātyantāsaktivaśājjāyamānatvācca idamanusmṛticihnam yadāha   muhurmuhurniḥśvasitairadhomukhavicintanaiḥ pradveṣādanyakāryāṇāṃ kathitānusmṛtiryathā  tathā yato māmapi na paśyati tatontaḥkaraṇaṃ kāpi lagnam tathā ca cintāsantatiparatayā dhyānāvadhānena śūnyā bāhyārthāgrāhiṇī dṛṣṭirasya yadāha  śūnyā dṛṣṭiḥ smṛtā cintāsaṃmohapraṇayā raddharūāvaleavi iha sahaaraṃ sahacara haṃ kiṃ nyadato naitemālatīmādhave tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭo mātravaḥ mādhavaḥ  svagatam tāmindusundara mukhīṃ suciraṃ vibhāvya cetaḥ kathaṃ kathamapi vyapavartate me lajjāṃ vijitya vinayaṃ vinivārya dhairyamunmathya mantharavivekamakāṇḍa eva diṣu  śūnyadṛṣṭilakṣaṇamapyāha   niścalā samatārā ca dhyānādbrāhmamagṛhatī tathā samapuṭopetā śūnyā dṛṣṭirudāhṛtā  tathā manastāpavato glāniḥ sā tathā manastāpavato glāniḥ sā ca kṣīṇakapolatādinonnīyate ata uktaṃ śarīramasauṣṭavaṃ vikalam iṣṭajanālābhabhāvanārthamāha śvasitamadhikam etaki nu syāt etadalasagamanatvādikaṃ rogajaṃ kāmakṛtaṃ veti vitarka ityarthaḥ rogaliṅgābhāvādanaṅgaliṅgasaṅgāñca niścayamāha  kimanyaditi athavā pakṣāntare itaḥ kāmātkimanyat nānyadityarthaḥ kiṃśabdo niṣedhe atra pāṃśukrīḍanātprabhṛtyanubhūtamādhavaśarīre tattadvikāradarśanāttarkavidyāvido makarandasya paricchedo yujyata eveti niścayaliṅgamāha   bhuvane kaṃdarpājñā bhramati sarva janamāskandati vika śīlamasyeti vikāri pūrvadaśātyāgena daśāntarayogo vikārastadyogi yauvanam ayaṃ tu yuvetyarthaḥ atra bhramatipadenānavachinnakriyatā tadvārā sarvakālatā bhuvanapadena sarvadeśatā ājñāpadena yuktijijñāsāṃ vinā svīkāraḥ vikāripadena mādhavāṅgīkāritā ca dhvanitā lalitāḥ sundarā madhurāḥ paribhāvyamānāste te prasiddhā bhāvā ramaṇīvadanavibhramādayā dhīratāṃ dhairya kṣipantyapanayanti tadanena kāmakṛtametadunnīyata iti bhāvaḥ prakṛtimadhurāḥ  ityapi pāṭhaḥ tatra prakṛtyā svabhāvata eva madhurā manoharāḥ mādhavapraveśa iha dvipadikayā yadāha    śokavibhramayukte tu vyādhicintāsamāśrite śrutavārtādivairūpye yojyā dvipadakā budhaiḥ  iti svagatamiti yattu śrāvyaṃ na sarvasya svagataṃ tadihocyate  iti bharataḥ anusmṛtimāha   tāmityādi tāṃ nāyikāmaciramadhunaiva vicintya mama cetaḥ kartṛ kathaṃ kathamapi mahatā kaṣṭena vyapavartate vyāvartate nāgacchati vā tasyāṃ lagnaṃ tāmeva dhāvatītyarthaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā bālatvena kulīnatvena ca yā lajjā tāmakāṇḍa evāprastāva eva vijitya rabhasakāla eva hiṃ lajjādyabhāvaprastāva iti bhāvaḥ vinayaṃ manomalakṣālanopadeśaṃ dūrīkṛtya mahānāyakatayā sāhajikaṃ dhīratvamunmūlya kīdṛśam mantharo mando viveka itikartavyatā yatra tat kriyāviśeṣaṇaṃ vā kīdṛśīm indoścandrātsundaraṃ mukhaṃ yasyāstām vaiyadhikaraṇyepi gamakatvātsamāsaḥ iha tāmityanusmṛtiḥ indusundareti guṇakīrtanam vi nirdiṣṭarūpaḥ praviśati mādhavaḥāścaryam prathamoṅkaḥ yadvismayastimitamastamitānyabhāvamānandamandamamṛtaplavanādivāṃbhūt tatsannidhau tadadhunā hṛdayaṃ madīyamaṅgāracumbitamiva vyathamānamāste makarandaḥ  upasṛtya sakhe mādhava ita itaḥ mādhavaḥ  parikramya kathaṃ priyavayasyo mama makarandaḥ makarandaḥ  sakhe mādhava lalāṭaṃtapastapati tapanastadasminnudyāne muhūrtamupaviśāvaḥ mādhavaḥ  yardebhirucitaṃ vayasyāya ubhau parikrāmataḥ kalahaṃsaḥ  dṛṣṭvā kathaṃ makarandasahacara idameva bālatrakulodyānamalaṃkaroti nāthamādhavaḥ taddarśayāmyasya madanavedanākhidyamānamālatīlocanasukhāvahamātmanaḥ praticchandakam athavā muhūrtaṃ viśrāmasaukhyaṃ bhāvyeti cakṣuḥprītiḥ kathamapītyudvegaḥ lajjāṃ vijityetyunmādaḥ mantharaviveka miti jaḍatetyanekāvasthoktā yadityādi tatsaṃnidhau yanmadīyaṃ hṛdayaṃ vismayenādbhutarasena stimitaṃ niścalam etena stambha uktaḥ ata evāstamito nāśaṃ prāpitonyo bhāvo vismayātirikto dharmo yatra tat anena jaḍatoktā yadāha  iṣṭaṃ vāniṣṭaṃ vā sukhaduḥkhe vā na vetti yo mohāt tūṣṇīkaḥ paravaśagaḥ sa bhavati jaḍasaṃjñakaḥ puruṣaḥ  ānandena nirantarasukhena mandaṃ mantharaṃ cābhūt amṛtaplavanādiva sudhāsekādiva atha ca yogābhyāsena kuṇḍalinyācaraṇenāmṛtasekā divetyarthaḥ tatrāpi paramānandasaṃdoho bhavatyeva etenādbhutanāyikādarśanajātabhāvabharamantharatā darśitā taddhṛdayamadhunā tadviyogeṅgāracumbitamivāmārāvasṛṣṭamiva vyathamānaṃ pīḍāyuktamāsta ityāścaryam na ca priyā sukhaṃ tadviyoge duḥkhamiti dṛṣṭacarameva tatkathamāścaryamiti vācyam ananubhūtarasasya tasya śiśutvena kimidaṃ yadakāṇḍa eva vyatheti tatsaṃbhavāt makarandaḥ ita itaḥ ihāgacchetyarthaḥ ādyāditvāttasiḥ etena mādhavasya bāhyāgrahānmitrādarśanaṃ sūcitam makarandaḥ lalāṭaṃ tapati lalāṭaṃtapaḥ asūryalalāṭayo  iti khaśpratyayaḥ khittvānmum mādhavīyamanmathonmādamapahnotukāmasyedaṃ vacanam mādhavaḥ vayasyāyeti ruyarthānāṃ prīyamāṇaḥ iti saṃpradānatā kalahaṃsaḥ atra makarandena puṣparasena sahacaro mādhavo vasanto bālabakulamalaṃkarotīti dhvanirapyunmiṣati muhūrta cetyatra susthite citte vaktuṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ sāndra āsīt ghamāṃśuḥ iyaṃ ca te śarīrāvasthā ityadhikaṃ kvacit  yathā priyavayasyāya rocate ityubhāvupaviśataḥ mālatīmādhave tāvadanubhavatu kadhaṃ maarandasahaaro idaṃ jjevtra bālavaulujjāṇaṃ alaṃkarodi ṇāhamāhavo tā daṃsemi se maaṇaveaṇākkhijjamāṇamāladīloaṇasuhāvaha attaṇo paḍicchandaaṃ ahavā muṃhuttaṃ visāmasokkhaṃ dāva aṇuhodu maka  tadasyaiva tāvaducchrasitakusumakesarakaṣāyaśītalāmodavāsi todyānasya kāñcanārapādapasyādhastādupaviśāvaḥ ubhau tathā kurutaḥ maka  vayasya mādhava adya kila sakalanagarāṅganājana pravartimahotsavābhirāmakāmadevodyānayātrāpratinivṛttamanyādṛśaṃ bhavantamavadhārayāmi api nāma manāgavatīrṇosi ratiramaṇabāṇagocaram maka paśya mādhava salajjamadhomukhastiṣṭhati vihasya tatkimavanatamugdhamukhapuṇḍarīkaḥ sthitosi anyeṣu jantuṣu rajastamasāvṛteṣu viśvasya dhātari samaḥ parameśvare ca soyaṃ prasiddhavibhavaḥ khaluṃ cittajanmā mā lajjayā tava kathaṃcidapahnutirbhūt makarandaḥ utphullapuṣpāṇāṃ ye kesarāḥ kiñjalkāstaiḥ kaṣāyo lohitaḥ śītalaśca ya āmodastena vāsitaṃ sugandhīkṛtamudyānaṃ yena tasya  kaṣāyaḥ surabhau lohitenyavat  iti medinīkaraḥ kaṣāyādisambandhena saurabhasyātigabhīratoktā āmudyatenenetyāmoda iti kapāyādisampade kāñcanāretyuktam pravartitaḥ kṛtaḥ abhirāmeti yātrānvayi iha makarandavacanena narmarūpaḥ pratimukhasandhiraktaḥ yadāha  śṛṅgārārtha trapākāri vākyaṃ goṣṭīṣu narma tat  iti apiḥ samuccaye nāma sambhāvanāyām idaṃ sambhāvyetāpītyarthaḥ manāgalpam ratiramaṇaḥ kāmaḥ makarandaḥ mugdhaṃ kiṃkartavyatāśūnyam puṇḍarīkaṃ sitapadmam virahadhūsaratvena mukhasya puṇḍarīkasāmyam tasya lajjayākathanamāśaṅkayāha  anyeṣvityādi mādhava tavāpahnutirlajjayā kathaṃcidapi mā bhūt lajjayāpahnavaṃ mā kṛthāḥ evamapratīkāraḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ khalu yataḥ soyaṃ cittajanmā kāmaḥ prakhyātapauruṣaḥ cittonmāthaviṣaya iti bhāvaḥ kīdṛśaḥ viśvasya dhātari jagattraṣṭari etannāsti kvacit kāñcanapāda adyaiva tāvat madano dṛśamiva gocaratāma avanamra ca yaḥ bahiḥ api kila prathamoṅkaḥ mādhava  vayasya kiṃ na kathayāmi śrayatām gatohamavalokitājanitakautukaḥ kāmadevāyatanam tatra cetastataḥ parikramyāvalokya ca pariśramādullasitamadirāmoda madhuraparimalākṛṣṭa sakalāmeladalipaṭalasaṃkulākulitamukulāvalīmanoharābharaṇaramaṇīyasyāṅkanabhuvo bālabakulasyālavāla parisare sthitaḥ tasya ca yadṛcchayā nirantairanipatitāni vikasitāni kusumanyādāya vidagdharacanāmanoharāṃ strajamābhinirmātumārabdhavānasmi anantaraṃ ca saṃcāriṇīva devasya markeraketanasya jagadvijayavaijayantikā nirgatya garbhabhavanādujjvalavidagdhamugdhanepathyaviracanāvibhāvitakumārībhāvā mahānubhāvaprakṛtiratyudāraparijanā kāpi tata evāgatavatī harenyeṣu jantuṣu mānuṣādiṣu ca rajastamoguṇapradhāneṣu samastulyavyāpāraḥ yadvā anyeṣu mānuṣādiṣu rajastamasāvṛteṣu ca tiryagyoniṣu viśvasya dhātari brahmāṇa para meśvare hare ca sama iti bhinnameva yojyam ato lajjāṃ tyaktvā kathayeti bhāvaḥ mādhavaḥ pariśramātsthita ityanvayaḥ pariśramātsthitohaṃ na tu sākāsatvāditi bhāvaḥ madirāmodavanmanoharo yaḥ parimalaḥ śubhagandhaḥ syācchubhagandhe parimalaḥ iti viśvaḥ milanmilitam saṃkulena vyāptākulitā yā bakulamukulāvalī vikāsābhimukhakalikārājiḥ saiva manoharamābharaṇaṃ tena ramaṇīyasya yadvā madirāmodena madhura iti samāsaḥ tena madirāmodasya bakulapuṣpodgamaṃ prati dohadatvamāha aṅganabhuvoṅganasthasya anena nikaṭavartinaḥ sekādinā manojñatā darśitā ihāṅganapadenuvidhāyakābhāvāṇṇatvaśrutirayuktā pṛṣodarāditvāṇṇatvamityapi vacomūlakameva pratyuta  aṅganaṃ prāṅgaṇe jāle kāminyāmaṅganā matā  iti viśvādikoṣāttavargapañcamopāttamaṅganaṃ kevalamiti śabdaprakāśācca nāntatva mevetyavadheyam ālavālaṃ khala iti khyātam syādālavālamāvālamambhasāṃ yatra dhāraṇam ityamaraḥ vidagdheti mālānirmāṇa kāmaśāstravaidagdhyadyotanāya uktaṃ ca mālāprathanavikalpā ityādineti bhāvaḥ atisukumāratayā kāminormanoharatayā sugandhitayā sundaratayā cānyapuṣpāṇi tyaktvā bakulapuṣpairmālāgrathanaṃsiha ata eva damayantīsvayaṃvarādāvapi bakulamālāsamamadhūkamālāparigrahaḥ saṃcāriṇī gamanaśīlā makaraketoḥ kāmasya vaijayantikā patākā garbhabhavanānmadhyāvāsādujjvalayā nirmalayāgrāmyayā ca śiśuprasādhanaviracanayonnītaḥ kumārībhāvaḥ kumārītvaṃ yasyāḥ kumārītvenāvaguṇṭhanapaṭādyabhāvāttadunnayanamiti bhāvaḥ mahānubhāvaprekatiratiprabhāvasvabhāvā atyudāro mahāndakṣiṇo vā udāro mahati dakṣiṇe kautūhalaḥ bakulamu nirantaravika vikasitanira ādāyādāya kusu vidagdhaviracanayā srajaṃ makaraketoḥ mugdhabāla mālatīmādhave sā rāmaṇīyakanidheradhidevatā vā saundaryasārasamudāyaniketanaṃ vā tasyāḥ sakhe niyatamindusuṃdhāmṛṇālajyotsnādi kāraṇamabhūnmadanañca vedhāḥ sā praṇayinībhiranucarībhiravirailakusuma saṃcayāvacayalīlādo haidinībhirabhyarthyamānā tameva baiṃkulapādapoddeśamāgatavatī tasyāñca kasminnapi mahābhāgadheyajanmani bahudivasopacīyamānamiva manmathavyathāvikāramurpalakṣitavānāsma yatosyāḥ atha iti śāśvataḥ parijanadākṣiṇyaṃ sānnidhyānayanena jñeyam tata eva tatraiva tadruṇakīrtanamāha  setyādi sā strī rāmaṇīyakasya manoharatāyā nidherādhārasyādhidevatādhiṣṭhātrī devatā yadvā rāmaṇīyakameva nidhistasyādhiṣṭhātrī rakṣikā devatā saundaryasārasamudāyasya kāntiniryāsapūrasya niketanaṃ gṛhaṃ vā niketanasyājahalliṅgatayā sāmānādhikaraṇyam manoharatvaṃ kāntimattvaṃ ca tatraiva dṛṣṭamiti bhāvaḥ vā samuccaye yadvā vā vikalpe tatra nirṇetuṃ na śakyata iti vikalpārthaḥ yadvā vevārthe rāmaṇīyakanidherdevatevetyarthaḥ vā syādvikalpopamayorivārthepi samucaye iti viśvaḥ yadvā rāmaṇīyakaṃ rūpādisampattistannidheradhidevatā anena śobhoktā yadāha  rūpayauvanalāvaṇyairupabhogopabṛṃhitaiḥ alaṅkaraṇamaṅgānāṃ śobheti parikīrtitā  saundaryetyādinā kāntiruktā yadāha  śobhaiva kusumāstreṇa pūritā kāntirucyate  atonayorbhedaḥ atyantavilakṣaṇāṃ tāmālokyotprekṣate niyataṃ nūnaṃ tasyāḥ kāraṇaṃ samavāyikāraṇamindusudhāmṛṇālajyotsnādikamabhūt candro mukhasya sudhādharasya mṛṇālaṃ bhujayoḥ jyotsnā lāvaṇyādīnāmiti bhāvaḥ ādipadena padma pādayoḥ kisalayau caraṇayoriti grāhyam sarvopamādravyaghaṭiteyamiti bhāvaḥ evaṃ madana evāsyā vedhāḥ sraṣṭābhūt cakārovadhāraṇe vedajaḍasya purāṇasya brahmaṇo nātra nirmāṇakauśalamiti bhāvaḥ atra kāmasya straṣṭṛtvenāśrutatvātkathamiti na deśyam asyā mohanītvena mohanapaṭukāmajanyatvotprekṣaṇāt adṛṣṭacaratvasyotprekṣāyāmanukūlatvāt asadāropaṇasyātprekṣātvāt niyatapadamutprekṣāvyañjakam nūnamityevamādibhiḥ iti vacanāt praṇayinī snigdhā anucarī dāsī sañcayaḥ samūhaḥ avacayastroṭanam dohadobhilāṣaḥ saharṣamāha  tameveti svodeśamāha  kasminnapīti bhāgadheyaṃ bhāgyam ityamaraḥ ihānumānarūpo garbhasandhiṃḥ kasmiṃścidityanenoktaḥ yadāha vyāpyena vyāpakajñānamanumānamudīritam iti vikāracihnamāha kalā anavarata kutūhalinībhiḥ abhilāṣiṇībhiḥ bālabakula kasmiṃ paścidapi upalabdhavāprathamoṅkaḥ parimṛditamṛṇālīmlānamaṅgaṃ pravṛttiḥ kathamapi parivāra prārthanābhiḥ kriyāsu kalayati ca himāṃśorniṣkaṅkasya lakṣmīmabhinavakaridantacchedapāṇḍuḥ kapolaḥ sā punarmama prathamadarśanātprabhṛtyamṛtavartiriva cakṣuṣorniratiśayamānandamutpādayantyayaskāntamaṇiśalākeva lohadhātumantaḥkaraṇamārkeṣṭavatī sarvathā kiṃ bahunā santāpasantatimahāvyasanāya tasyāmāsaktametadanapekṣitahetu cetaḥ prāyaḥ śubhaṃ ca vidhātyaśubhaṃ ca jantoḥ sarvakaṣā bhagavatī bhavitavyataiva parimṛditota yathāsyā aṅgaṃ parimṛditā mardanaviṣayīkṛtā yā mṛṇālī bisalatā tadvanmlānam kriyāsu tāmbūlabhakṣaṇādiṣu parijanayācanābhirasyāḥ kathamapi pravṛttiḥ iha mṛṇālīpadena tanutā mlānyā nidrācchedaḥ kathamapītyādinā viṣayanivṛttiḥ kathitā tanutvamlānatvamāndyaiglaniruktā yadāha  glānau tanutvavaivarṇyamandatādinidarśanam  nanu tanutvādinā vyabhicāriṇā kathaṃ kāmavikāronnayanamata āha  kalayatīti tasyāḥ kapālpre himāṃśoḥ śobhāṃ kalayati anena pāṇḍutā darśitā kīdṛśaḥ nūtanadāntidantakhaṇḍagauraḥ chidyata iti cchedaḥ khaṇḍaḥ ihābhinavapadena sapulakatvaṃ dhvanitam tathā ca kapolapāṇḍutvasapulakatvādinā kāmavikāravyāptena tadunnayanamiti bhāvaḥ virahe pāṇḍutāpi yadāha  aṅgasyā sauṣṭhavaṃ tāpaḥ pāṇḍutā kṛśatā ratiḥ  vartineṃtrāñjanalekhā ayaskānto lohākarṣako maṇiḥ lohadhāturloharūpaṃ dravyam antaḥkaraṇaṃ manaḥ mamāntaḥkaraṇaṃ kṛṣṭavatītyarthaḥ kiṃ bahunetyanena sakhedaniḥśvāsasūcanam santā petyādi mamaitaccetastasyāṃ viṣaya āsaktaṃ samantāllammamastītyarthaḥ santāpaparaṃparaiva mahāvyasanaṃ tadartham tādarthye caturthī santatipadena mālatīlābhamantareṇa yāvajjīvamavicchedastadalābhe prāṇahāniścoktā kīdṛśam anapekṣitanimittam etena viṣayālābhepyasya svābhāvikī prītiruktā yadāha   abhyāsādabhimānāñca tathā saṃpratyayādapi viṣayebhyaśca tattvajñā viduḥ prītiṃ caturvidhām  anena nijamucchṛṅkhalatvamapi nirastam ata evāhaprāya iti bāhulyena bhagavatī bhavitavyatāvaśyaṃbhāvi prātanakarma jīvānāṃ śubhamaśubhaṃ ca vidadhāti ata eva sarvekaṣā sarvaharā tathā ca mamāvaśyakaṃ duḥkhaṃ tvaṃ tu yathocitaṃ kuryā iti bhāvaḥ āsaktetyāḍyūrvāt ṣac samavāye taḥ A kāntaḥ darśanakṣaṇāt nayanayoḥ śayānanda nirantaramā upasaṃhṛtavatī mālatīmādhave makarandaḥ  vayasya mādhava snehaśca nimittasavyapekṣaśceti vipratiṣiddhametat paśya vyatiṣajati padārthānāntaraḥ kopi heturna khalu bahirupādhīnprītayaḥ saṃśrayante vikasati hi pataṅgasyodaye puṇḍarīkaṃ dravati ca himaraśmāṃvudgate candrakāntaḥ tatastataḥ mādhavaḥ  tataśca tatra sabhrūvilāsamatha soyamitarayitvā sapratyabhijñamiva māmavalokya tasyāḥ anyonyabhāvacatureṇa sakhījanena muktāstadā smitasudhāmadhurāḥ kaṭākṣāḥ atra sarvakaṣeti khacpratyaye khitvāmum makarandaḥ mādhavoktaprīteranimittakatvamupapādayati  sneha iti nimittamiha dvayaṃ bāhyamābhyantaraṃ ca tadiha bāhyahetvapekṣaḥ snehosthira eva nimittanivṛttau tannivṛtterāvaśyakatvāt ata āntaranimittāpekṣaiva snehasyeti bhāvaḥ vipratiṣiddhaṃ viruddham bāhyanimittāpekṣayā virodha iti bhāvaḥ svokte yuktimāha  vyatiṣajatītyādi āntaro hetuḥ kopyanirvacanīyaḥ padārthānnaranārīprabhṛtīnvyatiṣajati viśeṣato melayati yataḥ prītayo bahirupādhīnbāhyahetūnsaundaryādīnna saṃśrayante prakarṣeṇāvalambante kopītyanena janmāntarānubhavajanitasaṃskāratādhvaniḥ na khalvityanena dṛṣṭaśrutānumita sakalaihikopādhiniṣedhāttathāvasāyaḥ ata eva viśeṣaprakarṣadyotakābhyāmupasargābhyāmāsasya jīvitāvadhitvamuktam uktaṃ draḍhayati  yataḥ pataṅgasya sūryasyodaye puṇḍarīkaṃ vikasati candra udgata udite sati candrakānto dravati kṣarati ca tathā ca tīkṣṇakarodaye komalakamaladalavikāsādamṛtakarodaye pāṣāṇadāraṇācca sahajasiddha eva hetuḥ iha kiṃ bāhyaṃ kāraṇaṃ dṛśyate tadvatprakṛtepi svābhāvika eva sneha iti bhāvaḥ puṇḍarīkapadamiha padmamātraparam arthāntaranyāsoyam tatastata iti kathopakramarītiḥ mādhavaḥ tatra sthāne sabhrūvilāsamityādi atha tasyāḥ sakhījanena tadā soyamityuktvā sapratyabhijñamiva pūrvadṛṣṭamiva māmavalokya sabhrūvilāsaṃ sabhrūbhaṅgaṃ yathā tathā kaṭākṣāḥ kṣiptāḥ etena kaṭākṣāṇāṃ pūrvadṛṣṭapratyabhijñākārārpaṇatvamuktam kīdṛśena anyonyāśayavijñena anena nāyikāvyutpattyatiśaya uktaḥ kīdṛśāḥ smitamīṣaddhasitamevāmṛtaṃ tena manojñāḥ  īṣatpraphullitairgaṇḍaiḥ vudyate itīṣa nāma syameva prathamoṅkaḥ makarandaḥ  svagatam kathaṃ pratyabhijñāpi nāma  mādhavaḥ  atha tā salīlamuttālakarakamalatālikātaralavalayāvalīkamutrastamatta kalahaṃsavibhramābhirāmacaraṇa saṃcaraṇajhaṇajhaṇīyamānama mañjīrarasitānuviddhamekhalākalāpakalakiṅkiṇīraṇatkāramukharaṃ parivṛtya  bhartṛdārike diṣṭyā vairdhāmahe yadatraiva kopi kasyāpi tiṣṭhati  iti māmagulī dalavilāsenākhyatavatyaḥ makarandaḥ  svagatam hanta mahataḥ prāganurāgasyodbhedaḥ kaṭākṣaiḥ sauṣṭhavānvitaiḥ adṛṣṭadantakusumairuttamānāṃ smitaṃ matam  iti bharataḥ svasyācaratvena saṃbhāvanāyāmihevaśabdaḥ avalokyeti lalitā dṛṣṭiriyam yadāha  madhurākuñcitārā ca samrakṣepā ca sasmitā samanmathavikārā ca dṛṣṭiḥ sā lalitā matā iha tu harṣādiyamucitā yadāha   vṛtau harṣe ca lalitā  bhrūvilāsatyanena moṭṭāyitamapi kaṭākṣitam makarandaḥ pratyabhijñaikasya tattedantāvaiśiṣṭayam asyā evākāraḥ soyamiti nāma saṃbhāvanāyām adṛṣṭacaratvena mādhavapratyabhijñāyā asambhavāditi bhāvaḥ tāmeva sphoṭayati atheti anantaraṃ tāḥ sakhyo he bhartṛdārike  svāmiputriī harṣeṇa vayaṃ vardhāmahe yatotraiva sthāne kasyāpi kopi tiṣṭatītyuktvā māmaṅgulīkhaṇḍalīlayā kathitavatyaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā salīlaṃ savilāsaceṣṭitaṃ yathā tathā pratinivṛtya strīṇāṃ vilāsaceṣṭitaṃ līlā iti bharataḥ uttālamudbhaṭam vibhramo vilāso viśiṣṭabhramaṇaṃ vā mañjurmanojñaḥ mañjīro nūpuraḥ rasitānuviddhaḥ śabdānugataḥ mekhalāyāḥ kaṃlāpo gucchaḥ yadvā mekhalā ca kalāpaśca tayoḥ kiṅkiṇī kṣudraghaṇṭā mekhalā ca kalāpañca bhavecchroṇivibhūṣaṇam ekayaṣṭirbhavetkāñcī mekhalā tvaṣṭayaṣṭikā  raśanā ṣoḍaśa jñeyā kalāpaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ  iti bharataḥ idaṃ sarva nivartanākriyāvi śeṣaṇam gatiriyaṃ vikalā yadāha  āvege caiva harṣe ca kāyai ca tvarayānvite eteṣu ca gati prājño vikalāṃ saṃprayojayet  iti rājā bhaṭṭārako devastatsutā bhartṛdārikā rājapadamīśvaramātraparam tenāmātyakanyāpi bhartṛdāriketyucyata ityavadheyam kopi kasyāpītyanenānudbhaṭodbhāvanena tāsāṃ cāturyamuktam ata eva kasyāpīti sāmānya nirdeśātallībatvam anyathā strīliṅganirdeśaḥ syāt kopīti puṃli manirdeśastu spaṣṭārthaḥ anyathā kimapīti nirdeśe puṣpādipratipatyā saṃśayaḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ aṅgulīdalapadena savilāsākhyānamuktaṃ saṅghaptamākhyānaṃ vā dhvanitam idamākhyānaṃ narmavākyam yadāha  sahāsyavacanaprāyaṃ narbhecchanti manīṣiṇaḥ raṇaraṇāyamāna pratinivṛtya vardhase kasyā api vallabhaḥdarśitavatyaḥ mahataḥ khalu prathamānu miyānu  STRATE POTETYmālatīmāghave kalahaṃsaḥ  ākarṇya kathaṃ sarasaramaṇīyānubandhinī strījanakathā kaithaṃ sarasaramaṇijjāṇubandhiṇī itvīaṇakahā makarandaḥ  tatastataḥ mādhavaḥatrāntare kimapi vāgvibhavātivṛttavaicitryamullasitavibhrama mutpalākṣyāḥ tadbharisāttvika vikāramapāsta dhairyamācāryakaṃ vijayi mānmathamāvirāsīt stimitavikasitānāmullasadbhūlatānāṃ masṛṇamukulitānāṃ prāntaivistārabhājām pratinayananipāte kiṃcidākuñcitānāṃ vividhamahamabhūvaṃ pātramālokitānām makarandaḥ hanta harṣe udbhedaḥ prakāśaḥ kalahaṃsaḥ anubandhinī pratīyamānā atrāntara ityādi sakhīnāṃ darśanāvasara eva padmākṣyāḥ saṃbandhi tanmānmathaṃ kāmajamācāryakamupadeśakarmāvirāsītprakaṭībhūtam kīdṛśam bhedāstrayastasya mahānubandhakā rkaśyasaṃjñāḥ kathitā vidagdhaiḥ  iti bharataḥ bhūri pracuraḥ sāttvikavikāro yatra tat sattvaṃ mānasaṃ kimapi tena nirvṛttaḥ sāttviko bhāvaḥ yadāha  sattvokaṭe manasi ye prabhavanti bhāvāste sāttvikā nigaditāḥ kavibhiḥ purāṇaiḥ  tecasvedaḥ stambhotha romāñcaḥ svarabhaṅgotha vepathuḥ vaivarṇyamañja pralaya ityaṣṭau sāttvikā matāḥiti apāstaṃ kṣiptaṃ dhīratvaṃ yena tat mahābhijanatvādyanapekṣatvāditi bhāvaḥ vijayi sarvatrāpratihatam kumāryā api śiśutvādvijaya iti bhāvaḥ utpalākṣyā ityanena bahuvidhe netravikāre prītigo hāva ihoktaḥ yadāha  bhrūnetrādivikārādyaḥ śṛṅgārākārasūcakaḥsthāyibhāvaḥ sthito hāva īrṣyātaḥ prītigopi ca iha śloke vilāsa uktaḥ yadāha   dayitāvalokanādau viśeṣoṅgakriyāsu yaḥ śṛṅgāraceṣṭāsahito vilāsaḥ samudīritaḥ samprati  helā hāvatsamutthitā  iti bharatānusāreṇa hāvānantaraṃ helāmāha stimitetyādi nārīṇāṃ priyasambhogalajjāsādhvasakautukaiḥ svabhāvāviṣkṛto vego heleti parikīrtitaḥ  iti bharataḥ ślokārthastu tasyā ālokitānāṃ sahasā darśanānāṃ pātraṃ yogyohamabhūvaṃ vṛttosmi  sahasā darśanaṃ yatsyāttadālokitamucyate iti bharataḥ kīdṛśānām mardāyarūpanirūpaṇāścaryeṇa stimitāni niścalāni harṣeṇa vikasitāni praphullāni ca teṣām dṛṣṭiriyamadbhutā edāṇaṃ anayoḥ  dhātivṛtivartī āyatākṣyāḥ manasi prīti tataśca taiśca prathamoṅkaḥ alasavalitamugdhasnigdhaniṣpandamandai ravika vikasadantarvismayasmeratāraiḥ hṛdayamaśaraṇaṃ me pakṣmalākṣyāḥ kaṭākṣairapahṛtamapaividdhaṃ pītamunmūlitaṃ ca yadāha  samākuñcitapakṣamāgrā vismayodbhutatārakā saumyā vikasitāntā ca dṛṣṭiḥ syādadbhutābhidhā  yadvā stimitaṃ mandaṃ yathā tathā vikasitānāṃ prakāśitānāṃ prathamaṃ nāyakadarśanena śanaiḥ śanaiḥ prasāraṇamiti bhāvaḥ anenottarottaradarśanābhilāṣaḥ sūcitaḥ ullasantī capalā bhrūleteva yeṣu teṣāṃ dīrghavena rūpakam anena kāntādṛṣṭiruktā yadāha  harṣaprasādajanitā kāntātyarthe samanmathā sabhrūkṣepakaṭākṣā caśṛṅgāre dṛṣṭiriṣyate  masaṇāni cikkaṇāni lajjayā mukulitāni ca teṣām dṛṣṭiriyaṃ mukulatā  mugdhā nimalitāntā ca mukulā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  iti bharataḥ yadvā sukhabhāvanayā masṛṇaṃ mandaṃ yathā bhavati tathā mukulitānām etena darśanajanitānandasaṃpatparyavasānaṃ sūcitam punaḥ punadarśanakā ṭryā tiryagāyatatvena prānte nikaṭe ca vistāravatām śaṅkitā dṛṣṭiriyam yadāha  kiṃciñcalatsthirā kiṃcinnamitā tiryagāyatā gūḍhā cakitatārā ca śaṅkitā dṛṣṭirucyate  anena kaṭākṣaparyavasānamuktam pratīpadigāyatamannetrapāte niścala tvenāpaviddhaṃ mathitam madhyamānatayā dravarūpatvena pītam ata evonmūlitam tadā kimapi mayā na jñātamityarthaḥ ata evāśaraṇaṃ rakṣakaśūnyaṃ jātam tato tataḥ calita niṣyanda api kaṭākṣo nikhāta iva datta iva tadā tadavalokanaṃ mama hṛdaye lagnamivetyarthaḥ nikhāta ityanena kaṭākṣasya duḥsahatvamuktam kīdṛśyā tadānanaṃ vahantyā kīdṛśam muhurvalitā vakitā kandharā ghāṭā yatra padmavivartanasiddhiḥ kīdṛśaḥ prathamamānandahetutayāmṛtena digdha upacitaḥ pañcāddarśanānanda vicchedādviṣeṇa digdhaḥ tataḥ prabhṛti tasmādārabhya paricchedetyādi vikāraḥ kāmajo bhāvontarjaḍayati ṇāma māladī evva sā bhave makarandaḥ  svagatam aho abhiṣvaṅgaḥ tatkiṃ niṣedhayāmi suhṛdam athavā mā mūmuhatkhalu bhavantamananyajanmā mā te malīmasavikāraghanā matirbhūt ityādi nanviha nirarthakameva yasmā tkāmañca jṛmbhitaguṇo navayauvanaṃ ca prakāśam api vaiyasyena vidite tadnvayanāmanī darśitā pariccheda vyaktirityādi sannikṛṣṭepi ghaṭādau paricchedavyaktirnirṇayābhivyaktirna bhavati ghaṭādikamapi nirṇetuṃ na śaknomītyarthaḥ anena bāhyendriyāṇāṃ viṣayavyāvṛttiruktā abhyastepi vāraṃvāramanubhūtepi smaraṇamatathābhāvena khaṇḍasphuṭitatayā virasaṃ vairasyavat etena manasopaṭutvamuktam iyamanusmṛtyavasthā viṣayanivṛttyā santāpaḥ śītalasevanādapi nāpaitītyāhahimasarasi śītalasarovare candramasya mṛtakarakiraṇe vā me na santāpahāniḥ candramaḥ padaṃ lakṣaṇayā svakiraṇamāha iyamudvegāvasthā yadāha  āsane śayane vāpi na tiṣṭhati na tuṣyati autsukyaṃ ca bhavennityamudvegasthāna eva ca  niṣṭhāśūnyaṃ dhairyarahitaṃ mano bhramati ca svalpatvāt kimapi manorathamālikhatyāliṅgati anenonmādāvasthoktā kalahaṃsaḥ apahṛto vaśīkṛtaḥ apiḥ saṃbhāvanāyām nāma prākāśye svagatamiti yattu śrāvyaṃ na sarvasya svagataṃ tadihocyate iti bharataḥ abhiṣvaṅga āsaktirūpo manaḥparābhavaḥ  ākrośaśāpābhibhaveṣvabhi dhvaṅgapadaṃ viduḥ  iti śāśvataḥ mā mūmuhādati ananyajanmā kāmaḥ khalvatyartha mā mūmuhat na cittaviplavasahitamajījanat evaṃ ca te matirmalīmasavikāreṇa kāmajena ghanā nibiḍā mā bhūdityādi niṣedhavākyamihānarthakameva nanupadamananvaye yataḥ kāmo jṛmbhito valayito guṇo jyā yasya saḥ jṛmbhitaguṇa upacitavyāpāro vā kāmaḥ navayauvanaṃ ca jṛmbhitaguṇamprakāśitarūpādikamastītyarthaḥ atastatparādhīnoyaṃ na niṣeddhuṃ śakya ityarthaḥ prakāśamiti  yattu sarvajanaśrāvyaṃ prakāśaṃ tadidveṣyate ayathā  ṣaṃgaḥ mahānabhi priyasu yasmin vayasya api prathamoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥ  sakhe śrūyatām atha tasyāḥ kareṇukaurohaṇasamaya eva marhataḥ sakhīkadambakādanyatamā vārayoṣidvilambya bālabakulakusamāvacayakrameṇa nedayisī bhūtvā praṇamya kusumāpīḍavyājena māmevarmuktavatī mahābhāga suśliṣṭaguṇatayā ramaṇīya eṣa vaḥ sumanasāṃ saṃniveśaḥ kutūhalinī ca no bhartṛdārikasmin vartate tasya abhinavo vicitraḥ kusumeṣu  vyāpāraḥ tadbhavatu kṛtārthatā vaidagdhyasya phalatu nirmāṇaramaṇīyatā vidhātuḥ samāsādayatu sarasa eṣa bhartṛdārikāyāḥ kaṇṭhāvalambanamahārghatām  iti makarandaḥ  aho vaidagdhyam iti bharataḥ anvayo vaṃśaḥ mādhavaḥ kareṇukā hastinī anyatamānyā svārthe tamap yadvā ekaparyāyoyamavyutpanna evānyatamaśabdaḥ vārayoṣigaṇikā tasyā īdṛktvādupādānamiha vilambyaikākinī bhūtvā nedīyasī nikaṭasthā ca bhūtvā ubhayatra puṣpatroṭanakrameṇeti yojyam kusumāpīḍavyājena puṣpadāmacchalena abhyarthanābhaṅgabhayena chalena māmāheti bhāvaḥ atha ca kusumenāpīḍayati kusumāpīḍaḥ kāmaḥ tadvyājena māṃ praṇamyetyarthaḥ mahābhāga mahābhāgya bhāgo bhāgyārthayorapi  iti viśvaḥ suśliṣṭaguṇatayā sulagnasūtratvena saṃniveśo racanābhedaḥ kutūhalinā puṣpadāmni kautukavatī bhartṛdāriketyanena kanyātvāddarśanautsukyamu ktam yadvā bharatena kanyāyā visrambhapātratvasvīkārā diha kanyātvena tatsūcanam ābhanavo lokottaro vicitro bahuprakāraḥ kusumeṣu puṣpeṣu vyāpāro racanāprabandhaḥ etena mālyagrathanakuśalādbhutakauśalakutūhālanī setyuktam vaidagdhyasya grathanacāturyasya kṛtārthatā kṛtaprayojanatā vidagdhapreyasīyaṃ praśaṃsayeti bhāvaḥ phalatu sapha lostu vidagdhajanāya dānāt sarasa evāmlāna eva sraksaṃniveśaḥ mahārghatāṃ bahumūlyatām pakṣe vo yuṣmākaṃ saṃnniveśaḥ saṃyogaḥ parasparānurūpādinā ramaṇīyaḥ krīḍārhorhaṇīya eva iha vaṃ iti  yuṣmado gurāvekeṣām iti gaurave bahuvacanam kutūhālanī dūtasamāje sākāṅkṣā abhinavobhūtapūrvaḥ tadekāsaktatvāt vicitraḥ sādhuḥ vividhavikārakāritvenāścaryajanako vā kusumeṣoḥ kāmasya vyāpāro mohanam vaidagdhyasya sakalakalābhijñatāyāḥ sārthakatvam vidagdhaprītijanakatvāt nirmāṇaramaṇīyatā ghaṭanasaundaryam phalatu anurūpajanaṃsasargāt no cedidaṃ sarve byarthamiti bhāvaḥ rasaḥ śṛṅgāronurāgo vā kaṇṭhāvalambanamāliṅganam mahārghatā durlabhatvam tadiha śliṣṭapadena nāyakavyutpattimabhiprāyaṃ ca jñātvā dūtīvyāpāraḥ prasaratīti dhvanitam makarandaḥ vaidagdhyaṃ śliṣṭapadaprayogāditi bhāvaḥ dhiro tataḥ dārikā vartate tasyā mabhi kusumeṣuvyā strīka kadambām mabhihitamālatī mādhave mādhavaḥ tayā ca madanuyuktayā samākhyātam  iyamamātyabhūrivasoḥ prasūtirmālatī nāmāhaṃ ca bhartṛdārikāyāḥ prasādabhūmirdhātreyikā lavaṅgikā nāmeti kalahaṃsaḥ  saharṣam kiṃ nāma mālatīti diṣṭyā vilasitaṃ khalu bhagavatā devena kusumāyudhena jitamasmābhiḥ kiṃ ṇāma māladitti diṭhṭhiā vilasidaṃ kkhu bhaavadā deveṇa kusumāuheṇa jidaṃ ahyo  makarandaḥ svagatam amātyabhūrivasorātmajetyaparyāptirbahumānasya api ca mālatī mālatīti modate bhagavatī kāmandakī tāṃ ca rājānandanāya prārthayate iti kiṃvadantī śrūyate mādhavaḥ  tayā cauhamanurudhyamānastāṃ bakulamālāmātmanaḥ kaṇṭhādavatārya dattavān asau punarabhiniviṣṭayā dṛśā mālatīmukhāvalokanavihastatayā viṣamaviracitaikabhāgāṃ tāmeva bahumanyamānā mahānayaṃ prasāda iti gṛhītavatī anantaraṃ ca yātrābhaṅgapracalitasya mahataḥ paurajanasya saṃkulena vighaṭitāyāṃ tasyāmāgatosmi makarandaḥ  vayasya mālatyā api snehadarśanātsuśliṣṭametat yopi hi kapolapāṇḍutādircihna sūcitaḥ prākpravṛddhastasyāḥ kāmābhiṣvaṅgaḥ sopi tvannibandhana iti vyaktamevaitat etattu na jñāyate va dṛṣṭapūrvastayā vayasya iti na khalu tādṛśyo mahābhāgadheyauḥ kumāryonyatrāsaktacetaso bhūtvāparatra cakṣūrogiṇyo bhavanti api ca mādhavaḥ anuyuktayā pṛṣṭayā prasūtirapatyam prasādabhūmirviśvāsasthānaṃ tasyāḥ tava ca prasādabhūmiranukampāpātraṃ mālādānāt kalahaṃsaḥ atra vilasitaṃ vizambhitam anayoranyonyānurāgāditi bhāvaḥ makarandaḥ bahumānasya gauravasyāparyāptiranavadhikatvam anabhiyojyatvarakṣatvādiyogāditi bhāvaḥ mādhavaḥ anurudhyamāno mahuryācyamānaḥ asaulavāṅgakā abhiniviṣṭayātiyatnaniveśitayā vihastatayā vyākulatayā mahānayaṃ prasāda iti yato na vastuni prema kiṃtu guṇeṣviti bhāvaḥ makarandaḥ suśliṣṭaṃ niścitam dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśyo mahākulajāḥ cakṣūrāgānurāgayoreka viṣayatvaṃ bharatamatam anyadapyanu ekāpatyaratnaṃ tajjita  ca kila yāṃcate cānubadhya abhyarthya  prati pauranaigama paurāhanā cihnaḥ prāganurāga bhiṣaṅga dheyajammānaḥ cānurāgiṇyaḥ kalahaṃsalakaṃ darśayati prathamoṅkaḥ anyonyasabhinnadṛśāṃ sakhīnāṃ tasyāstvayi prāganurāgacihnam kasyāpi kopīti niveditaṃ caṃ dhātreyikāyāścaturaṃ vacaśca upatya idaṃ ca daṃ a iti citrapha ubhau paśyataḥ makaranda  kalahaṃsaka kenaitanmādhavasya praticchaṃdakamabhilikhitam kalahaṃsaḥ  yenaivāsya hṛdayamapahṛtam jeṇa jevva se hiaaṃ avaharidaṃ makarandaḥ  api mālatyā kalahaṃsaḥ  atha kim aha iṃ vayasya makaranda prasannaprāyaste vitarkaḥ mādhavaḥ makarandaḥ  kalahaṃsaka kutosyādhigamaḥ kāśāt kalahaṃsaḥ  mayā tāvanmandārikāhastāt tayāpi lavabhinkāsa maie dāva mandāriahatthādo tāe vi lavaṅgiāsaāsādo makarandaḥ  atha kimāha mandārikā mandārikā mādhavālekhyaprayojanaṃ mālatyāḥ kalahaṃsaḥ  utkaṇṭhāvinoda iti ukkaṇṭhāviṇoda tti makarandaḥ  vayasya mādhava sarvathā samāśvasihi rāgacihnamāha  anyonyetyādi tvayi tasyāḥ prāganurāgacihnaṃ vyaktamevāsti katham sakhīnāmanyonyasaṃgatadṛśāṃ kasyapi kopīti nivedanamekam kathamanyathā sakhījanastvāṃ vīkṣya kaṭākṣayati tāṃ kathaṃ vā sakhījano vadatyevamiti bhāvaḥ aparaṃ lavaṅgikāyā vyutpannaṃ vacanam kathamanyathā kutūhalinītyādi vadatīyamiti bhāvaḥ  saṃgate dārite bhinnaḥ iti viśvaḥ kalahaṃsaḥ atra yena janenāpahṛtam yannibandhanosya kāmavikāra iti bhāvaḥ makarandaḥ mālatyā likhitamityarthaḥ kalahaṃsaḥ atha kiṃ svīkāre mādhavaḥ vitarka ūhaḥ makarandaḥ adhigamaḥ prāptiḥ kalahaṃsaḥ utkaṇṭhāvinoda iti mādhavānuraktā mālatī tamananuprāptavatī citralikhitālokanenāpi ramata iti bhāvaḥ kopyeṣa itīhitaṃ asmātparam  mādhavaḥ  kiṃ cānyat makarandaḥ  dhātre  iti kecit edaṃ cittam api nāma maha mama  mālatīmādhave yā kaumudī nayanayorbhavataḥ sujanmā tasyā bhavānapi manorathabandhabandhuḥ tatsaṃgamaṃ prati sakhe na hi saṃśayosti yasminvidhiśca madanaśca kṛtā bhiyogaḥ draṣṭavyasvarūpā ca bhavato vikārahetustadatraivālikhyatāṃ mālatī mādhavaḥ  yadabhirucitaṃ vayasyāya tadupanaya citraphalakaṃ citra cairtikāśca makaranda upanayati mādhavaḥ  likhan sakhe makaranda vāraṃ vāraṃ tirayati dṛśorudgamaṃ bāṣpapūrastatsaṃkalpopahita jaḍima stambhamabhyeti gātram sadyaḥ svidyannayamaviratotkampalolāṅgulīkaḥ pāṇirlekhāvidhiṣu nitarāṃ vartate kiṃ karomi yetyādi he sakhe tatsaṃgamaṃ prati naiva saṃśayosti bhavato nayanayoryā kaumadī jyotsnā ānandakāritvāt tasyā manorathabandhurabhilāṣanibandhanāya priyaḥ śobhanajanmā bhavānapi nanu parasparānurāgepi vidhikāmavaimukhyānna siddhirata āhayasminsaṃgame vidhimadanau kṛtaprayatnau cakṣuṣprītyā kāma etaddeśānayanādvidhiḥ kṛtābhiyoga ityarthaḥ abhiyogācca kanyālābhaḥ yadāha   abhiyogāddhi kanyāyā lābho niścita eva ca  iti citreṇa mādhavacittānurāgamuddīpayati  draṣṭavyeti mādhavaḥ vayasyāyetyatra rucyathanāṃ prīyamāṇa  iti saṃpradānatā adhunā manaḥsaharṣātsāttvikabhāvamāha vāraṃ vāramityādi ayaṃ mama pāṇirlekhāvidhiṣu citranirmāṇeṣu nitarāmatyarthe vartata eva na tu likhati atra kiṃ karomi yathā tathā likhāmītyarthaḥ natarām  iti pāṭhe naiva vartata ityarthaḥ yato bāṣpapūrastadanudhyānādānandāśrupravāho vāraṃvāraṃ dṛśorudramaṃ pracāraṃ tirayati chādayati tasyāḥ saṃkalpena cintanenopahito jaḍimā sarvakāryāpratipattiryasya tadgātraṃ śarīraṃ stambhaṃ niścalatvamabhyeti harṣabhayarogavismayaviṣādamadadoṣasaṃbhavaḥ stambhaḥ  iti bharataḥ kīdṛśaḥ sadyo likhanopakramakāla eva svidyannābhavan aviratotkampenādhikacalanena lolāṅgulī yatra saḥ aṅgulyā likhanahetutayā taccāpalyādalikhanaṃ sūcitam tadihāśrustambhasvedakampā uktāḥ romāñcādikaṃ ca noktam teṣāṃ likhanāpratikūlatvāt sarvamidaṃ sāttvikaṃ harṣāt yadāha  krodhabhayaharṣalajjāduḥkhaśramarogatāpapīḍābhyaḥ vyāyāmasādhvasādeḥ svedaḥ syātpīḍanenāpi śītabhayaharṣarodhasparśajarārogajaḥ kampaḥ  iti aghunā mālatī citraṃ yogau tatrabhavataḥ varti dṛśāvudgataḥprathamoṅkaḥ tathāpi vyarṣasitosmi cirādālikhya darśayati makarandaḥ citraṃ nirvarṇya upapannastāvadatrabhavatobhiṣvaṅgaḥ sakautukam kathamacireṇaiva nirmāya likhitaḥ ślokaḥ vācayati jagati jayinaste te bhāvā navendukalādayaḥ prakṛtimadhurāḥ santyevānye mano madayanti ye mama tu yadiyaṃ yautā loke vilocanacandrikā nayanaviṣayaṃ janmanyekaḥ sa eva mahotsavaḥ praviśya satvaraṃ mandārikā  kailahaṃsaka padānusāreṇopalabdhosi mādhavamakadrakṣyatīti sānurāgopālambhaṃ ślokaṃ likhati  jagatītyādi te te navendukalādayo bhāvāḥ padārthā jayino madajanane sarvatrāpratihatāḥ svabhāvato manojñā anye santyeva ye mano madayanti mama punarna madahetavaḥ pratyuta dāhahetava eveti bhāvaḥ atra jayina ityanena kālaviśeṣe deśaviśeṣe ca jayaśālina ānandasaṃdohadā ityuktam bhāvyante bhāvanāmarhanti sundaratayeti bhāvāḥ mālatībhinnāḥ sahṛdayahṛdayāhlādakāḥ te ta iti vīpsayā candrādayo devādayaśca prasiddhā eveti darśitam sarvanāmnā ca ye yatra cetaḥpratiṣṭhāste tatra gṛhyanta iti dhvanitam tuśabdenānyeṣāṃ tathātvaṃ tatsaṃpratipattidvāretyuktam kastarhi madaheturata āha  mama punariyaṃ citralikhitā mālatī nayanayojyotsnā yannetragocaraṃ prāptā sa evaikotra janmani mahotsavaḥ atra kiṃ punaḥ saṃbhogādikamityanurāgaḥ sa eva mahotsavaḥ anurāgo bhavatu mā vā bhūdityupālambhaḥ etenātyantānurāgo mālatyāṃ darśitaḥ ekapadenā nyeṣāmāvirbhāvepi nānandakatvam ata eva sa evetyanena tatpoṣaḥ janmanīti sāmānyanirdeśena samastajanmani mālatītulyā nāstīti vyajyate vācikoyaṃ rasaḥ yadāha   rasānurūpairālāpaiḥ ślokairvākyaiḥ padaistathā nānālaṃkārasaṃyuktairvāciko rasa ucyate  iti iha prakṛ timadhuratvepi mālatyā eva madajananādvyatirekālaṃkāraḥ priyākhyānātpriyolaṃkāraḥ vilocanacandriketi rūpakam na cātra navendukalā pratipacandrakalā sā ca na madaheturiti vācyam yato nūyata iti navaḥ praśastendurityarthaḥ yadvā navaṃ nūtanamindukalādikaṃ ceti dvandvaḥ yadvā navaḥ sāgarādutthitamātraḥ pūrṇa evetyarthaḥ praviśyeti yatra paṭīkṣepeṇa praveśastatra praviśyetyuktiḥ anusāronusaraṇam etepi ye citraphalake likhitāḥ iha gauravādekatve bahu avahitaḥ vilokya jātā manoratha paṭākṣepeṇa kalahaṃsa kalahaṃsa cora cora mālatīmādhave randau vilokye salajjam kathametāvapi mahānubhāvāvihaiva upasṛtya praṇamāmi kalahaṃsaa paāṇusāreṇa uvaladdhosi kadhaṃ edevi mahāṇuhāvā ih jevva paṇamāmi ubhau  mandārike ita ausyatām mandā  upaviśya kalahaṃsaka upanaya me citraphalakam kalahaṃsaa uvaṇehi me cittaphalaaṃ kala  gṛhāṇaitat gehra edaṃ mandā vilokyai kalahaṃsaka kena kiṃnimittaṃ vātra mālatyālikhitā kalahaṃsaa kene kiṃṇimittaṃ vā ettha māladī ālihidā kalahaṃsaḥ  ya eva yannimittaṃ mālatyā jo jevva jaṃṇimittaṃ māladīe mandā  saharṣam diṣṭayā darśitaphalamidānīṃ vijñānaṃ prajāpateḥ diṭhṭhiā daṃsidaphalaṃ dāṇiṃ viṇṇārṇa paāvaiṇo maka  mandārike yadatra vastunyeṣa te vallabhaḥ kathayati api tattartho mandā  mahābhāga atha kim mahābhāa a īṃ maka  va punarmālatī mādhavaṃ prāgdṛṣṭavatī mandā   lavaṅgikā bhaṇati vātāyanagateti lavaṅgiā bhaṇādi vādāaṇagadatti  maka  vayasya nanvamātyabhavanāsannarathyayaiva bahuśaḥ saṃcarāvahe tadupapannametat mandā  anumanyetāṃ māṃ mahānubhāvau yāvadetadbhagavato devasya vacanam dvitve vā bahuvacanam mālatyā abhilikhita iti śeṣaḥ tathā ca mālatyā vinodāya mādhavo likhitastenāpi sā tadarthaṃ likhitetyarthaḥ mandārikā atra vijñānaṃ śilpikauśalam anurūpānurāga danayoriti bhāvaḥ avitathaṃ satyam tattathota evametanmālatyaiva mādhavapraticchandakaṃ likhitamityarthaḥ vātāyanagatā dṛṣṭava dṛṣṭā eltha atra  āgamyatām gṛhītvā vi nirūppa kena uṇa punaḥ  saha svagataṃ vaiṇā sakhi mandā apyavitathaṃ tat tarahā mahābhāgau prathamoṅkaḥ madanasya sucaritaṃ priyasakhyai lavaṅgiāyai nivedayāmi aṇumaṇṇantu ma mahāṇubhāā jāva edaṃ bhaavado devassa maaṇassa sucaridaṃ piasahīe lavabhiāe ṇivedemi makaḥ  prāptāvasarametadbhavatyāḥ mandārikā citraphailakaṃ gṛhītvā niṣkrāntā makarandaḥ  vayasya kharatarakiraṇoyaṃ bhagavānsahastradīdhitiralaṃkaroti madhyamahnastadehi saṃstyāyameva gacchāvaḥ ityutthāya parikrāmataḥ mādhavaḥ  evaṃ hi manye api ca gharmāmbhovisaravivartanai ridānīṃ mugdhākṣyāḥ parijanavārasundarīṇām tatprātarvihitavicitrapatrarekhāvaidagdhyaṃ jahati kapolakuṅkurmāni unmīlanmukulakarālakundakośapraśyotaddhanamakarandagandhabandho tāmīṣatpracalavilocanāṃ natāṅgīmāliṅganpavana mama spṛśāṅgamaṅgam prātarviracitavikaiḥ dharmāmbhaso tītyarthaḥ lavaṅgikāyā dvārā mādhavānurāgo mālatyāmastvityarthaḥ makarandaḥ saṃstyāyo gṛham saṃstyāyaḥ saṃniveśe ca saṃghātapi ca dṛśyate  iti modinīkaraḥ gharmetyādi mālatyāḥ parijanavārasundarīṇāṃ kapolakuṅkumāni citrapatrāvalīvaidagdhyaṃ yattadadhunā madhyāhe jahati tyajanti visarasya samūhasya vivartanairvividhajalakaṇaiḥ karaṇaiḥ anena nāyikāyāḥ sukumāratayā niḥsahatvamuktam mālatyāḥ kanyātvena patrāvalyabhāvātparijanetyuktam māṅgalyatayā prātareva kuḍkumena patrāvalīlikhanam ata eva vasantakālasya śītatvātkuḍakumena bhūṣākaraṇamiti matamapāstam  dhārāsiktavasuṃdharāsurabhayaḥ ityabhidhānādvarṣākālaprastāvāt  samūhanivahavyūhasaṃdohavisaravrajāḥ  ityamaraḥ ihonmādāvasthā ata evātra tatsaṃbaddhā kathā yadāha  tatsaṃbaddhāṃ kathāṃ yuṅkte sarvāvasthāgatāmiha  iti unmīladiti he pavana unmīlanmukulena vikacakorakeṇa karālādviṣamātkundagucchātkṣarannibiḍamakarandaśca gandhaśca tayorbandho makarandasya yo gandhastadvandho tatsaha aṇumaṇṇādu mahābhāo mahābhāā ṇivedissābhi bhāṇḍam madhyānho vartate tadehi rībhiḥ kuṇḍalāni puccha koṣāt pracyo lalita pracalitalo mālatīmādhave makarandaḥ  svagatam abhihanti hanta kathameṣa mādhavaṃ sukumārakāyamanavagrahaṃḥ smaraḥ vaikṛtarvivartadāruṇaḥ acireṇa kalabhaṃ kaṭhora iva kūṭapārkalaḥ tadane bhagavatī kāmandakā naḥ śaraṇam mādhavaḥ  svagatam āścaryam paśyāmi tāmita itaḥ purataśca pañcādantarbahiḥ parita eva vivartamānām udbuddhamugdhakanakābjanibhaṃ vahantīmāsaktatiryagaparvartitadṛṣṭi vaktram careti vā īdṛśopi tvaṃ me na sukhāya kiṃtu tāpāyātastāṃ mālatīmiṣadāluiṅganmamāṅgamaṅgaṃ pratyaṅgaṃ spṛśa amṛtamayatadaṅgasaṅgaśītastvaṃ mama tāpaśāntaye bhaviṣyasīti bhāvaḥ yadvā tadīyatāpaśāntirbhavatvityanurāgāttāmāliṅgannityuktam tāṃ kīdṛśīm pracalanetrāṃ virahe pavanasya duḥsahatvena bhayāditastataḥ kṣiptanetrām ata eva namrībhavadanāṃ ca iha viṣamakundakośasaṃcaraṇena gatipratibandhānmāndyaṃ makarandasaṅgācchaityaṃ gandhabandhutayā saugandhyaṃ ca vāyoruktam īṣadāliṅgannityanena surabhipadenābhighātaniḥsahatvaṃ mālatyāmuktam  karālo danture tuṅge  karālo danture tuṅge ityamaraḥ mādhavasyānaṅgaduḥsahatvamāha abhihantītyādi eṣa smaronavagrahaḥ pratirodhaśūnyaḥ komalakāyaṃ mādhavaṃ kathamacireṇaivābhihanti hantānukampāyām hanta harṣenukampāyām  ityamaraḥ kīdṛśaḥ vikṛtasya bhāvo vaikṛtaṃ tasya vivartonyathāvasthānaṃ tena dāruṇo duḥkhadaḥ yathā kalabhaṃ karibālakaṃ mṛdukāyaṃ kaṭhoro duḥsahaḥ kūṭapākalo hastivātajvaraḥ acireṇa hanta tathetyarthaḥ sopyanavagrahopratikaraṇīyo vikṛtivivartadāruṇaśca bhavati  gajaṃ vātajvaro hanti tathā vai kūṭapākalaḥ  iti vaidyake makarandaḥ idaṃ svagatam svayamanadhyavasāyādāha  tadati ata eva bhagavatī jñānasaṃpanneha śaraṇaṃ rakṣikā dvitīyāṅkāvatāroyam yadāha   aṅkāvasāne yatraiva bhāvinoṅkasya sūcyate vastubījamupoddhātaiḥ soṅkāvatāra iṣyate idānīmunmādāvasthodbhāvanābalāttanmayatvamāha  paśyāsītyādi tāmekāmeva vivartamānāṃ prapañcarūpāṃ paritaḥ sarvatra paśyāmotyāścaryam vivartamānatvamevāha ita ita ubhayapārśve puratogre paścātpṛṣṭhe antarmanasi bahistvagbhāge anena tadāveśātsarvatra tanmayatvamuktam yadāha   yo yena bhāvenāviṣṭaḥ sukhadenetareṇa vā sa grahasmara vivarṇa pālaka atrabhavatī ātma bahiśca paritaśca māsaṅga ṅgi varjita prathamoṅkaḥ prakāśam vayasya mama hi saṃprati prasarati parimāthī kopyayaṃ dehadāhastirayati karaṇānāṃ grāhakatvaṃ pramohaḥ raṇaraṇakavivṛddhiṃ bibhradāṃvartamāna jvalati hṛdayamantastanmayatvaṃ ca dhatte iti niṣkāntāḥ sarve iti bakulavīthī nāma prathamoṅkaḥ tadāhitasaṃskāraḥ sarvaṃ paśyati tanmayam  parita ityatra paryabhibhyāṃ ca  iti tasiḥ kīdṛśīm vakraṃ vahantīm udbhaddhaṃ vikasitaṃ mugdhaṃ kāntaṃ yatsuvarṇapadmaṃ tato niratiśayā bhā dīptiryasya tat tannibhaṃ tattulyamiti vā etena gaurītvamuktam āsaktena mayyāsaktyā tiryagapavartitā dṛṣṭiryasya tat yathā yāntyā tayāhaṃ dṛṣṭastathaiva tāṃ paśyāmīti bhāvaḥ adhunā sarvākāreṇa pīḍāmāhaprasaratītyādi vayasya paśya saṃprati mama kopyanirvacanīyasvarūpo dehadāhaḥ prasarati vyāpnoti ata eva parimāthī sarvato mathanaśīlaḥ karaṇānāmindriyāṇāmarthagrāhakatvaṃ me pramohastirayati pidadhāti sarvendriyasaṃmoho mametyarthaḥ mama gātraṃ śarīram kartṛ raṇaraṇakasya viyogatarorvṛddhimu pacayaṃ bibhradāvarti bhrāmyadasti yadvā raṇaraṇakaḥ kāmastasya vivṛddhimadhikādhikadaśāgāmitvam  māro raṇaraṇaḥ kāmo viṣayaḥ  ityutpalinī tathā mama hṛdayam kartṛ antardahati jvalatītyarthaḥ tanmayatvaṃ mālatīmayatvaṃ ca dhatte īdṛśī mama daśā saya eva vipattimādadhāti tadatra yathāvattvamācareti bhāvaḥ atrāvartīti vyādhiḥ jvala tītyudvegaḥtanmayatvamityunmādaḥ hṛdayasya tu tanmayatvadhāraṇena duḥsahadaśāyāmapi ṣatvam  uta niścayavitarkayoḥ iti dharaṇiḥ kāmopacaraṇaṃ narma yadāha  upacāraḥ strīpuṃsayormanojanmanibandhanaḥ sa evātra parijñeyo narmasaṃjñaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ  iti bharataḥ lavaṅgikā itīti syājjanāntikam  iti bharataḥ lavaṅgikā mālatīṃ sākāṅkṣayati udgamamutpattim mālatī asti me kutūhalam tatpṛcchetyarthaḥ lavaṅgikā atra yasya kṛta iti śeṣaḥ kāmandakī sakṛtrimāvahitthamāha ekaguruḥ samānaṃ tīrthamupādhyāyo yasya  samānatīrthe vāsī  iti yapratyayaḥ vyatikaritetyādi iha jagati kathamapi śāpādinā tādṛśāḥ svargiṇaḥ saṃbhavanti kīdṛśāḥ yaśobhirvyāptadiksvarūpāḥ kāma  nepathye śaṅkhadhvaniḥ   aho kātipātaḥ saṃprati hi kṣipannidrāmudrāṃ madanakalaha cchedasulabhāmaivāptotkaṇṭhānāṃ vihagamithunānāṃ prathamataḥ dadhānaḥ saudhānāmalaghuṣu nikuñjeṣu ghanatā masau odarahma sopānenāvatarāvaḥ kāma  apavārya sādhu saṃprati mayā taṭasthyaiva mālatīṃ prati nisṛṣṭārthadūtīkṛtyasya laghūkṛto bhāraḥ tatha hi varenyasmindveṣaḥ pitari vicikitsā ca janitā manaḥpratiṣṭhasāhasavāñchayā brūte  lavaṅgikā  saṃjananena  iti pāṭhe saṃjananaṃ sopānameva kāmandakī taṭasthatayā ghaṭitatvena sādhutvam nisṛṣṭārtheti strīpuṃsayorāśayamādadhānā svayaṃ ca kārye pratipādayantī sṛṣṭārthikā sā paradārayoge dūtī niyojyā bahudhā sudhībhiḥ iti bharataḥ mālatīṃ pratītyanena madayantikāṃ prati vidyata eveti prakṛte niṣpannaṃ svavyāpāramāhavara ityādi anyasminvare nandane dveṣaḥ kāritaḥ pitāra nindā janitā purāvṛttodvāraiḥ śakuntalādīnāṃ pitṛnirape vatse sukhaṃ sthīyatām sahi kadhaṃ ppasūdo vopyasau subha saṃjavaṇeṇa avalokite sādhu vṛttasya thaṃdūtyasya kutaḥ māhābhāgyaṃ vidhivi tṛtīyoṅkaḥ tataḥ praviśati buddharakṣitā buddharakṣitā  parikramya ākāśe avalokite api jānāsi kva bhagavatīti avaloide avi jāṇāsi kahiṃ bhaavaditti avalokitā  praviśyai buddharakṣite kiṃ pramugdhāsi kopi kālo bhagavatyāḥ piṇḍapātavelāṃ varjayitvā mālatīmanuvartamānāyāḥ buddharakkhide kiṃ pamuddhāsi ko vi kālo bhaavadīe piṇḍapāṃdavelaṃ vajjia māladīṃ aṇuvamāṇāe prasthitāsi huṃ tumaṃ uṇa kahiṃ buddha  huṃ tvaṃ punaḥ huṃ tvaṃ punaḥ kutra patthidāsi ava  ahaṃ khalu bhagavatyā tasya śaṃkaragṛhāsaṃbaddhaṃ kusumākaraṃ nāmodyānaṃ gatvā kubjakanikuñjaparya ntaraktāśokagahane tiṣṭheti gataśca tatra mādhavaḥ ahaṃ kkhu bhaavadīe māhavasaāsaṃ aṇuppesidā saṃdi a tassa saṃkaragharasaṃbaddhaṃ kusumāaraṃ ṇāma ujjāṇaṃ gadua kujjaaṃṇi uñjaperantarattāsoagahaṇe citi gado a tattha māhavo kṣātmadānakathanaiḥ kāryaparipāṭī kathitā māhātmyaṃ mahattvaṃ tasya stutaṃ yatkulādyacca guṇāttadapi iti hetoḥ anantaraṃ vatsasya paricayaḥ samāgamo vidhātuḥ kartavyaḥ etenāṅkāvatāropi sūcitaḥ prasaṅgādvyājādanyāpadeśāditi sarvatra yojyam dhavalagṛha iti dhavalagṛhopalakṣita ityarthaḥ asūta yaṃ ratnadharonavadyonavadyarūpā damayantikā ca jagaddharaṃ tatkṛtaṭippaṇeṅkogamaddatīyo rasarāśivāsaḥ iti dvitīyoṅkaḥ mādhavasakāśamanueṣitā saṃdiṣṭaṃ ca tadārambhasya pratijñātaparicayasyānyonyadarśanālāpādirūpasamāgamātmakatayā tvena tannirvāhikāyā madayantikāyāḥ sūcanāya tatsaṃbandhādbuddharakṣitā praveśaḥ yadvā niyuktaiva mayā buddharakṣitetyanena prathamā dvitīye ca mālatī prati laghūkṛto bhāra ityanena sūcito buddharakṣitāyāḥ praveśaḥ avalokitā atra pramugdhā prasmṛtā piṇḍapātaḥ saugatānnam kopyakālo niṣiddhakālaḥ tathā caiva sadaiva mālatīsamīpe bhagavatī vartata ityarthaḥ buddharakṣitā humanumatau smaraṇe vā avalokitā atra itarāḥ hā dhik hā dhik gāḍhaprahāratayā klāmyati mahābhāgaḥ haddhī haddhī gāḍhappahāradāe kilammadi mahābhāo mādhavaḥ  kathaṃ pramugdha eva kāmandakīṃ prati bhagavati paritrāyasva mām kāma ityamaraḥ kā mādhavau vyāghrabhayatrāṇopakāritayā vyavasthita madayantikāsaṃbandhātsaharṣatvam daṃṣṭrāyudho vyāghraḥ pramathito nihataḥ amunetyarthāt itarāḥ duṣṭamupakrāntaṃ durjātam kāma vyāghre caure ca vyālaḥ iti śāśvataḥ sa makarandaḥ kṣititalaniṣaktakhaḍga latāvaṣṭambhena niścalaḥ iha kṣatena rujārūpaḥ saṃdhipraveśa uktaḥ yadāha   rujā proktā prahāravyathā avaṣṭambhanamavaṣṭambhaḥ saṃbhrāntā vimugdhā pramugdho mohaṃ gataḥ kāma iti darśanātsamāśvāsa iti bhāvaḥ makaranda iti paśyāma prāsūta yaṃ ratnadharotimānyotimānyarūpā damayantikāpi jagaddharaṃ tatkṛtaṭippaṇeṅkogamattṛtīyo rasarājiramyaḥ iti tṛtīyoṅkaḥ vyasarasau kṛtaścāmunā asmātprāk  priyaṃ priyaṃ naḥ saṃvṛttam iti ṭī viṣakta niṣaṇṇa bhāgo makarandaḥ pari paritrāyasva nanvehi paśya vastāvatcaturthoṅkaḥ tataḥ praviśato madayantikālavaṅgikābhyāmavalambitau pramugdhau mādhavamakarandau saṃbhrāntā kāmandakī mālatī buddharakṣitā ca mada  prasīda bhagavati paritrāyasva paritrāyasva madayantikānimittaṃ saṃśayitajīvitaṃ vipannajanānukampinaṃ mahābhāgam pasīda bhaavadi parittāhi parittāhi madaantiāṇimittaṃ saṃsaidajīvidaṃ vivarṇaijāṇukampiṇaṃ mahābhāaṃ itarāḥhā dhik hā dhik kimidānīmasmābhiratra prekṣitavyam haddhī haddhī kiṃ dāṇiṃ ahiṃ ettha pekkhidavvaṃ kāma  ubhau kamaṇḍalūdakena siktvā nanu bhavatyaḥ paṭāñcalena vatsau vījayantu mālatyādayastathā kurvanti makarandaḥ  samāśvasyāvalokya ca vayasya kimetat nanu svastha evāsmi atikātarosi mada  saharṣam aho pratibuddhamidānīṃ makarandapūrṇacandreṇa ahmahe paḍivuddhaṃ dāṇiṃ maarandapuṇṇacandeṇa mālatī  mādhavasya lalāṭe hastaṃ datvā mahābhāga diṣṭyā vardhase nanu bhaṇama pratibuddha eva te priyavayasyaḥ pratipannacetano mahābhāgo makaranda itimahābhāa diṭhṭhiā vaḍūsi ṇaṃ bhaṇāmi paḍivuddho jeva de piavaasso paḍivaṇṇaceaṇo mahābhāo maarando tti mādhavaḥ  samāśvasya vayasya sāhasika ehyehiityāliṅgati kāma  ubhau śirasyāghrāya diṣṭayā jīvitavatsāsmi itarāḥ  priyaṃ priyaṃ naḥ saṃvṛttam piaṃ piaṃ ṇo saṃuttaṃ sarvā harṣe nāṭayanti janāntikam halā madayantike eṣa eva saḥ buddha halā madaantie eso jevva so tata iti saṃbhrāntā vyākulā mada anāpannamāpadgatam ammahe harṣe ācarye vā mālatī vardhasa ityanena vardhāpanaṃ yācanoktiprakāraḥ kāma śirasyāghrāṇamāyurvardhanāyeti vṛddhāḥ buddha haleti sakhīsaṃbodhanam mālanī saṃbhrāntāca ṇimittasaṃ vipaṇṇānu puṇṇimā sakhi lavaṅgike āśvasya jīvadvatsāmālatīmādhave mada  sakhi jñātameva mayā yathaiṣa mādhavoyamapi sajana iti sahi jāṇīdaṃ jevva mae jaha eso māhavo aaṃ vi so jaṇo tti buddha  api satyavādinyaham avi saccavādiṇī ahaṃ mada  na khalvanyādṛśeṣu yupmādṛśya pakṣapātinyo bhavanti mādhavamavalokya sakhi mālatyā api ramaṇīyosminmahānubhāvenurāgapravādaḥpunarmakarandameva saspṛhamavalokayati ṇa kkhu aṇṇārisesu tuhmārisīo pakkhavādiṇīo honti sahi māladīe vi ramaiṇījjo imassi mahāṇuhāve aṇurāappavādo kāma  svagatam svagatam ramaṇīyorjitaṃ hi madayantikāma karandayo daivādadya darśanam prakāśam vatsa makaranda kathaṃ punarāyuṣmānasminnavasare madayantikājīvitaparitrāṇaheturbhagavatā daivena saṃnidhāpitaḥ maka  adyāhamatairnagara eva kāṃcidvārtāmupaśrutya mādhavasya cittodvegamadhikamāśaṅkamānastvaritamavalokitāniveditakusumākarodyānavṛttāntaḥ parāpatanneva śārdūlāvaskandagocaragatāmetāmabhijātakanyakāmabhyupapannavānasmi mālatīmādhavau vimṛśataḥ kāma   svagatam vṛttena khalu mālatīpradānena bhavitavyam prakāśam vatsa mādhava diṣṭayā suhṛdbuddhyā vardhitosi mālatyā tadayamavasaraḥ prītidāyasya makarandanāmāgrahaṇena svāmitvamabhipraiti madyantikā saṃbhāvanāyāmapiśabdaḥ na hi pakṣapātinyastvādṛśyo mandaṃ bhadraṃ vadantīti bhāvaḥ kāma akleśopanatatvena ramaṇīyam śārdūlanāśenopakārapūrvakamutpannatvādūrjitaṃ sātiśayam  āyuṣmāniti vṛddhena vācyo bālaḥ śubhāśayaḥ iti bharataḥ maka udyāna vṛttānto mālatīpratyakṣamuttaropakramaḥ parāpatannāgacchan avaskandotikramaḥ gocaramityajahalliṅgatayānvayaḥ abhijātā kulīnā tathā cābhijātyena madupakāraṃ jñāsyatīti bhāvaḥ ābhijātyena jñānaṃ ca tathāvidhākārādinā kanyaketyatrānukampāyāṃ kan abhyupapattiḥ prāptiḥ vimṛśataḥ parasparakleśakā esa pio jaṇo esa mahābhāo māha aaṃ alā ṇijjo evva saṃdarśa hetoḥ nagare imām vṛttāntenacaturthoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥbhagavati īṃyaṃ hi yadyālavraṇitasuhṛtpramohamugdhaṃ saujanyādvihitavatī gatavyathaṃ mām tatkāmaṃ prabhavati pūrṇapātravṛttyā svīkarte mama hṛdayaṃ ca jīvitaṃ ca lava  pratīṣṭaḥ khalu naḥ priyasakhyāyaṃ prasādaḥ paḍicchido va ṇo piasahīe aaṃ pasādo madayantikā  svagatam jānāti mahānubhāvoyaṃ janovasare gurukaramaṇīyaṃ mantrayitum jāṇādi mahāmuhāvo asa aramāṇijjaṃ mantiduṃ mālatī  svagatam kiṃ nāmakarandenodvegakāraṇaṃ śrutaṃ bhaviṣyati kiṃ ṇāma maarandeṇa uvveakālaṇaṃ sudaṃ bhavissadi mādhavaḥ  vayasya kā punarmamādhikodvegaiheturvārtā praviśya puruṣaḥ  vatse madayantike bhrātā te jyāyānamātyanandanaḥ samādiśati adya parameśvareṇāsmadbhavanamāgatya bhūrivasorupari paraṃ viśvāsamasmāsu ca prasādamāviṣkurvatā svayameva pratipāditā mālatī tadeha saṃbhāvayāvaḥ pramodamiti  vayasya iyaṃ sā vārtā maka bhāvaḥ prītidāyasya vardhāpakadānasya yadityādi vyāghrakhaṇḍitasuhṛtpramohena saṃtaptaṃ māṃ saujanyena vigatakleśaṃ kṛtavatī tatotyartha mama hṛdayaṃ jīvitaṃ ca pūrṇapātravṛttyā vardhāpakena svīkartumiyaṃ prabhavati tvaṃ ca prabhavasītyarthaḥ tadāyatte me hṛdayajīvite iti bhāvaḥ yadvā corikāvivāhasaṃpādanena hṛdayahāritā nocejjīvitahāritetyarthaḥ  vardhāpakaṃ yadānandādalaṅkārādikaṃ punaḥ ākṛṣya gṛhyate pūrṇapātraṃ pūrṇānakaṃ ca tat  iti hārāvalī  pūrṇapātraṃ vardhāpakepi ca  iti medinīkaropi madayantikā gurukaramaṇīyaṃ śrotrasukham mādhavaḥ makarandena kāṃcidvārtāmupatratyeti yaduktametacchaṅkamānaḥ pṛcchati  vayasyeti puruṣaḥ jyāyāñjyeṣṭhaḥ parameśvaro iyaṃ mālatī kāruṇyāt bhagavati mahābhāadheo ṇuhāvo jaṇo gurua iti nāsti kvacit udvegavārtā prasādam mālatīmādhave mālatīmādhavau vaivarṇya nāṭayataḥ mada  saharṣaṃ mālatīmāśliṣyaṃ sakhi mālati tvaṃ khalvekanagaranivāsena sahapāṃsukrīḍanātprabhṛti me priyasakhyāsīrbhaginikā ca sāṃprata punargṛhasya maṇḍanaṃ jātāsi sahi māladi tumaṃ kkhu ekkaṇaaraṇivāseṇa sahapaṃsukīlaṇādo pahudi me piasahī āsī vaiṇiā a saṃpadaṃ u gharassa maṇḍaṇaṃ jādāsi kāma vatse madayantike diṣṭayā vardhase bhrāturmālatīlābhena mada  yuṣmākamāśiṣāṃ prabhāveṇa sakhi lavaṅgike phalitā no manorathā yuṣmākaṃ lābhena tuhmāṇaṃ āsisāṇaṃ pahāveṇa sahi lavaṅgie phalidā ṇo maṇorahā tuhmāṇaṃ lāheṇa V lava  sakhi kimasmākamapyetanmantrayitavyam sahi kiṃ ahmāṇaṃ vi edaṃ mantidavyam mada  sakhi buddharakṣite idānīṃ vivāhamahotsavaṃ saṃbhāvayāvaḥ sahi buddharakkhide dāṇiṃ vivāhamahosavaṃ saṃbhāvehma buddha  sakhi ehi gacchāvaḥsahi ehi gacchadma ityuttiṣṭhataḥ lava  janāntikam  bhagavati yathaite hṛdayabharitodvṛttavismayānandasundarā āndolāyamānadhīratvamanoharāḥ paryasyanti kaṭākṣavikṣepāstathā madayanti tarka kāmakarandayordalitanīlotpaladāmasadṛkṣāḥ rājā viśvāsamabhedam saṃbhāvayāmaḥ kārayāmaḥ utsavapūrvako harṣaḥ pramodaḥ madayantikā madbhātṛvadhūbhaviṣyasīti bhāvaḥ kāmandakī nośavdosmākamityarthe niṣedhe ca tulyarūpa iti niṣedhopyatra sphurati ata eva sotkaṇṭhamāha  bhrāturityādi madaya ubhayatrottaramāha yuṣmākamiti bhariā iti pāṭhe bhṛtāḥ pūrṇā ityarthaḥ lavaṅgikā ayamabhisaṃdhiḥ yūyaṃ rājñaḥ praṇayino vayaṃ sevakāḥ ato yuṣmatsaṃbandhena vayaṃ pūrṇamanorathā iti vacanamātram vastutastu tvatsaṃbandha evāsmākaṃ na bhaviteti mādhavavivāhasyāvaśyakatvāt yadvā yadetattvayā mantritamasmākaṃ manorathāḥ pūrṇā yuṣmākaṃ lābheneti vayameva tadvadāmaḥ tena tvaṃ makarandena pariṇetavyeti manorathā asmākameva pūrṇā bhaviṣyantīti gūḍhamuktam vyaktaṃ tu yuṣmākaṃ rājamitrāṇāṃ lābhena rājasevakā vayameva pūrṇamanorathā iti bhāvaḥ yaṃdvā etatkāmandakyākhyaṃ mantrirūpaṃ dravyamasmākamapyatra viṣaye vartate tena pratihatametat lavaṅgikā atra bharamito bharitaḥ śakandhvāditvātpararūpam yadvā bharaṇaṃ bharaḥ bharaḥ saṃjātosya tārakāditvāditac vyavasthitavibhāṣayā veṃṭprāpteḥ ata eva vāsavadattādau bhariteti prayogaḥ hṛdaye bharitau pūrṇāvudvṛttā āliṅgaca uṇa ahmāṇaṃ asmākaṃ  pasādeṇa bhariā asthi ei dāva mahosabaṃ parivartantecaturthoṅkaḥ yāmi maṃnorathanirvṛttasamāgamāvetāviti bhaavadi jahā e hiaabhairaduvvittavihmaāṇandasundarau āndolāantadhīrattaṇamahoharā pallatthanti madaantiāmaarandāṇaṃ dalidakandodāmasaricchā kaḍakkhavikkhevā tahā takkemi maṇorahaṇivyuttasamāmā detti kāma  vihasya nanvimau vilokanena manasaṃ muhurmuhurmonamanubhavataḥ tathā hi īṣattiryagvalanaviṣamaṃ kūṇitaprāntametatpremodbhedastimitaluṃlitaṃ kiṃcidākuñcita antarmodānubhavamasṛṇaṃ stambhaniṣkampapakṣma vyaktaṃ śaṃsatyaciramanayordṛṣṭamākekarākṣam vamāntau vismayānandau tābhyāṃ sundarāḥ vyāghranipātāddhṛdayanihito vismayaḥ iṣṭadarśanādānandaḥ āndolitaṃ parityaktaṃ yaddhīratvaṃ tena manoharāḥ dalitaṃ vikasi tam kando nīlotpalam sadṛkṣāstulyāḥ kāntādṛṣṭiriyam kāmandakī mohanaṃ suratam ata eva kāmaśāstram   mohanaṃ nārabhettāvadyāvannotkaṇṭhitā priyā  iti īṣadityādi etadanayordṛṣṭaṃ darśanaṃ vyaktaṃ śaṃsati yadetau mānasaṃ mohanamanubhavata ityanvayaḥ dṛṣṭaṃ kīdṛśam īṣanmanāktiryagvalitena viṣamaṃ mandam anena saṃkalpasaṃgatānaṅgasya parābhyūhaśaṅkiteyaṃ dṛgityuktam yadāha  śaṅkāyāṃ śaṅkitā jñeyā iti kuñcitaprāntamākuñcitāpāṅgam madayantikāyā jaḍatvānmakarandasyānyadarśanasāsūyatvājjihmā dṛṣṭiḥ yadāha  jihyā dṛṣṭirasūyāyāṃ jaḍatālasyayostathā iti dṛṣṭidvayana surataprāgavasthoktā premṇa udbhedādatiparipākāstimitaṃ sthiraṃ lulitamardhamukulitaṃ ca ardhamukuliteyaṃ dṛk yadāha  aṅgādiṣvardhamukulā gandhasparśasukhādiṣu ardhavyākoṣapakṣmāyā grastārdhamukulaiḥ puṭaiḥ smṛtārdhamukulā dṛṣṭiḥ kiñcinmīlitatārakā  anena ratābhoga uktaḥ nakhadaśanakṣatādiśaṅkayā mānaṃ sūcayati kiñcidākuñcite anamite bhruvau yatra tat ekasyā eva bhruva utkṣepaṇaṃ kuñcanamiha yadāha ekasyā evaṃ utkṣepo bhruvaḥ kuñcanamucyate  kope cāsya prayogaḥ yahāhakope vitarke helāyāṃ līlādau sahaje tathā darśane grahaṇe caiva bhruvamekāṃ samutkṣipet mānasyālpatvasūcanārthamā prayogaḥ ratāvasānamāha  hṛdaye harṣānubhavena masṛṇaṃ snigdhaṃ mandaṃ vā ratānte lajjāmāhastambhaṃ lajjānvitatayā patitārdhapuṭatvāt kathaṃ punaḥ saṃbhogo bhāvīti cintayā niṣkampam śūnyatayā niṣkampaṃ vā tādṛśaṃ pakṣma
