trasta I mālatīmādhave puruṣaḥ  vatse madayantike ita itaḥ maida  apavārya sakhi buddharakṣite api punarapi dṛśyate eka jīvitapradāyī puṇḍarīkalocanaḥ sahi buddharakkhide avi puṇopi dīsai eso jīvidappadāī puṇḍarīaloaṇo buddha  yadi daivamanukūlaṃ bhaviṣyati jai devvaṃ aṇuūlaṃ bhavisadi iti puruṣeṇa saha niṣkrānte mādhavaḥ  apavārya cirādāśātantustraṭatu bisinīsūtrabhiduro mahānādhiivyādhirniravadhiridānīṃ prasaratu pratiṣṭhāmavyājaṃ vrajatu mayi pāriplavadhurā vidhiḥ svāsthyaṃ dhattāṃ bhavatu kṛtakṛtyaśca madanaḥ atha vā samānapremāṇaṃ janamasulabhaṃ prārthitavato vidhau vāmārambhe mama samucitaiṣā pariṇatiḥ tathāpyasmindānaśravaṇasamayesyāḥ pravigalatprabhaṃ prātaścandradyuti vadanamantardahati mām iha yatra tadvicchedamāha  ākekaramakṣi yatra tat ākekarā tvarāloke vicchede proṣiteṣu ca ityādyuktam tadihākekaralakṣaṇa ākuñcitetyādi prathamapadenoktam dvitīyena muhurvyāvṛttatāretyuktam tṛtīyena harṣitārdhetyāyuktam mayantikā api nāma saṃbhāvanāyām avyayasamudāyatvāt mādhavaḥ karuṇāvasthāmāha  cirādityādi ciraśaṅkitaḥ āśātanturmālatīprāptyāśā rūpahṛdayāvalambanaṃ saṃprati bhidyatām bisinīpūtravadbhiduro bhedanasvabhāvo yataḥ bhideḥ karmakartarīti kurac saṃbhūya truṭitatvena mṛṇālatantusāmyam nairāśyānmaraṇamāha ādhirmanovyathā tadrūpo vyādhiranavācchannota eva mahān vyāpnotu mahattvaniravadhitvābhyāṃ maraṇamāha āśācchedānantaraṃ ca maraṇamucitameva yadāha  sarvaiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārairyadā nāsti samāgamaḥ kāmāgninā samāptasya jāyate maraṇaṃ tataḥ strīhetumaraṇādadhīratvamāśaṅkayānujñottaramāha pāriṣṭhavadhurā capalakakṣā  avyājaṃ satyaṃ  pratiṣṭāṃ  sthitiṃ mayi badhnātu abhīṣṭalābhena vidhirnirākulo bhavatu mālatīṃ vinā duḥsahavedanādāyī manobhūḥ kṛtakṛtyo bhavatu maraṇādadhikaṃ kiṃ kartavyamasyetyarthaḥ etadupālambhagarbhe vaca udvegāt yadāha   hṛddāhacintāniḥśvāsaglānikhedaprajāgaraiḥ rodanairmandabhaṇitaidaivopālambhanena ca  iti samānetyādi vāmārambhe pratikūle vidhau mamaiṣā pariṇatiḥ pūrvoktā yuktaiva kī etannāsti kvacit drakṣyate aviṇāma adhi vyājāṃ sthairyam samuditā paricaturthoṅkaḥ kāmandakī  svagatam evamatidurmanāyamānaḥ pīḍayati māṃ vatso mādhavo vatsā mālatī ca duṣkaraṃ nirāśā prāṇiti prakāśam vatsa mādhava pṛcchāmi tāvadāyuṣmantam api bhavānamaṃsta yathā bhūrivasureva mālatīmasmabhyaṃ dāsyatīti mādhavaḥ  salajjam nahi nahi kāma  na tarhi prāgavasthāyāḥ pairihīyase maka bhagavati darttepūrvetyāśaṅkayate kāma  jānāmi tāṃ khalu vārtām idaṃ tāvatprasiddhameva yathā nandanāya mālatīṃ prārthayamānaṃ bhūrivasurnṛpatirmuktavānprabhavati nijasya kanyakājanasya mahārāja iti makarandaḥ  astyetat kāmandakī  adya ca rājñā svayameva dattā mālatīti puruṣeṇāveditam tadvatsa vākpratiṣṭhāṃni dehināṃ vyavahāratantrāṇi vāci puṇyāpuṇyahetavo vyavasthitāḥ sarvaṃ ca vacanānāmāyattam sā ca bhūrivasorvāganṛtātmikaiva na khalu mahārājasya mālatī nijā kanyakā kanyakapradāne ca nṛpatayaḥ pramāṇamiti naivaṃvidho dharmācārasamayaḥ tasmādavimarśitavyametat kathaṃ ca vatsa māmanavadhānāṃ manyase paśya dṛśasya tulyaprītiṃ duṣprāpaṃ janaṃ yācitavataḥ vāme hi vidhau sulabhamapi na labhyate kiṃ punarasulabhamiti bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭakāraṇasyānupalambhādvidhervāmatvam asulabhatvaṃ paratantrattvāt yadyapi yukterthe khedo nāsti tathāpyasyā mālatyāstādṛśaṃ mukhaṃ māmantardahati etanmukhaṃ vīkṣya manastāpo me bhavatīti bhāvaḥ asmindānaśravaṇasamaye nandanāya mālatī dātavyeti śrutvā khedātkāntiśūnyatvam ata eva prātaścandrakānta kvāpi vigatakānti bhavati atha ca prātañcandropamayā rāgadhvanevidhiṃ prati mālatīkopopi sūcitaḥ kāmandakīduṣkaraṃ yathā tathā prāṇiti jīvati amasta manyate sma prāgavasthā mālatīprāptilakṣaṇā taddānasyājñānāditi bhāvaḥ dattapūrvā pūrva dattā supsupeti samāsaḥ idaṃ ca tāpahetuḥ vāgiti vāci sarva pratiṣṭitamiti bhāvaḥ anṛtātmikāsatyā dharmācārasamayo dhārmikasiddhāntaḥ etad api bhavānityasya prāk kvacit atha kiṃ bhūrivasuḥ parihīyate adatapūrvā tu evamukta saṃpratyeva puru nibandhanāni vyavasthāḥ sarveṣāṃ janānāmāyatanta iti kanyādāne mevaitat mālatīmādhave mā vo sapatneṣvapi nāma tadbhūtpāpaṃ yadasyāṃ tvayi vā viśaṅkayam tatsarvathā saṃgamanāya yatnaḥ prāṇavyayenāpi mayā vidheyaḥ  suṣṭhu yujyamānamādiśyate yuṣmābhiḥ api ca dayā vā sneho vā bhagavati nijesmiñśiśujane bhavatyāḥ saṃsārādviratamapi cittaṃ dravayati aṃtaśca pravrajyāsulabhasamayācāravimukhaḥ prasaktaste yatnaḥ prabhavati punardevamaparam nepathye bhagavati kāmandaki eṣā maṭṭinī vijñāpayati mālatīṃ gṛhītvā tvaritamāgaccheti bhaavai kāmandai esā bhaṭṭiṇī viṇṇāvedi jadhā māladiṃ gheṇa turidaṃ ācchetti kāmandakī  vatse uttiṣṭha maka  sarve uttiṣṭhanti mālatīmādhavau sakaruṇānurāgamanyonyamavalokayataḥ samayāḥ śapathācārakālasiddhāntasaṃvidaḥ iti viśvaḥ nijāvadhānamāha  mā veti asyāṃ mālatyāṃ tvayi ca yatpāpaṃ vivāhānirvāhe maraṇarūpaṃ śaṅkanīyaṃ viprayogajanyaduḥkhādi vā tacchatruṣvapi nāma prākāśye mā vābhūnmaiva bhaviṣyati vāśabda evārthe svakartavyamāha  taditi tasmāyuvayoḥ saṃbandhāya sarvaprakāreṇa jīvatyāgenāpi mayā prayatnaḥ kāryaḥ yadi buddhikauśalena na siddhistadā prāṇavyayenāpi sādhyamityapeḥ svarasaḥ maraṇāderamaṅgalatayā pāpapadenopanyāsaḥ śatruṣvapi mābhūditi lokokticchāyālaṅkāraḥ dayetyādi he bhagavati asmin śiśujane bālajane mādhave mālatyāṃ ca dayā karuṇā sneho mamatā ca saṃsārādviraktamapi bhagavatyāścittaṃ dravayatyākaroti bhavatyā iti dayādyanvayi cittānvayi ca kākākṣigolakavat vāśabdau cārthe ata eva cittadravaṇāt vratagrahaṇapūrvakasarvaiṣaṇānivṛttiḥ pravrajyā tasyāṃ sulabhaḥ avaśyaṃbhāvī samayācāronuṣṭānaviśeṣo dhyānādiviṣayastatra vimukho nirūddho yatnaste prasaktovicchinnaḥ san prabhavati ca evārthe kāryāsiddhiradṛṣṭavilambāt tatra na bhavatyā doṣa ityāha aparaṃ punardevaṃ prabhavati īśvarastrīṣu rājñīpadopacāreṇa bhaniītyuktam bharatopyāha  rājastriyastu saṃbhāṣyāḥ sarvāḥ parijanena tu bhaṭṭinī svāminī vāṃ sarva suṭhu tataśca samayasulabhā bhartrī vi yathā jadhā  gheūṇa āacchadu uttiṣṭhottiṣṭhacaturthoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥ svagatam kaṣṭametāvatī hi lokayātrā mālatyā samaṃ mādhavasya aho nu khalu bhoḥ suhṛdiva prakaṭayya sukhanaṃdaḥ prathamamekarasāmanukūlatām punarakāṇḍa vivartanadāruṇaḥ praviśināṣṭa vidhirmanaso rujam mālatī apaṃvārya mahābhāga locanānanda etāvaddṛṣṭosi mahābhāauṃ loaṇāṇanda ettiaṃ diṭhṭhosa lavahā dhik hā dhik śarīrasaṃśayameva naḥ priyasakhyāropitāmātyena haddhī haddhī sarīrasaṃsaaṃ jjevva ṇo piasahī ārovidā amacceṇa mālatī  svagatam pariṇatamidānīṃ me jīvitatṛṣṇāyāḥ phalam nirvyūḍhaṃ ca niṣkaruṇatayā tātasyāpi kāpālikatvam pariniṣṭhito duṣṭadaivasya dāruṇasamārambhasadṛśaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tatkamihopālabhe mandabhāginī kaṃ vāśaraṇā śaraṇaṃ pratipadye pariṇadaṃ dāṇiṃ me jīvitatihāe phalam ṇivvūḍhaṃ a ṇikkaruṇadāe tādassa vi kāvāliattaṇaṃ pairiṇihido dudeva dāruṇasamārambhasariso pariṇāmo tā kaṃ ettha uvālabhāmi mandabhāiṇī kaṃ vā asaraṇā saraṇaṃ parivajjāmi lava  sakhi ita itaḥsahi ido ido  iti kāmandakyā saha niṣkrāntetyevaṃ nāṭye prāhurvicakṣaṇāḥ  mādhavaḥ lokayātrā darśanādikam aho nu khalu bho ityavyayasamudāyo nirvede suhṛdityādi ekatraiva raso ratiryasyāstām yadvā eka eva rasaḥ śṛṅgāro yasyāṃ tām nirantarāṃ vānukūlatāmānukūlyaṃ prathamaṃ prakāśya sukhaprado vidhiḥ punarmanaso rujaṃ pīḍāṃ praviśinaṣṭayatiśayitāṃ karoti kīdṛśaḥ akāṇḍādakasmādvivartanenānyathābhāvena viruddhavartanena vā dāruṇo duḥkhadāyī suhṛdiva yathā mitramānukūlyamutpādya sukhapradaṃ sadakāṇḍa eva viruddhācaraṇānmanaḥpīḍāṃ karoti tathetyarthaḥ mālatī punadarśanaṃ na bhaviteti bhāvaḥ ata evaitāvadityanena karuṇā nayanānandetyanenānurāgaḥ mālatī atra purā virahadaśāyāṃ mādhavapraticchandakādidarśanāddhāritasya jīvitasya paryavasānaṃ vṛttamiti pariṇatapadasyārthaḥ kāpālikatvaṃ nṛśaṃsatā aghoraghaṇṭasya sūcanamapyetat mādhavaḥ janmasāphalyaṃ māla pradām svagatam  mahāṇubhāa ṇandakara paḍidi pratiṣṭhinaḥ   devvahadaassamālatīmāve mādhavaḥ  svagatam nūnamāśvāsanamātrametanmādhavasya sahajasnehakātarā karoti bhagavatī sodvegam hanta sarvathā saṃśayitajanmasāphalyaḥ saṃvṛttosmi tatkimidānīṃ kartavyam vicintya na khalu mahāmāṃsavikrayādainyamupāyaṃ paśyāmi prakāśam vayasya makaranda api bhavānutkaṇṭhate madayantikāyauḥ maka  atha kim tanme manaḥ kṣipati yatsarasaprahāramālokya māmagaṇitaskhaladuttarīyā trastaikahāyanakuraṅgaviloladṛṣṭirāśliṣṭavatyamṛtasaṃvalitairivāṅgaiḥ mādhavaḥ  sulabhaiva buddharakṣitāpriyasakhī bhavataḥ api ca pramathya kavyādaṃ maraṇasamaye rakṣitavataḥ pariṣvaṅgaṃ labdhvā tava kathamivānyatra ramatām tathā ca vyāpāraḥ kamalanayanāyā nayanayostvayi vyaktasnehastimitaramaṇīyaściramabhūt tīprāptyā mahāmāṃseti bhāvyaṅkasūcanam vīrahastānmāṃsaṃ gṛhītvā vīrāyābhimatavaradānamiti śmaśānasiddhayoginīmatam yadvā ubhayathā maraṇamupasthitam mahāmāṃsavikraye mālatīlābhopi śaṅkayata iti tatkaraṇam māṃsavikrayasya makarandasaṃnidhāvaśakyatvānmakarandaṃ madayantikāṃ pratyutkaṇṭhayati  vayasyeti madayantikāyāḥ kṛta iti śeṣaḥ yadvā adhīgartheti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭī makarandaḥ atha kiṃ svīkāre tanma ityādi tanmama cittaṃ harati yadetādṛśairaṅgairmāmāliṅgitavatī sarasaḥ saraktaḥ prahāro yatra tādṛśaṃ māmavalokya ata eva tvarayāgaṇitaṃ skhalat prabhraśyaduttarīyaṃ stanāvaraṇavāso yasyāḥ sā etena nirantarastanasparśaḥ sūcitaḥ ata evānandasaṃdohadāyitvādamṛtasiktairiva bhayavattvena trastaikavarṣīya hariṇasyeva cañcalā dṛṣṭiryasyāḥ sā varṣodo hāyanostrī syāt  ityamaraḥ mādhavaḥ trāsena tvadāliṅganaṃ na tu snehāditi śaṅkāpanodāya dūtīsulabhatayānurāgamevāhasulabheti pramathyetyādi sā tavāliṅganaṃ prāpyānyatra kathaṃ ramatām api tu naiva ivaśabdonavakṛptau kulīnaika māliṅgaya nānyatra ramata iti bhāvaḥ kīdṛśasya kravyamāmamāṃsamattīti kravyādvayāghraḥ taṃ vināśya maraṇakāle tāṃ anyadupāyāntaram kāyām sahasāpra rapā na durlabhā vadanāyāḥcaturthoṅkaḥ marka  taduttiṣṭha pārausindhusaṃbhedamavagāhya nagarīmeva praviśāvaḥ utthāya parikrāmataḥ mādhavaḥ  ayamasau mahānadyorvyatikaraiḥ ya eṣaḥ jalanibiḍitavastravyaktanimnonnatābhiḥ parigatataṭabhūmiḥ stronamātrotthitābhiḥ rucirakanakakumbhaśrīmadābhogatuṅgastanavinihitahastasvastikābhirvadhūbhiḥ iti niṣkrāntāḥ sarve iti śārdūlavibhramo nāma caturthoṅkaḥ rakṣitavataḥ etena kṛtopakāritoktā atopi nānyatra ramate padmākṣyāścakṣuṣostathā tena prakāreṇa tvayi vyāpāraca vyaktaḥ snehātstimito mandota eva ramaṇīyaściramabhūt rāgeṇa tayā sābhilāṣamālokitosīti bhāvaḥ etenānurāga uktaḥ yadāhānurāgaprakaraṇe  tuṣyatyasya kathābhistu sasnehaṃ ca nirīkṣate kravyamāmiṣamuddhāsam iti hārāvalī pārā ca sindhuśca maṇibandhanavinyastāvarālau strīprayojitau uttānau vāmapārśvasthau svastikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  arālaścaivam  ādyā dhanurlatākārā kuñcitoṅguṣṭakastathā śeṣā bhinnordhvavalitā arāleṅgulayaḥ kare  kanaketyādinā tāsāṃ gaurītvamuktam maṅgalakalaśānābhivaiṣāṃ darśaneneṣṭasiddhirapi sūcitā asūyaṃ ratnadharo dvijeśo dvijeśakanyā damayantikāpi jagaddharaṃ tatkṛtaṭippaṇeṅkogamaccaturtho rasarāśivāsaḥ iti caturthoṅkaḥ etannāsti kvacit varadā maka saṃbhedaḥ snāta pañcamoṅkaḥ tataḥ praviśatyākāśayānena bhīṣaṇojjvalaveśā kapālakuṇḍalā kapālakuṇḍalāṣaḍadhikadaśanāḍīcakra madhyasthitātmā hṛdi mahāmāṃsavikrayapratijñayā ca mādhavasya śmaśānapraveśe satyaṅkāvatāraḥ ākāśayānena praveśo yogasiddhisūcanāya bhīṣaṇā bhayaṃkarī ujjvalaveśā viśuddhaśarīrā etadapi yoginītvādeva ṣaḍadhiketyādi sa daśa nāḍyo hṛdvataikottaraśatasaṃkhyāsu tiryagūrdhvādhogata nāḍīṣu pradhānatamāstāsāṃ cakraṃ tasya madhye padmamadhyavartisūkṣmākāśadeśe prāṇādyādhāre sthita ātmā kūṭastho nityo yasya sa tathā tatra pramāṇam  āśiraḥśravaṇaṃ dehaṃ yadyapi vyāpya tiṣṭhati tathāpyasya paraṃ sthānaṃ hṛtpaṅkajasamudrakam iti sthitirapi tasya tatra paramātmatattvāvirbhāva eva yadvā ṣaḍbhiradhikā daśanāḍyaḥ ṣoḍaśasaṃkhyāstāsāṃ cakraṃ tatra madhye sthitaścāsāvātmā cātmasvarūpaḥ taduktam sarva śivamayaṃ matam iti yadvā ṣaḍadhikaṃ yaddaśanāḍīcakram matabhede jjvalā iyamahamidānīm pañcamoṅkaḥ nityaṃ nyastaṣaḍaṅgacakranihitaṃ hṛtpadmamadhyoditaṃ paśyantī śivarūpiṇaṃ layavaśādātmānamabhyāgatā nāḍīnāmudayakrameṇa jagataḥ pañcāmṛtākarṣaṇādaprāptotpatanaśramā vighaṭayantyagre nabhombhomucaḥ nityanya kapālakuṇḍalāyāḥ pūrvoktabhīṣaṇojjvalatvamupapādayati  ulloleti gaganatalagamanavego mayi sakalaṃ ramaṇīyaḍāmaratvaṃ ramaṇīyatvaṃ manoharatvaṃ ḍāmaratvaṃ bhīṣaṇatvamudbhaṭatvaṃ vā keolisaṃrambhanirbharatvaṃ vā saṃdhatte samartha kurute ḍāmaroḍḍāmarau bhīme kelisaṃrambhanirbhare  iti ratnakośaḥ vegabalādullālena yātāyātena skhalitā yā kapālānāṃ kaṇṭhavartinī mālā tasyāḥ saṃghakaṇitenānyonyakapālasaṃghṛṣṭidhvaninā karālā mūkā kṣudraghaṇṭikā yatra saḥ kapālamāloccadhvaninā tadbhuneraśravaṇānmūkatvamiva mūkatvam yadvā tathāvidhakkaṇitena karālā danturā viṣameti yāvat kiṅkiṇī yatra saḥ kulayoginīnāṃ kiṅkiṇyādidhvaninā sānandatvam yadāha   samudraghoṣasaṃbhārakiṅkiṇīghaṇṭikāsvanaiḥ sadānando bhavedyogī na nidrā na kṣudhā tṛṣā  iti tadevāha viṣvagiti jaṭānāṃ bhāraḥ samūho nibiḍaṃ dṛḍhaṃ yathā tathā granthibaddhopi viṣvagvṛttiḥ sarvatovyāpī san pracalati gaganagamanavegādityarthāt viṣvakśabdo nānārthaḥ suṣamādiṣu paṭhyate tena ṣatvam kṛtāvṛttiḥ kṛtagatāgatā kṛtamaṇḍalabhramaṇā khaṭṭāṅga sahitā ghaṇṭā saṃskāreṇa saṃtānena yaḥ kkāṇo dhvananaṃ tena dīrgha paṭu ramaṇīyaṃ ca yathā tathā raṭati śabdāyate etena ḍāmaratvamuktam khaṭṭāṅgaṃ vādyabhedaḥ vāyurūrdhva patākā dhūnoti kampayati dhūñ kampane dīrghāntaḥ svaratītyādisūtre nyāsakāraṇoktaḥ kīdṛśaḥ vivṛtāni yāni nirmāsatayā śavaśirāṃsi teṣāṃ śreṇayaḥ paṅkayastāsāṃ yāni kuñjani gahanāḥ pradeśāsteṣu guñjandhvanan ata evottāla udbhaṭadhvānaḥ kṣudaghaṇṭikānāmajasraraṇatkṛti udvṛtta udbhinna no patākāmpañcamoṅkaḥ parikramyāvalokya ca gandhamāghrāya idaṃ tāvatpurāṇanimbatailākta paribhṛ jyamānarasonaigandhibhiścitādhūmaiḥ purastādvibhāvitasya mahataḥ śmaśānavāṭasya nedīyaḥ karālāyatanaṃ yatra paryavasitamantrasādhanasyāsmadguroraghoraghaṇṭasyājñayā saviśeṣamadya pūjāsaṃbhāro mayā saṃnidhāpanīyaḥ kathitaṃ ca me guruṇāvatse kapālakuṇḍale adya bhagavatyāḥ karālāyāḥ prāgupayācitaṃ strīratnamupahartavyaṃ tatraiva nagare vimaste iti tadvicinomi sakautukamagrevalokya  tatkoyamatigambhīramadhurākṛtiruttambhitakuṭilakuntalaḥ kṛpāṇapāṇi śmaśānavāṭamavatarati ya eṣa kuvalayadalaśyāmopyaṅgaṃ dadhatparipāṇḍuraṃ lalitacaraṇanyāsaḥ śrīmānmṛgāṅkanibhānanaḥ harati vinayaṃ vāmo yasya prakāśitasāhasaḥ pravigaladasṛkpaṅkaḥ pāṇirlalannarajāṅgalaḥ hetuśca anena ramaṇīyatvamuktam nikkāṇo nikkaṇaḥ kkāṇaḥ kvaṇaḥ kvaṇanamityapi  ityamaraḥ yadvā paṭuraṭanena ramaṇīyatvaṃ patākākampanena ḍāmaratvamatroktam idaṃ tāvaditi purāṇetyādinā citādhūmānāṃ svabhāvākhyānam aktaṃ mrakṣitam paribharjanaṃ vahnimadhyanikṣepapākaḥ amlarasenaikenonaṃ pañcarasaṃ rasonam lasūna iti khyātam vaṭyate veṣṭyateneneti vāṭaḥ halaśceti ghañ  panthā vāṭaḥ patho māthaḥ iti bhāguriḥ nedīyo nikaṭam paryavasitaṃ samāptaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ ca mantrasādhanaṃ puraścaraṇajapādi saṃbhāraḥ samūhaḥ upayācitaṃ manīṣitārthaṃ svīkṛtam  yaddīyate tu devebhyo manorājyasya siddhaye upayācitakaṃ tattu dohadaṃ saṃpracakṣate  iti hārāvalī strīratnamiti jātau jātau yadutkṛṣṭaṃ taddhi ratnaṃ pracakṣate iti viśvaḥ viditamupalabdha vicitamiti pāṭhenviṣṭam gambhīretyādi  vikārāḥ sahajā yasya harṣakodhabhayādiṣu bhāveṣu nopalabhyante tadgāmbhīryamudāhṛtam  iti abhyāsātkaraṇānāṃ tu śliṣṭatvamupajāyate mahatsvapi vikāreṣu tanmādhuryamudāhṛtam  iti bharataḥ uttambhito juṭākāreṇa baddhaḥ kuṭilo vakraḥ kuntalaḥ keśo yasya saḥ etena raudrarasavattoktā kuvalayetyādi ya eṣa svabhāvānnīlanalinapatravacchayāmopi vipralambhātsarvataḥ pāṇḍuramaṅgaṃ dadhat lalito ramaṇīyo vikaṭo bhīṣaṇo nyāso dehanyāso yasya saḥ lalitatvaṃ svabhāvāt vikaṭatvaṃ raudrāt yadvā nyāsaḥ karacaraṇādicālanam śrīmānatiramyaḥ mṛgāṅkanniratiśayā bhā yatra tādṛśamānanaṃ yasya ata eva heyatvārthaṃ mṛgāṅkapadenopanyāsaḥ yasya vāmaḥ pāṇirvinayaṃ haratyapanayati atra hetumāha pravigaladasapaṅkaḥ sravadrudhirakardamaḥ rasonakarasa adhastāt hi adya mayā vicitaṃ kuntalabhāraḥ dhūsaram vikaṭa mālatīmādhave nirūpya aye sa eṣa kāmandakī suhṛtputro mahāmāṃsasya paṇāyitā mādhavaḥ tatkimanena bhavatu samīhitaṃ saṃpādayāmi vigalitaprāyaiḥ paścimasaṃdhyāsamayaḥ tathā hi saṃprati vyomnastāpicchagucchāvalibhiriva tamovallarībhivriyante paryantāḥ prāntavṛtyā payasi vasumatī nūtane majjatīva vātyāsaṃveṃga viṣvagvitatavalayitasphītadhūmyāprakāśaṃ prārambhepi triyāmā taruṇayati nijaṃ nīlimānaṃ vaneṣu parikramya niṣkrāntā viṣkambhakaḥ tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭo mādhavaḥ mādhavaḥ  sāśaṃsam premāḥ praṇayaspṛśaḥ paricayādudgāḍharāgodayāstāstā mugdhadṛśo nisargamadhurāśceṣṭā bhaveyurmayi yāsvantaḥkaraṇasya bāhyakaraṇavyāpārarodhī kṣaṇādāṃśaṃsāparikalpitāsvapi bhavatyānandasāndro layaḥ lalañcañcalaṃ narajāṅgalaṃ mahāmāṃsaṃ yatra saḥ nahi vinīto raktaṃ mahāmāṃsaṃ ca dhārayati atra pūrvārdhena lalitatvamuttarārdhena vikaṭatvamuktam ata eva vyaktasāhasaḥ mahāmāṃsadhāritvena vīrabībhatsarasāvuktau yadāha   utsāhādhyavasāyādvismayaharṣācca mohācca vividhādgandhīvaśeṣādvīraraso nāma saṃbhavati anabhimatadarśanena ca gandharasasparśaśabdadoṣaiśca uttejanaiśca bahubhibabhatsarasaḥ samudbhavati  dadhadityatra nābhyastācchaturiti numo niṣedhaḥ jāṅgalaṃ nirjanasthāne triliṅgayāṃ piśitestriyām  iti medinī karaḥ paṇāyitā vikretā vigalitaprāyo bhraṣṭaprāyaḥ vyomna ityādi gaganasyopāntā dhvāntalatābhirvyāpyante tamālapuṣpastabakapatibhiriva evaṃ ca pṛthivyu pāntabhāgena nūtane jale majjatīva utprekṣeyam triyāmā rātriḥ prārambhe pradoṣamātrepi nīlatvaṃ nijaṃ vaneṣu taruṇayati kīdṛśam vātānāṃ samūhā vātyā tasyāḥ saṃvegena vivartanena viṣvak caturdiśaṃ vitatā vistāritā valayiṃtā valayākārā sphītā gabhīrā yā dhūmyā dhūmasamūho nīhāro vā tatsadṛśam evaṃ cāndhakāropagamādgataprāyā saṃdhyetyarthaḥ  dhūmyā dhūmasamūhepi nīhārapi nigadyate  iti dharaṇiḥ sāśaṃsaṃ saprārthanam premetyādi mugdhadṛśo mālatyāstāstā anubhūtāśceṣṭāḥ saṃbhoge cumbanādayo mayi punarbhūyāsuḥ  ceṣṭāviśeṣāḥ saṃbhoge cumbanāliṅganādayaḥ iti yathāsamī prāyaśca śriyante saṃgena vilasita śuddhavi viṣaya āśaṃkā sāndrodayaḥkiṃ ca pañcamoṅkaḥ atimuktaṃmaddrathitakesarāvalīsatatādhivāsasubhagārpitastanam api karṇajāhaviniveśitānanaṃ priyayā tadaṅgaṃ parivartamānuyām atha vā dūre tāvadetat idame prārthaye saṃbhūyeva sukhāni cetasi paraṃ bhūmānamātanvate yatrālokapathāvatāriṇa ratiṃ prastauti netrotsavaḥ yadvālendgukaloccayaāvacitaiḥ sārairivotpāditaṃ tatpaśyeyamanaṅgamaṅgalagṛhaṃ bhūyopi tasyā mukham kaṇṭhābharaṇam kīdṛśyaḥ prathamaṃ premṇā saṃbhogaprītyā iva tāpaśāntiheturomāñcādijanakatvāt tato viśvāsamupetya cittaprasādaspṛśaḥ tataḥ paricayātsukhāstrādabhedādudbhaṭarāgodrekāḥ nisargamadhurāḥ sahajamanojñāḥ yāsvāśaṃsopanītāsvapi kṣaṇānniratiśayasukhaghano layo līnatā bhavati tāsu ceṣṭāsu mano līyata ityarthaḥ kīdṛśaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya manaso bāhyendriyavyāpārāvarodhanaśīlaḥ mālatīmayatvena manmano bāhyaviṣaye na vyāpriyata ityarthaḥ ata evānekaśaṅkātaṅka saṃkulepi tatra sthāne mādhavasya na sādhvasādikamapīti bhāvaḥ yadvā tāstāceṣṭā bakulavathyādipu yāstayā kṛtāstāstā mayi bhaveyuḥ tāsāmeva durlabhatvādāśaṃsanīyatā prathamaprītihetutvadāliṅganamāśāste  atimuktetyādi priyayā saha tadaṅka pariva ttimapyahamāpnuyām tattasyā aṅke koḍe sarvatobhāvena vartanam hṛdayāliṅganamityarthaḥ āpārbhainnakramaḥ yadvā tadaṅke parivartanamūrdhvādhaḥkrameṇa puruṣāyitamāpnuyām kīdṛśaḥ priyayā karṇajāhe karṇamūle viniveśitamānanaṃ yatra mamāpi saḥ prathamapakṣe karṇa mūlerpitamānanaṃ yena saḥ tasya pākamūle pīlvādikarṇādibhyaḥ kuṇavjāhacau  iti mūle jāhacpratyayaḥ atikrāntā muktā yayā sātimuktā muktāhāramapāsya tadarpaṇādatikramaḥ yadvā atimuktātiviralā mālatyavalokanavyāsaṅgāt etādṛśī yā madrathitā kesarāvalī tasyāḥ satatādhivāsena subhagaḥ surabhirarpitaḥ stano yatreti kriyāviśeṣaṇam avimukteti pāṭho na manoharaḥ aviyuktatvādeva satatādhivāsasya labdhatvātsatatagrahaṇasya vyarthatvāt saṃbhūyetyādi tasyāstanmukhaṃ punarapi paśyeyamityetadeva prārthaye aṅka prāpterdurlabhatvāditi bhāvaḥ kīdṛśam kāmasya maṅgalārtha gṛham tatra kāmo hṛṣṭo vasatītyarthaḥ yadvā kāmasya maṅgalaghaṭitaṃ hiraṇyaghaṭitaṃ gṛham kalyāṇaṃ maṅgalaṃ vidyātkāñcanaṃ ca tadakṣamam  iti viśvaḥ yadvā anaṅgasya maṅgalānāmupacayahetūnāṃ saukumāryādīnāṃ gṛham ata evotprekṣate bā takagra mudrathita kaṇṭa nanaḥ daṅka parivṛttiṃ meva tāvat kalodayātḥ dupacitaiḥ  vāsāditaṃ  mālatīmādhave na viśeṣaḥ mama hi saṃprati yatsatyamardhunā tatsaṃdarśanenātisvalpopi sātiśayaprāktanopalambhasaṃbhāvitātmajanmanaḥ saṃskārasyānavarataprabodhātpratāyamānastadvisadṛśapratyayāntarairatiraskṛtapravāhaḥ priyatamāsmṛtipratyayotpattisaṃtānastanmayamiva karotyantarvṛttisārūpyataścaitanyam tathā hi līneva pratibimbiteva likhitevotkīrṇarūpeva ca pratyupteva ca vajralepaghaṭitevāntarnikhāteva ca lacandrakalodayādgṛhītaiḥ sāraistpāditamiti atrodayāditi bhāvena dravyābhidhānānnavendukalāyā avacitāḥ sārāstairutpāditamivetyarthaḥ sakalajanānāndinavenduka lātopyadhikamanoharamiti bhāvaḥ yadvā lyablope pañcamī tena bālendukalodayaṃ prāpyāvacitairityarthaḥ yadvā bālendukalodayātpratipaccandrakalodayādārabhyāvacitaiḥ pūrṇimāparyantamityarthāt ārabhyetyasya lābhaḥ pañcamīta eva tathā ca pūrṇendunā mukhasāmyaṃ labhyate kvacitkaloccayāditi pāṭhaḥ tatroccayātsamūhādityarthaḥ yatra mukhe saṃmukhībhūte sukhāni kartṝṇi militveva paraṃ bhūmānaṃ bāhulyaṃ vistārayanti citte anenāntaḥprītiruktā ivaśabda utprekṣāyām evapāṭhe vismaya evaśabdaḥ bahiḥprītimāhanetrotsavolabvalābhābhimānonurāgaṃ prastauti sravati ratedrevamayotvāt samādhiralaṅkāraḥ mānasamautsukyātiśayamāha  mama hīti sāmakīnaḥ priyāsmaraṇarūpajñānotpatteḥ saṃtānaḥ pariṇatisamūhaḥ smṛtirūpa eva mama caitanyamātmatattvaṃ tanmayamiva karoti mālatīmayaṃ karotītyarthaḥ kīdṛśaḥ pratāya māno dīrghabhavan atra hetuḥ saṃskārasya bhāvanāyā atiśayitaprabodhādudrekāt kīdṛśasya saṃskārasya sātiśayātsādarāsphuṭākārādvā bakulavīthyāṃ pūrvakālānubhapratāyamānatvamevopapādayatitadvisadṛśairmālatīvilakṣaṇaviṣayairjñānāntarairatiraskṛtapravṛttiḥ tathā cāntarā viṣayāntarāsphuraṇānna pravāhatiraskāra iti bhāvaḥ nanvātmatattvasya puṣkarapalāśavannirlepatayā kathaṃ mālatīmayatvamata āha  antariti antaḥpadamiha buddhitattvaparam tathā ca buddhitattvasya yā pravṛttiḥ sahajasiddho vyāpāraḥ sā yata ātmatattve bhedāgrahātpratibhāsate tasmāt sāṃkhyadarśane buderbhoktṛtvāt yadvā antarvṛttiriti bhāvapradhānam tathā cāntavṛttitvamantaravasthānarūpaṃ sādṛśyamātmabuddhyo stasmāt svoktameva līnevetyādi sā priyāsmākaṃ cetasi lagnā saṃbaddhā saṃbaddhatve yathāsaṃbhavaṃ prakārānāhalīneva nihnuteva yatra yasya saṃbaddhasya na pratyakṣopalambhastatra tallīnamityucyate yathā payasi līnaṃ lavaṇam sarvatrātra lagnatvasya prakārabhedevāllavdhajanmanaḥ darśayati prabodhanāt pratā  adhunā saṃdarśanaṃ neti svalpopi viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvitātmanaḥ pratīya visadṛśaiḥ prabhāva karoti vṛtti lekha pañcamoṅkaḥ sā naścetasi kīliteva viśikhaiścetobhuvaḥ pañcabhi cintāsaṃtatitantujālanibiḍasyūteva lagnā priyā nopamābhedaḥ pūrvapūrvāparitoṣādvā tathā hi līnatvasyāpratibhāsātspaṣṭapratibhāsārthamāhapratibimbiteva yatra svacchadravyābhihataṃ cakṣuḥ parivṛtya dravyāntaraṃ gṛhṇāti tattatra pratibimbitamityucyate yathā sphaṭike raktapuṣpam praticchāyāyā vastvantarasaṃsargādhīnatvenāsāhajikatvātsāhajikatvopavarṇanāyāha  likhiteva yatpraśithilāvayavasaṃyogāśrayeṇa dravyeṇa ghanadravyopari saṃsthānaviśeṣavannirmīyate tattatra likhitamityucyate yathā patre lipiḥ likhitasya jalāyupanipātavināśitayā na cirasthāyitvamatastadarthamāha  utkīrṇarūpeva yadyatra nibiḍadravye tādṛśena kiñcidavayavavibhāgaḥ kriyate tattatrotkarṇim yathā ṭaḍkādinā śilādi asyāpyekabhāgavṛttitayā sarvavṛttitvārthamāha   pratyupteva pratyuptamardharopitam yadyatra dravyāntarasaṃsargi tattatra pratyuptam yathāgulīyake maṇyādi asyāpi śakyoddhāratvānnibiḍasaṃbandhāyāha   vajralepaghaṭiteva yadyatra kiṃciddhanadravyābhighātajanyakarmajanyasaṃyogavibhāgānā śrayi tattatra vajralepaghaṭitam yathā hīrakādi tathāpi lepasya bahirvṛttitvādantaḥsaṃsargārthamāha antarnikhāteva yadyatra saṃbaddhamūrdhvādhaḥ saṃyogādinā dhṛtaṃ nopalabhyate tattatra nikhātamucyate yathā bhūmau mūlakādi nikhātatvaṃ sarva ropaṇamuptatvamardharopaṇamityanayorbhedaḥ nikhātasyāpi nirbandhātiśayena śakyoddhāratayā vive kādiduḥśakyatvārthamāhakāmasya pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ kīliteva kīlitasya pratikīlanoddhārthatayāśakyonmūlanāyāha  cintāparamparā sūtrasamūhena gāḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā syūteva sīvanaṃ prāpiteva jālanibiḍasīvanenānucchedanīyatvamuktam ihopadheyābhedepyupādhibhedādapaunaruktyamityavadheyam ekameva hi vastu tattadupādhivaiśiṣṭyādbhinna buddhiviṣayo yathā daṇḍikuṇḍalitvādi yadvā nosmākaṃ cetasi sā lagnā dṛḍhaṃ saṃbaddhā dṛḍhasaṃbaddha eva lagnapadārthaḥ  śaro lagnaḥ  ityādau tathādarśanāt dṛḍhasaṃbaddha eva nānāprakāreṇa sthirīkriyate kāmabāṇapañcakena kīliteva cintāpravāharūpatantusaṃtatyā syūteva nanu dvayamapyado na yuktam tayā sahāntarasya caitanyasya saṃbandhābhāvāt ato viṣayaviṣayiṇāstadātmarūpa eva saṃbandha iti yogācāramatamanenoktam pratibimbiteveti sāṃkhyamatopadarśanam likhiteveti sautrāntikamatopadarśanam tatra hi jñānena svīyākārārpaṇaṃ viṣaye kriyata iti tattadākārasyābhivyaktiḥ śilādau turaṃgādivaditi likhanasāmyam utkīrṇarūpeveti viṣayākāreṇa caitanyapariṇāma ihotkīrṇarūpatā atastridaṇḍimatam pratyupteveti pūrvarūpatirodhānādanyarūpāvirbhāvena suvarṇaracitabhājanādāviva tattadviṣayākāratayā jñānavipariṇāma iti pātañjalamatam vajralepaghaṭitevati naiyāyikamatam tadīyamātrarūpo hi svabhāvabhedaḥ prakāśasya viṣayaviṣayibhāvaḥ ayaṃ ca yāvadvastusthiratayā vajralepaghaṭanāto na bhiyate antarnimālatīmādhave nepathye kalakalaḥ mādhavaḥ ākarṇya aho saṃprati pragalbhamānakauṇapanikāyasya mahatī śmaśānavāṭasya raudratā asmin hi paryantapratirodhimeduracayaṃstyānaṃ citājyotiṣāmaujjvalyaṃ parabhāgataḥ prakaṭayatyābhogabhīmaṃ tamaḥ saṃsaktākulakelayaḥ kilakilākolāhalaiḥ saṃmadāduttālāḥ kaṭapūtanāprabhṛtayaḥ sāṃrāviṇaṃ kurvate khāteveti vijñānavādimatopadarśanam atra hi vijñānasyāntarnikhananānna bāhyavastusthitiriti ihāpi tathā ete ca viṣayaviṣayibhāvavikalpāstaccintā prakāratvānmādhavasya citte viparivartante evaṃ ca cetasā saha saṃbandhaḥ pañcātkīlanena vā sīvanena vā gāḍhasaṃbaddhatāṃ gatā bhavati lagnā tataśca taddarśanaṃ mahāpuruṣānubhūtaṃ tasyeti kimatra citramiti bhāvaḥ atra pañcabhirityanena yugapatkāmabāṇaviṣayatvamātmano nivedayatā duḥsahadaśāśālitvaṃ sūcitam cetobhuva ityanena tatprabhavasya tasya kauśikaghaṭānāṃ ghūtkārarūpaṃ saṃvalgitaṃ dhvanitam ṛndacchṛgālānāṃ ḍātkṛtirḍātkāraḥ śabdaviśeṣaḥ anayoḥ tābhyāṃ bhṛtaḥ pūrito yaḥ prāgbhā rogrataṭaṃ tena bhīṣaṇastaṭairlakṣitā lakṣaṇe tṛtīyā antarabhyatare śīrṇākhuṭitā ye karaṅkāḥ kapālāni teṣāṃ karkaro bhagnāvayavaḥ kākara  iti prasiddho vā karkaro yatra ata eva taratāṃ saṃtaraṇaśīlānāṃ saṃrodhyavarodhakaḥ kūlaṅkaṣaḥ kūlavidārako  yaḥ srotonirgamastena ghoro ghargharovyaktarūpo ravaḥ śabdo yatra sā taraḥsaṃrodhīti pāṭhe tarasā vegena saṃrodha gamanavirodhi karkareṇa dṛḍhena tarasā saṃrodhītyarthaḥ alpā kuṭī kuṭīraḥ syāt  ityamaraḥ ghaṭāśabdaḥ samūhamātravacanopi karighaṭādau tvātyāntikastasya prayoga ityavadheyam ghūtkāraḍātkṛtī anukaraṇaśabdau kvacit phātkṛtīti pāṭhaḥ tatrāpi phātkṛtiranukaraṇaśabda eva pherupheravajambukāḥ ityamaraḥ  taṭaḥ prāgbhāra ityapi  ityamaraḥ karkaro bhagnabhāgepi dṛḍhepi khaṇḍitepi ca  iti dharaṇiḥ tadiha karaṅkakarkarasaṃkulanadīpravāhastīraṃ pātayati ghargharavaṃ ca kuruta iti sphuṭameva nepathye hā tāta ityatra drāgatipra nāmātibhīṣaṇa vikāraiḥ niḥsattvāḥ sarve eṣa sarva saṃvellita saṃvargita saṃvardhita dhātkṛti kīrṇa karpara taraḥsaṃ  taratsaṃ ṭī  mālatīmādhave jano vipadyate hā tāda ṇikkaruṇa eso dāṇiṃ de ṇarendacitārāhaṇovaaraṇaṃ jaṇo vipai mādhavaḥ  sākūtamākarṇya nādastāvadvikalakurarīkūjitasnigdhatāracittākarṣī paricita iva śrotrasaṃvāda meti antarbhinnaṃ bhramati hṛdayaṃ vihvalatyaṅgamaṅga derhastambhaḥ skhalayati gatiṃ kaḥ prakāraḥ kimetat karālāyatanāccāyamuccarankaruṇo dhvaniḥ vibhāvyate nanu sthānamaniṣṭānāṃ tadīdṛśam bhavatu paśyāmi iti parikrāmati tataḥ praviśato devatārcanavyagrau mālatī ca kapālakuṇḍalāghoraghaṇṭau kṛtavadhyacihnā mālatī  hā tāta niṣkaraṇa eṣa idānīṃ te narendracittārādhahāyogepi na dvitīyā hāśabdasya śokavācina upagrahāt tasya ca saṃbodhane prathamāprayogāt tadanyārthasya yoge dvitīyeti nyāsaḥ aṅkamukhe strīratnāpahārasya sūcitatvānnepathye bhaṇanamidam nāda ityādi ayaṃ tāvannādaḥ śrotrayoḥ saṃvādaṃ pūrvopalambhākāratāmeti kīdṛśaḥ vikalā trastā yā kurarī  hāpūtī iti prasiddhā pakṣivadhūstasyāḥ kūjitavatsnigdhaḥ snehalastāra uccaśca trāsānmālatyāstāro nādaḥ ata eva cittākarṣī priyatvāccittānukarṣakaḥ paricita iva pūrvamupalabdha iva ata eva śrotrasaṃvāditāsya paricayaśca śaṅkaragṛhe vṛttaḥ yadi śrotrasaṃvādameti kathaṃ tīṃvakāra ityata āha antarbhinnaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ saṃśayākrāntaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhramati dolāyate ubhayata ākarṣāt atra mālatīgamanāsaṃbhavātsaṃvādasya ca sphuṭatvāt yadvā antarbhinnaṃ viddhamamasaṃbhavenetyarthāt tathā bandhugatāniṣṭaśaṅkākalaṅkātpratyaṅgaṃ vihvalati karādīni kampanta ityarthaḥ tasyāḥ kathamihāvasthānamiti bhayāddehastambhaḥ yadāha   harṣavyādhitrāsaroṣādyaiḥ stambhaḥ saṃbhavati cintāstimitatvādgatiśca skhalati kathamakasmādeva mamedaṃ vṛttamiti vimarśamāha  koyaṃ prakāraḥ kiṃnimittaṃ snehamāviṣkaroti kimetat saiveyaṃ kimanyadvā tattulyamityarthaḥ saṃbādhamiti pāṭhe karṇapīḍāṃ karotītyarthaḥ nādaśrutyā mohāt karāletyādi ayamutthitakaruṇaraso dhvaniḥ kathaṃ vā saṃbhāvyata ityanvayaḥ uccarannuttiṣṭhan vitarkasaṃpraghāraṇamāha  nanviti nanu saṃbhāvanāyām īdṛśāṃ saṃbhāvyamānajātīyānā maniṣṭānāṃ janavadhānāmidaṃ karālāyatanaṃ sthānamiti saṃbhāvyate vadhyacihnaṃ nyastālaktaketyādi vāvajjai gātra dehorakampa  karuṇadhva īdṛśam devārca rcanā  pañcamoṅkaḥ nopakaraṇaṃ jano vipadyate hā amba snehamayahṛdaye hatāsi daivadurvilasitena hā mālatīmayajīvite mama kalyāṇasādhanaikamuktasakalavyāpāre bhagavati cirasya jñāpitāsi duḥkhaṃ snehena hā priyasakhi lavaṅgike svapnāvasaramātradarśanāhaṃ te saṃvṛttā hā tāda ṇikkaruṇa aiso dāṇiṃ de ṇarendacittārāhaṇovaaraṇaṃ jaṇo vipajjai hā amba siṇehamaahiae hadāsi devvaiduvvilasidenahā māladīmaajīvide maha kallāṇasāhakka mukkasaalavvāvāre bhaavadi cirassa jāṇāvidāsi dukkhaṃ siṇeheṇa hā piasahi lavabhie siviṇaavasaramettadasaṇā ahaṃ de saṃtā mādhavaḥ  hantai saiveyaṃ hariṇekṣaṇā saṃpreti nirasta evaṃ saṃdehaḥ tadapi nāmaināṃ jīvantīṃ saṃbhavaye tvaritaṃ parikāmati kāpālikā  devi cāmuṇḍe namaste namaste sāvaṣṭambhāniśumbhasaṃbhramanamagolaniṣpīḍananyañcatkarpara kūrmakampavigaladbrahmāṇḍakhaṇḍasthiti pātālapratimallagallavivaraprakṣiptasaptārṇavaṃ vande nanditanīlakaṇṭhapariṣadyaktaddhiṃ vaḥ krīḍitam api ca pracalitakarikṛttiparyantacañcannakhāghātabhinnenduniḥ syandamānāmṛtaśyota jīvatkapālāvalīmukta caṇḍāṭṭahāsatra sadbhūribhūtapravṛttastuti mālatī atra bhagavati kāmandaki iti śeṣaḥ cirasya bahukālam ekaśubhasthāne ekamukhamiti pāṭha ekamukhamekavākyatāpannam mādhavaḥ hanteti niścayalābhe kāpālikau sāvaṣṭambhetyādi devi yuṣmākaṃ krīḍitaṃ nṛtyaṃ vande kīdṛśam sāṭopo yo niśumbho nirdayayantraṇaṃ karaṇabhedastataḥ saṃbhramādānamato bhūgolasyāvanicakrasya niṣpīḍanena nyañcadadhogacchat karparaṃ pṛṣṭhāsthi yasya kūrmasya tasya kampenāṅga cālanena vigalantī bhraśyantī brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍasya sthitiryatra tattathā anena bhūkampa uktaḥ tathā ca namrībhūtabhūgole tvarṇavānāmutsekātpātālatulyagallavivare prakṣiptāḥ saptārṇavā yatra tat nanditabhairavasabhaṃ ca prakaṭavibhavam utkṣiptā tu bhavetpāṇirniśumbhoyaṃ nigadyate aḍgulyogrāñcitāḥ sarvāḥ pādāgratalasaṃcare  iti bharataḥ kaṭāhe ca kapālepi pṛṣṭāsthani ca karparaḥ  iti śāśvataḥ nāṭyeśvarīvarṇanamidam daṇḍakamāha  praca litetyādi devi yuṣmākaṃ tāṇḍavamuddhataṃ nṛtyamasmākamabhīṣṭyā aśubhanāśāya tuṣṭayā mātaḥ duvvāradevva ṇekkasaha śubha madire  hanna saṃprati  eva me tadahamapi saṃbhāvayeyamiti jhaṭiti cāmuṇḍe bhagavati nirbhara vyaktaṃ tava aghora mālatīmāghave śvasadasitabhujaṅgabhogāṅgadagranthiniṣpīḍenasphāraphullatphaṇāpīṭhaniryadviṣajyotirujjṛmbhaṇoḍḍāmaravyastaivistāridoḥkhaṇḍaparyāsitakṣmādharam jvaladanala piśaṅkanetracchaṭāsauṭabhī mottamāṅgabhramiprastutālātacakrakriyāsyūtadigbhāgamuttuṅgakhadāṅgakoṭiṃdhvajodbhūtivikṣiptatārāgaṇaṃ pramuditakaṭapūtanottālavetālatālasphuṭatkarṇasaṃbhrāntagorīghanāśleṣahṛṣyanmanatrayambakānandi vastāṇḍavaṃ devi bhūyādabhīṣṭeyai ca hṛṣṭayai ca naḥ ityabhinayataḥ ānandāya ca bhūyāt ariṣṭyā iti pāṭhe riṣṭiraśubhaṃ tadabhāvoriṣṭistasyai anena bhāvyaniṣṭārthasūcakadaṇḍopyuktaḥ yadāha   ākasmikasaṃbaddhaṃ samarthamiva yadbhavet vācāmante sa daṇḍaḥ syādbhāvyaniṣṭārthasūcakaḥ riṣṭiḥ khaḍne nāśubhe strī  iti medinīkaraḥ ariṣṭe tu śubhāśubhe  ityamaraḥ yadvā ṛkāro devamātā syāt  iti kośādṛśabdātsaṃbuddhau guṇe ca he aḥ devamātaḥ iṣṭyā abhīṣṭyai bhūyādityarthaḥ kīdṛśam pracalitagajāsuracarmaparyanteṣūnamatāṃ nakhānāmāghātairbhinnātsphuṭitāddevīmastakasthacandrātkṣaradamṛtasya śyotenāplavena jīvantībhiḥ kapālāvalibhirmuṇḍamālābhirmuktaiścaṇḍāgṛhāsairatyucca hasanaistrasatāṃ bahubhūtagaṇānāṃ pravṛttā stutiryatra yadvā bhūtagaṇaiḥ pravṛttā pravartitā stutiryatra tat antarbhāvitaṇyarthaḥ yadvā pracalitaḥ karicarmarūpovaviryatra tat paścātkarmadhārayaḥ tathā tāṇḍavāḍambarāyāsena śvasatāṃ śyāmasarpāṇāṃ kāyairye keyūrākāragranthayasteṣu niṣpīḍanenotphāla udgata mukhavikāsastaralo vā phullanvistāritāṅgacayaḥ phaṇāpīṭhaḥ vistāritayā pīṭhena rūpakam tato nirgataviṣāgnerujjṛmbhaṇenādhikyenoḍḍāmaraḥ kelisaṃvasturasātiśayo bhayaṃkaro vā viṣamo vā vyasta itastatogāmī vistārī dīrghau yo doḥkhaṇḍa samūhastena paryāsitaḥ kṣiptaḥ parvato yatra tat devyā anekabāhuśālitayā doḥkhaṇḍa ityuktam abjādikadambe khaṇḍamastriyām ityamaraḥ tathā jvalatānalena piṅgalaṃ yannetraṃ lalāṭalocanaṃ tasya cchaṭā jvālānirgamaprasarastasya  sāṭena vistāreṇa bhīmaṃ yaduttamāṅgaṃ śirastasya bhramirmaṇḍalākāreṇa bhramaṇaṃ tayā prastutā prārabdhālātacakrakriyā vahniprajvalitārdhakāṣṭhaviśeṣakarma tayā syūtā ivaikatra pratibaddhā iva digbhāgā yatra tat tathātimahā khaṭṭāṅgāgradhvajotkampādvikṣipta itastatastārāpraṇo yatra tat tathā hṛṣṭakaṭapūtanodbhaṭavetālānāṃ tālena kalakalena sphuṭatkarṇāta eva saṃbhrāntā trasantī satvarā vā gaurī tasyā nibiḍāliṅganena hṛṣyaccittaṃ tryambakaṃ śivamatyarthaḥ mānandayati iti ābhīkṣṇye ṇiniḥ sāṭo nikuñje vistāre iti viśvaḥ śṛṅgamagre ḍitotphāla notphulla vyakta vistāra cchanna bhāra sāra piśaṅgarikhajjaṭājūṭa bhīmo śṛṅgadhva dariṣṭyaipañcamoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥ  vilokya hā dhik pramādaḥ nyastālakta karaktamālyavasanā pākhaṇḍacaṇḍālayoḥ pāpārambhavatormṛgīva vṛkayorbhīrurgatā gocaram seyaṃ bhūrivasorvasoriva sutā mṛtyormukhe vartate hā dhikkaṣṭamaniṣṭamastakaruṇaḥ koyaṃ vidheḥ prakramaḥ kapālakuṇḍalā taṃ bhadre smara dayitotra yastavābhūdadya tvāṃ tvarayati dāruṇaḥ kṛtāntaḥ mālatī hā yi mādhava paralokagatopi yuṣmābhiḥ smartavyoyaṃ janaḥ na khalu sa uparato yasya vallabho janaḥ smarati hā daṃīa māhava paraloagado vi sumaridavvo tumahiṃ aaṃ jaṇo ṇa hu so uvarado jassa vallaho jaṇo sumaredi pi kīrtitam iti śāśvataḥ mādhavaḥ dhik pramāda ityatra vartata iti kriyādhyāhāraḥ tata upapadavibhakteḥ kāraka vibhaktirbalīyasīti dhigyoge dvitīyāṃ bādhitvā prathametyavadheyam nyastetyādi seyaṃ bhūrivasoḥ sutā yasyāḥ kṛte mayaivaṃ duḥkhamanubhūyate pākhaṇḍacaṇḍālayorgocaraṃ saṃmukhaṃ gatā pākhaṇḍeṣu caṇḍālosau taddarśanavirūddhakriyākāritvāt yadāha   na bhuñjītārkapatreṣu strībālaṃ naiva ghātayet yadvā pākhaṇḍau ca tau caṇḍālau ca niṣiddhakriyatvāt yadāha  avadhyāstu sadākhyātāḥ sarvayonigatāḥ striyaḥ  caṇḍālatvādeva pāpārambhavatormāraṇapravṛttayoḥ nyaste alaktakarakte mālyavasane yasyāṃ sā etadvadhyacihnam yathā mṛgī vṛkayoḥ saṃmukhaṃ gatā tatheyaṃ bhīruḥ mṛgītyanena bhayacalanetratoktā vasordevatābhedasya etenāsya sukhitvamuktam mṛtyoryamasya mukhe vartate ata eva hāśabdaḥ paridevite strīratnamapi vadhyata iti nindāyāṃ dhigiti vi ṣāde kaṣṭam kopeniṣṭam astā naṣṭā karuṇā dayā yatra etādṛśo vidherārambhaḥ koyam ninditoyam kīdṛgvā  kiṃ vitarke paripraśne kṣepe nindāprakārayoḥ  iti viśvaḥ karuṇoyaṃ rasaḥ  iṣṭavadhadarśanādvā karuṇaraso nāma saṃbhavati  iti bharataḥ caṇḍālopi ca cāṇḍālaḥ  iti śabdabhedaḥ puṣpapuṣpasrajau mālyam ityamaraḥ taṃ bhadra ityādi praharṣiṇīcchandasā ślokārdham cāmuṇḍe bhagavatītyādyagrimārdham he bhadre yastava dayito vallabhatveneṣṭastaṃ smara gurutvātsmaraṇamasya yadāha   patireko guruḥ strīṇām iti yadvā madupaharaṇīyatvena sa iha janmani te vallabho na bhūta eva ato janmāntarepi tallābhāya taṃ smara yadāha   yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaranbhāvaṃ tyajatyante kalevaram taṃ tamevaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ  iti kṛtānto yamaḥ mālatī pāṣaṇḍa  khaṇḍi kayoḥ mariṣṭa tvaṃ ṇāha daiaṇāi mālatīmādhave kapāla  hanta mādhavānurakteyaṃ tapasvinī aghoraghaṇṭaḥ  śastraimudyamya yadastu tadastu vyāpādayāmi cāmuṇḍe bhagavati mantrasādhanādāvuddiṣṭāmupanihitāṃ bhajasva pūjām iti hantumupakrāntaḥ mādhavaḥ  sahasopasṛtya apehi pratihatosi kāpālikāpasada mālatī sahasavalokya paritrāyatāṃ paritrāyatāṃ mahābhāgaḥ parittāadu paritāadu mahābhāo iti mādhavamāliṅgati mādhavaḥ  mahābhāge na bhetavyaṃ na bhetavyam maraṇasamaye tyaktvā śaṅkāṃ pralāpaniraṃgalaṃ prakaṭitanijasnehaḥ soyaṃ sakhā pura eva te sutanu visṛjotkampaṃ saṃpratyasāviha pāpmanaḥ phalamanubhavatyugraṃ pāpaḥ pratīpavipākinaḥ smaraṇaphalamāhayasyetyatrādhīgartheti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭī yasya guṇamiti vā antakāle mādhavasmaraṇaṃ muktiheturiti kaṭākṣitam kapālakuṇḍalā hanta khede kāmandakīmitraputratvānmamāpi mādhavastādṛśa eva tadanuraktā ceyaṃ kathaṃ vadhyeti kheda iti bhāvaḥ ata eva tapasvinyanukampyā aghoraghaṇṭaḥ uddiṣṭāṃ vācā pratijñātām upanihitāmupaḍhaukitām mādhavaḥ kaphoṇeradhobhāgo maṇibandhaparyantaḥ prakoṣṭaḥ vikṣipyāpasārya khaḍgahastatvena bāhumadhyepasāraṇaṃ jāti pratihato nirākṛtaḥ apasada nindita maraṇetyādi soyaṃ tava mitraṃ purata eva vartata ityākṣepāt yo bakulavīthyādiṣu sānurāgadarśanaprasannayā tvayā svīkṛtaḥ maraṇasamaya ityanenānurāga uktaḥ yadāha  sāhasānuraktaṃ hi striyo bhajante  iti tatra muktāśaṅko nirbhayaḥ pākhaṇḍāditi bhāvaḥ ata eva pra tānena nirargalonabhibhāvyaḥ pralāpeti pāṭhe hā nātha mādhavetyādimālatīpralāpena nirargala ucchṛṅkhala ityarthaḥ tyaktvā śaṅkāmiti pāṭhe śaṅkā bhayaṃ lajjādikaṃ vā vyaktyā pratāpanirākulo vā pratāpaniraṅkuśo vetyarthaḥ yadvā śaṅkāṃ tyaktvā yaṃ prati tvayā prakaṭito nijasnehaḥ soyamityarthaḥ yadvā ayaṃ kīdṛśaḥ prakāśitātmasnehaḥ maraṇasamaye rakṣaṇāditi bhāvaḥ he sutanu ata udgataṃ kampaṃ tyaja asau pāpaḥ saṃpratyeva pāpmano niṣiddhācaraṇasya phalaṃ maraṇarūpamugraṃ tīvramanubhaviṣyati saṃpratītyamālatīṃ vikṣipya āḥ durātman mālatī varākī śakti etannāsti kvacit nārtham khaṅgaṃ prakoṣṭhena vi gṛhītvā vi khaḍnaṃ mādhavama vilokya bhāo māhavo muktāśaṃka ṭī gala vā punaḥpañcamoṅkaḥ aghora   āḥ ka eṣa pāposmākamantarāyaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ kapāla   bhagavan sa evāsyā snehabhūmiḥ kāmandakīsuhṛtputro mahāmāṃsasya paṇāyitā mādhavaḥ mādhavaḥ  sāsram mahābhāge kimetat mālatī  cirādāśvasya mahābhāga ahamapi na jānāmi etāvatpunarjānāmi uparyālindakaṃ prasupteha prabuddhāsmi yūyaṃ punaḥ kva mahābhāa ahaṃ viṇa jāṇāmi ettiaṃ uṇe jāṇāmi uvarialindaaṃ pasuttā iha pabuddhāhma tujhe uṇa kahiṃ mādhavaḥ  salajjam tvatpāṇipaṅkajaparigraha dhanyajanmā bhūyāsamityabhiniveśakadarthyamānaḥ bhrāmyannamāṃsapaṇanāya paratabhūmāvākarṇya bhīru ruditāni tavāgatosmi mālatīsvagatam kathaṃ mama kāraṇādevātmanirapekṣaḥ parikrāmati kadhaṃ mama kālaṇādo eva appaṇirapekkho parikkāmadi nena prakṛtopayuktaṃ nijāptatvaṃ pauruṣaṃ ca dhvanitam kīdṛśasya pratīpo viparīto vipāko viruddhapariṇatiryatra tasya anubhavatītyatra vartamānasāmīpye vartamānavadveti bhaviṣyati laṭ śṛṅgāravīrasaṃbhedotra aghoraghaṇṭaḥ antarāyo vighnaḥ kapālakuṇḍalā bhūmiḥ sthānam mālatī trāsātiśayāccirānniḥśvāsaḥ atropari saudhopari alinde  oṭhṭha  iti prasiddhe yūyamiti ahamabalā suptā cānyenānītā yūyaṃ dhīrādhīrā vibuddhā apīdānīmiha kimarthamāgatā ityarthaḥ tvadityādi he bhīru mahāmāṃsavikrayāya smaśāne yogatosmi bhramaṃstava kranditānyākamahāmāṃsavikrayaphalamāha  tvaditi vā puṇyajanmāhaṃ bhavāmītyabhiniveśenātiyatnenāveśena tvadvivāhena kadarthyamānaḥ dhanyajanmā pīḍyamānaḥ atastvāṃ vinā na me jīvanamiti saṃbhāvyamānaphalatayā māṃsavikraye pravṛttosmīti bhāvaḥ tvatpādapaṅkajeti pāṭhe preyasīcaraṇagrahaṇasya māna eva kartavyatayā mānaprasādanamevottarottaraṃ caritetyāśaṃsitavān ata eva salajjamityuktamiti bhāvaḥ  dhanyaḥ puṇya iti smṛtaḥ iti viśvaḥ kutsitorthaḥ kadarthaḥ bhīru ityanena rodanopapattiruktā tadiha tvannimittamahaṃ sāhasī tvaṃ punaḥ kīdṛśīti na jāne iti tātparyam mālatī ata eva harṣavismayavaśādāha mālatī  kathamityādi paribhramaṇamitastato gamanam ātmanirapekṣaḥ smaśānabhramaṇena ahaṃ na kiṃvi jevtra apavārya evvaṃ ede pekkhaṃ  khā paribbhamandi evamete ā pekṣaṃ kṣā pariśramanti mālatīmādhave mādhavaḥ aho nu khalu bhoḥ tadetatkākatālīyaṃ nāma saṃprati hi rāhoścandrakalāmivānanacarīṃ daivātsamāsādya me dasyorasya kṛpāṇapātaviṣayāṃdācchindataḥ preyasīm ātaṅkādvikalaṃ drutaṃ karuṇayā vikṣobhitaṃ vismayātkrodhena jvalitaṃ mudā vikasitaṃ cetaḥ kathaṃ vartatām aghora  re re jīvanābhāva evāsyā iti bhāvaḥ corikayāpaharaṇena dasyutvam tadiha prathamārdhena heturuktaḥ dvitīyena phalamāha  ātaṅkāccittacamatkārādvikalaṃ na tvasya nisargasāttvikasya bhayamiti yadyapi tathāpi bhagavatī kāmandakī etannāsti kvacit sahasrasaṃ dasmātprade kalahaṃsaḥ  praviśya  vahiṇā maarandasaṇāhaṇa māha  ido  ṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥmālatyāḥ prathamāvalokaṃdivasādārabhya vistāriṇo bhūyaḥ snehaviceṣṭitairmṛgadṛśo nītasya koṭiṃ parām adyāntaḥ khalu sarvathāsya madanāyāsaprebandhasya me kalyāṇaṃ vidadhātu vā bhagavatīnītirviparyetu vā maka  vayasya kathaṃ bhagavatyāḥ sumedhaso nītirviparyeṣyati kala  upasṛtya nātha diṣṭyā vardhase pravṛttā khalu yātrābhimukhaṃ mālatī ṇāha diliā vaṭṭasi pauttā kkhu jettāhimuhaṃ māladī mādhavaḥ  api nāma sayam maka  sakhe kimaśraddadhānaḥ pṛcchasi na kevalaṃ pravṛttā pratyāsannā ca vartate tathā hi asmākamekaparda eva marudvikīrṇajīmūtajālarasiṃtānukṛtirninādaḥ gambhīramaṅgalamṛdṅgasahasrajanmā śabdāntaragrahaṇaśaktimapākaroti garbhagṛhavartitvena mādhavasya guptatvam mādhavaḥ rājaviruddhaco rikāvivāhasya duṣka ratayā kāmandakī pratijñāsatyatvena ca saṃdehavānāha mālatyā ityādi mamāsya vipralambhajakleśasya sarvathobhayaprakāreṇa niścitamadyāntaḥ samāptiḥ kīdṛśasya mṛgadṛśo mālatyāḥ pracurapremṇā yāni viceṣṭitāni taiḥ parāṃ koṭiṃ prakarṣakāṣṭāṃ prāpita sya ādyadarśanadinādārabhya vistāraṃ gataiḥ tatra prathame bakulavīthiceṣṭābhirdvitīye mādhavacitrāvalokanādinā tṛtīye svapnopabhogavarṇanādinā caturthe mohanāśakakarasparśādinā pañcame bhayakanpitāṅgāliṅganādinā vistāra iti bhāvaḥ paryavasānamāha bhagavatīnītiḥ kāmandakīnisṛṣṭārthadūtīkalpaḥ kalyāṇaṃ śubhaṃ mālatīvivāhalakṣaṇaṃ vā karotu viparyaye tu viphalā vā bhavatu tathā ca vivāhe sati śṛṅgārasaṃbhogalābhena kāmāyāsaśāntiḥ viparyaye maraṇāditi bhāvaḥ makarandaḥ sumedhasaḥ subuddheḥ viparyeṣyati viparyayameṣyati kalahaṃsakaḥ atra yātrā gamatasya mukhamārambham mādhavaḥ tadvākyasyāśvāsaparatvaṃ tarkaya nāha  apīti api nāmeti saṃbhāvanāyām asmākamityādi vātanamū vistārimeghasamūhaśabditatulyo gambhīramaṅgalārthamurajasahasrajanmā śabda ekapada lokanadinādā sasya me sarvataḥ sumedhāyāḥ sā medhāśaktiḥ ṇāha māhava idomuhaṃ satyametad dadhāna iva padmeṣa ninadā śravaṇa mālatīmādhave tadehi jālamārgeṇa paśyāmaḥ tathā kurvanti kalahaṃsakaḥ  nātha prekṣasva prekṣasva ime tāvadutpatitarājahaṃsavibhramābhirāmacāmarasamīraṇodballakadalikāvalītaraṅgitottānagaganāṅganasarovarānarantaroddaṇḍapuṇḍarīkavibhramaṃ vahanto dhavalātapatranivahā dṛśyante imāḥ savilāsa kavalita tāmbūlaṃvīṭikāpūritakapolamaṇḍalābhogavyatikara skhalitamadhuramaṅgalodgītabaddhakolāhalairvividharatnālaṃkārakiraṇāvalīviḍambita mahendracāpavicchedavicchuritanabhaḥsthalairvārasundarīkadambairadhyāsitā utkaṇatkanakakiṃkiṇījālajhaṇajhaṇajhaṃkāriṇyaḥ kariṇyaḥ ṇāha pekkha pekkha imedāva uppaḍiarāahaṃsavibbhamāhirāmacāmarasamīraṇovvellakadaliāvalītaraṅgiduttāṇagaaṇaṅgaṇasarovaraṇirantaruddaṇḍapuṇḍarīavinbhamaṃ vahanto dhavalādavattaṇivahā dīsanti imāo savilāsakavalidatambūlavīḍiāpūridakavolamaṇḍalābho avvaiarakkhalidamahuramaṅgaluggīabaddhakolāhalehiṃ viviharaaṇālaṃkārakiraṇāvalīviḍāmbada mahindacāvaiviccheavicchuridaṇahatthalehiṃ vārasundarīkadambehiṃ ajjhāsiā okvaṇantakaṇaakiṃkiṇījālajhaṇajhaṇajhaṃkāriṇīo kariṇīo mādhavamakarandau sakautukaṃ paśyataḥ makarandaḥ  spṛhaṇīyāḥ khalvamātyabhūrivasorvibhūtayaḥ tathā hi prerimayūkha mecakacayai rummeṣicāpacchedacchāyāsaṃvalitairvivartibhiriva prānteṣu paryāvṛtāḥ ekasminkṣaṇesmākaṃ śabdāntaragrahaṇasāmarthya nirākaroti vādyaraveṇānyaśabdo na śrūyata ityarthaḥ sahasragrahaṇamanekopalakṣaṇam sahasrapatravat kalahaṃsakaḥ mādhavotsāhārthamāha  nātheti atra utpatita uḍḍīnaḥ vibhramo vilāso viśiṣṭabhramaṇaṃ vā abhirāmastulyaḥ udvellankampamānaḥ kadālikā patākā taraṅgitaṃ taraṅgayuktam uttānamagabhīram gaganameva saraḥ uddaṇḍamudgatadaṇḍam ātapatraṃ chatram maṅgalātapatramiti pāṭhe vivāhe śuklacchatrasya praśasta tathā maṅgalapadena śvetatvamuktam etāḥ kariṇyaśca dṛśyanta ityanvayaḥ cakārotrādhyāhartavyaḥ carvitaṃ bhakṣitam vyatikaraḥ saṃghaṭṭaḥ skhalitaṃ bhaṅgimat maṅgalodgītaṃ maṅgalarūpamuccairgānam viḍambitaṃ sadṛśīkṛtam vicchedaḥ khaṇḍaḥ vicchuritaṃ vyāptam jhaṇajhaṇārūpo jhaṅkāraśabdaḥ premadityādi taraṇikiraṇasaṃparkādūrdhvamukhairmaṇidāptisaṅkhairvivartibhiritastato gataiḥ prānteṣu nikaṭeṣu paryāvṛtā carvitatā ṭī lāvalipū sarerāṇi maṅgaladha cāpakhaṇḍa kiṃkiṇījhaṇa jālarīṇaa sakautukau saspṛhamiitya ramaṇīyāḥ ṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ vyaṃktākhaṇḍalakārmukā iva bhavantyuccitracīnāṃśukaprastārasthagitā ivonmukhamaṇijyotirvitā nairdiśaḥ kalahaṃsakaḥ  kathaṃ sasaṃbhramānekapratihāramaṇḍalāvajitojjvalakanakakaladhautapatravicitravetralatāparīkṣiptarekhāracitamaṇḍalo dūrata eva saṃsthitaḥ parijanaḥ eṣā ca bahalasindūranikarasaṃdhyārāgoparakta mukhaghūrṇatkāntanakṣatramālābharaṇadhāriṇīṃ kareṇarajanīma laṃkurvatīta eva kautūhalonmukhasamastalokadṛśyamānamanoharā pāṇḍuraparikṣāmadehaśobhā prathamacandralekhāvibhramaṃ vahantī kiṃcidantaraṃ prasṛtā mālatī kadhaṃ sasaṃbhamāṇeapaḍihāramaṇḍalāvajjidujjalakaṇaakaladhauavattavicittavettaladāparikkhittarehāraidamaṇḍalo ra do jjevva se saṃhido pariaṇo esā a bahalasindūraṇiarasaṃjjhārāovaratta byāptā iva diśo vyaktendracāṃpā iva bhavanti kīdṛśaiḥ preṅkhanta itastataścalanto bhūrīṇāṃ suvarṇānāṃ mayūkhāḥ kiraṇā yatra tādṛśo mecakaḥ snigdhaścayo yeṣu taiḥ mayuramecakanibhairiti pāṭhe preṅkhannṛtyanyo bahumayūrastasya mecakāñcandrakānniratiśayā bhā yeṣāṃ taiḥ mecakaścandra ke snigdhe śyāmalepi ca dṛśyate  iti viśvaḥ bhūri klī suvarṇe ca prājye syādvācyaliṅgakam  iti medinīkaraḥ unmeṣyuḍḍīno yaścāṣaḥ pakṣibhedastasya cchadacchāyayā pakṣakāntyā saṃvalitairiva militaiḥ kīdṛśyaḥ udgatacitrasya cīnadeśabhavavastrasya prastāreṇa śayyayā prasāreṇa vā cchannā iva prastārastanitaṃ śayyā iti hārāvalī maṇaya ihābharaṇastharatnāni kalahaṃsakaḥ atrāvarjitā tiryaktyaktā kanakaṃ hiraṇyam kaladhautaṃ rajatam  kaladhauta hemaraupyayoḥ iti viśvaḥ paṅkena lepena vetralatā vetradaṇḍikā parikṣiptā racitā racita maṇḍala iti asmānmaṇḍalātkenāpi na bahirgantavyamiti bhāvaḥ dūrata eva mālatyā ityarthāt pṛthusindūrapūra eva sandhyārāgastenoparaktā kiñcidāraktā caṭulā capalā ghūrṇatī lambamānā yā nakṣatramālā saptaviṃśatimauktikamālā hastiprasādhanabhedo vā saivābharaṇaṃ taddhāriṇīm rātripakṣe nakṣatramālā tārakāmālā kareṇurhastinī saiva rātristām dṛśyamānā cāsau manoharā ceti samāsaḥ pāṇḍurā dhūsarā parikṣāmātikṛśāṅgadīptiryasyāḥ sā etena candrakalāsāmyamutam dṛśyamānetyanenānyeṣāṃ darśanamātraṃ tava paramupabhogo mālatyā iti sūcitam pāṇḍuretyādinā mālatyāmāntara udvega uktaḥ kiñcidantaraṃ kiyaddūram prasṛtā gatā kaladhautaṭaṅkapatreti pāṭhe ṭaṅkapatraṃ paṭṭiketyarthaḥ vyaktā raktacaṭulaghū ṭī paṅka pattalipta dūrasaṃṭidomālatīmādhave kantaṇakkhattamālābharaṇadhāriṇiṃ kareṇuraaṇiṃ alaṃkarantī ido jjavvai kodṛhalummuṃhasamatthaloadissantamaṇuharā paṇḍuraparikkhāmadehasohāṃ paḍharmaṃcandalehāvibbhamaṃ vahandī kiṃci antaraṃ pasaridā māladī muhagholanta makarandaḥ  vayasya paśya paśya iyamavayavaiḥ pāṇḍukṣāmairalaṃkṛtamaṇḍanā kalitakusuṃmā bālevāntalatā pariśoṣiṇī vahati ca varārohā ramyāṃ vivāhamahotsavaśriyamudayinīmuddrauḍhāṃ ca vyanakti manorujam kathaṃ niṣāditā gajavadhūḥ mādhavaḥ  sānandam kathamavartīya bhagavatīlavaṅgikābhyāṃ samamitaḥ pravṛttaiva tataḥ praviśati kāmandakī mālatī lavaṅgikā ca kāmandakī saharṣamapavārya vidhātā bhadraṃ no vitaratu manojñāya vidhaye vidheyāsudaivāḥ paramaraṇīyāṃ pariṇatim kṛtīrthā bhūyāsaṃ priyasuhṛdpatyopayamane prayatnaḥ kṛtsnoyaṃ phalatu śivatātiśca bhavatu iyamityādi iyaṃ varārohā praśastaśroṇikā vivāhamahotsavasaṃpatti prakṛṣṭāṃ ramyāṃ ca vahati sahajaramaṇīyatvāt ugāḍhāṃ prabalāṃ cittapīḍāṃ ca prakāśayati kīdṛśī pāṇḍukṣāmairaṅgairalaṅkatabhūṣaṇā atiramyatayāmībhireva bhūṣaṇānyalaṃkriyanta iti bhāvaḥ antarabhyantare pariśoṣiṇī ata evāṅgānāṃ pāṇḍukṣāmatvam kalitaṃ parihitaṃ kusumaṃ yayā sā bālā ṣoḍaśavarṣavayaskā avayavairityanena sarvāgīṇaṃ pāṇḍutvāyuktam lateva yathā latā navā vasantādiprabhāvātsupuṣpāpi kutaścidvaikṛtādantaḥpariśoṣaṃ vahati tatheyamapītyarthaḥ niṣāditā upaveśitā avatāraṇārthamidam kāmandakī saharṣamitya bhīṣṭasaṃpādanāditi bhāvaḥ vidhātetyādi nosmākaṃ manojñāya hṛdisthāya vidhaye vyāpārāya prakṛtavivāhāya bhadraṃ kuśalamavighnaṃ vidhātā dadātu vidhaya ityatra tādarthye caturthī kriyārthopapadasyeti vā vṛttepi kārye rājavirodhādaniṣṭamāśaṅkayāha  paramaramaṇīyāmavirodhinīṃ timuttaraviśuddhiṃ devāḥ kurvantu svasyāpi phalamāha  ahaṃ kṛtakṛtyā bhūyāsam yato mālatīmādhavayorvivāhe samastoyaṃ prayatnaḥ phalatu uttarakālaśuddhayā phaladāyī bhavatvityarthaḥ pariṇatiśuddhayā śivadāyī bhavatu kalyāṇakarostvityarthaḥ pariṇa muhamahura halupphullamuha sohāvibhāvidāṇaṅgaveaṇā paḍhamuggaañccanda hasantī kiṃvi kimapi  klāntaiḥ maṇḍalā sumatrātevā mā jātevā ramyā mudbhutāṃ kṛtārthī tyopayamataḥ hṛdi yatnairabhimataḥ prayāsaḥ śivadāyīṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ mālatī  svagatam kena punarupāyena sāṃprataṃ maraṇanirvāṇasyāntaraṃ saṃbhāvayiṣye maraṇamapi mandabhāgadheyānāmabhimatamiti durlabhaṃ bhavati keṇa uṇa uvāeṇa saṃpadaṃ maraṇaṇivvāṇassa andaraṃ saṃbhāvaissaṃ maraṇaṃ vi mandabhāadheāṇaṃ ahimadaṃ tti dullahaṃ hodi lavaṅgikā  svagatam atiklāmitā khalu priyasakhyetenānukūlavipralambhena adikilammidā kkhu piasahī ediṇā aṇuūlavippalambheṇa  praviśya pālakahastā pratīhārī  bhagavati amātyo bhaṇati etena narendrānupreṣitena vivāhanepathyena devatāpuratolaṃkartavyā mālatīti bhañaivadi amacco bhaṇādi ediṇā narindāṇuppesideṇa vivāhaṇevattheṇa devadāpurado alaṃkaridavvā māladi tti kāmandakī  yuktamāhāmātyaḥ māṅgalikaṃ hi tatsthānam ato darśaya pratī  etattāvaddhavalapaṭṭāṃśukacolakametaccottarīyaraktavarṇāśukam ime ca sarvāṅgikā ābharaṇasaṃyogāḥ ayaṃ ca mauktikāśivatātiśca bhavatviti pāṭhe śivatātiḥ śivakaraḥ sarvadevāttātilityanuvartamāne śivaśamariṣṭasya kare iti tātila atra maraṇameva sarvaduḥkhanāśakatayā nirvāṇaṃ mokṣastasyāntaramavasaraḥ yadvā maraṇameva nirvāṇaṃ nirvṛtiḥ sukham nirvāṇaṃ nirvṛtau mokṣe iti viśvaḥ antaramavasarādhyātmasadṛśeṣu  iti medinīkaraḥ mālatī saṃbhāvayiṣye samyak prāpsyāmi bhū prāptāvityasyātmanepadino rūpam sāṃpratamityanena mādhavālābhānnandanalābhavilambanāceti darśitam mandabhāgyatayā mādhavaprāptivanmaraṇamapi na syāditi bhāvaḥ lavaṅgikā atra klāmitā kamaṃ śramaṃ prāpitā anukūlena mādhavena saha vipralambho virahastena yadvā anukūlo nandanastasya vipralambhena vañcanayā pratīhārī peṭakaṃ mañjūṣā peṭakaṃ pustakādīnāṃ mañjūṣāyāṃ kadambake  iti medinīkaraḥ paṭakagrahaṇaṃ tu nandanaprasādhanārtham atra nepathyaṃ prasādhanam kāmandakī yuktamiti etatprasādhanena makarandamalaṃkṛtya madayantikāṃ vivāhayiṣyāmīti bhāvaḥ māṅgalikaṃ maṅgalahetuḥ pratīhārī atra dhavalaṃ yatpahuṃ sūtramayamaṃśukaṃ tena nirmitaścolakaḥ kūpasakaḥ me mandabhāadheāe ahimadaṃ adidu adikīlāliā atikleśitā  kilāmidā peṭālaka bhūṣaṇapaṭalaka amañco bhaavadiṃ viṣṇavedi devadāe mālatīmādhave hāraḥ etaccandanam eṣa sitakusumāpīḍa iti edaṃ dāva dhavalapasuacolaaṃ edaṃ a uttarīarattavaṇṇaṃsuaṃ ime a savvaṅgiā āharaṇasaṃjoā aṃaṃ a mottiāhāro edaṃ candaṇaṃ eso sidakusumāpīḍo tti kāma  apavārya ramaṇīyaṃ hi vatsaṃ makarandamavalokayiṣyati madayantikā prakāśam gṛhītvā bhavatvevamityucyatāmamātyaḥ  tathā tahā iti niṣkāntā  lavāṅgake praviśa tvamabhyantaraṃ vatsayā mālatyā saha  atha bhagavatī punaḥ kva adha bhaavadī uṇa kahiṃ kāma   ahamapi tāvadviviktelaṃkaraṇaratnānāṃ prāśastyaṃ śāstrataḥ parīkṣaṣye iti niṣkrāntā pratī kāma lava mālatī  svagatamū lavaṅgikāmātraparivārāsmi saṃvṛttā lavaṅgikāmettaparivārahmi saṃutta lava  etaddevatāmandiradvāram tatpraviśāvaḥ edaṃ devatāmandiraduvāraṃ pavisī iti praviśataḥ maka  vayasya itastāvatstambhāpavāritau tiṣṭhāvaḥ tathā kurutaḥ  sakhi ayamaṅgarāgaḥ imāḥ kusumamālāḥ sahi aaṃ lava aṅgarāo imāo kusumamālāo mālatī  tataḥ kim taṃdo kiṃ colaḥ kūrpāsakostriyām ityamaraḥ uttarīyarūpaṃ raktāṃśukaṃ sindūrīvastram āpīḍaḥ śekharostriyām  iti medinīkaraḥ bhavatīti saṃbodhanam kāmandakī gurusamakṣaṃ mālatyanurāgānubhavo mādhavasya na syādata uktam praviśa tvamiti kāmandakī vivikte vijane mālatī hṛddvatamaraṇāvakāśaprāptyā sānandoktiriyam bāhyasaṃvedanābhāvānmālatī na paśyatīti bhāvaḥ makarandaḥ apavāritaṃ vyavahitam lavaṅgikā atrāṅgarāgaḥ kuṅkumādiḥ mālatī tatprayojanamapaśyantīvāha  tataḥ kiṃ mayānena kartavyamityarthaḥ jualaṃ rīaṃ rattaṃsuaṃ ime sideti nāsti kvacit janaḥ bhavatvomi ātmagatam vārā dāva asmāraparaṃ prakāśaṃ edaṃ devatā i tā tat pavisad piṃasahī itaḥ stambhāntaritau paśyāvaḥ  ṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ lava  sakhi asminpāṇigrahaṇamaṅgalārambhe kalyāṇasaṃpattinimittaṃ devatāḥ pūjayetyambayānupreṣitāsi sahi imassi pāṇiggahaṇamaṅgalārambhe kallāṇasaṃvattiṇimittaṃ devadāo pūjehi tti ambāe aṇuppesidāsi mālatī  kimidānīṃ dāruṇasamārambhadaivadurvilāsapariṇāmaduḥkhanirdagdhamānasāṃ punaḥ punarmarmacchedaduḥsahaṃ māṃ mandabhāginīṃ dunoṣi kiṃ dāṇiṃ dāruṇasamārambhadevvaduvvilāsapariṇāmadukkhaṇiddaddhamāṇasaṃ puṇo puṇo mammaicchedadūsahaṃ maṃ mandabhāiṇīṃ dūmāvesi lavaṅgikā  atha kimasi vaktukāmā aha kiṃsi vattakāmā mālatī  yadidānīṃ durlabhābhiniveśamanorathavisaṃvaidbhāgadheyo jano mantrayate jaṃ dāṇiṃ dullahāhiṇivesamaṇorahavisaṃvadantabhāadheo jaṇo mantedi makarandaḥ  sakhe śrutam mādhavaḥ  śrutamasaṃtoṣaśca hṛdayasya mālatī  lavadbhikāṃ pariṣvajya paramārthabhagini priyasakhi lavaṅgike eṣedānīṃ te priyasakhyanāthā maraṇe vartamānāgarbhanirgamanirantaropakāroparūḍhavisrambhasadṛśaṃ pariṣvajya tvāṃ prārthayate yada tehamanuvartanīyā tato māṃ hṛdayena dhārayantī samagra saubhāgyalakṣmīlavaṅgikā atra pāṇigrahaṇeti sāmānyoktyā mādhavanandanayorvivāhaśleṣeṇa narmasphoṭoyaṃ bhāvaḥ yahāha  śleṣeṇoktistu bhāvānāṃ narmasphoṭa itīritaḥ mālatīatra durvilāsapariṇāmaḥ priyatyāgāpriyaprāptilakṣaṇaḥ duḥsahamiti kriyāviśeṣaṇam anayā śliṣṭaṃ madraco na jñātamata iyamevaṃ vadatvityata āha lava atha kimityādi mālatī atrābhiniveśinā manorathena visaṃvādaṃ pratikūlaṃ bhāgyaṃ yasya saḥ makarandraḥ mādhave durlabhāṃ vāñchāṃ matvāha  sakhe śrutamiti mādhavaḥ śliṣṭe vacasyaniṣṭāśaṅkitamāha  asantoṣa iti mālatī atra paramārthetyādinā viśvāsapātratvamuktam virūḍha upacitaḥ sadṛśaṃ yathā tathā pariṣvajyetyanvayaḥ anuvartanīyopakartavyā samagrasaubhāgya padenāravindaspardhinī śobhoktā yadāha  uttamairguṇibhiḥ spardhā yā gahaṇārambhe devadāṃ nivveda ai visaṃvāda ṭī kiṃ śrūyatāma ṣastu kāravirūḍha parigrahaikamaṅgalaṃ śrīmādhavasya mukhāravindamānandamasṛṇamavalokayiṣyasi paramatthabahiṇi piasahi lavaṅgie esā dāṇiṃ de piasahī aṇāhā maraṇe vaṭṭamāṇā āgabbhaṇiggamaṇirantarovaārovarūḍhavissambhasarisaṃ parissajjia tumaṃ patthedi jai de ahaṃ aṇuvaṇīā tado maṃ hiaeṇa dhāraantī samaggasohaggalacchīpāraṃggahekamaṅgalaṃ māhavasiriṇo muhāravindaṃ āṇandamasiṇaṃ avaloaissasi iti roditi mālatīmādhave mādhavaḥ  vayasya makaranda mlānasya jīvakusumasya vikāsanāni saṃtarpaṇāni sakalendriyamohanāni ānandanāni hṛdayaikarasāyanāni diṣṭyā mayāpyadhigatāni vacomṛtāni mālatī  yathā tasya jīvitapradāyino janasyāvasiteti māṃ śrutvā saṃtapyamānasya tattathāvidhaṃ śarīraratnaṃ na parihīyate yathā ca lokāntaragatāmapi māmuddiśya sa janaḥ smaraṇasaṃkathāmātrapariśeṣāṃ kālāntasā śobhā prakīrtitā  māṃ hṛdaye dhārayantītyanena paraṃparayā mamāpi darśanaṃ syādityu ktam mādhavaśriya ityatra prākṛte pūrvanipātāniyamāchrīmādhavasyetyarthaḥ ānandamasṛṇatvena snigdhā dṛṣṭiruktā mlānasyetyādi vacāṃsyevāmṛtāni mayāpi diṣṭayā nirṇītāni tvayā śrutamityādinā nirṇītāni mayā tvadhunetyapipadārthaḥ amṛtatulyatvamāha mlānasya pratyāśābhaṅgajñānena saṃkocitasya jīvapuṣpasya prakāśanāni amṛtepi sarvaprakāśakatayā mlānapuṣpaprakāśakatvam saṃtarpaṇāni tṛptikaraṇāni amṛtepyevam saṃtarpaṇe sati bāhyendriyatarpakāṇi amṛtepyevam ānandanānyantarmodakāni āyyata ānīyatenenetyāyanam rasasyāyanaṃ rasāyanam vacasāṃ cittollāsakatvena navatvajananādi vā mṛtasya jarādināśakatvena navatvajananādidamiti bhāvaḥ yadvā amṛtapadena jalamokṣapīyūṣāpyucyante tatrādyapadena jalasāmyam mokṣasāmyārthapadatrayam mokṣe hi samyaktṛptiviṣaye nirākāṅkṣataiva indriyamohopi viṣayagrahābhāvāt  ānandaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tacca mokṣe pratiṣṭhitam  iti śruterānandamayatā mokṣe yadvā ādyapadābhyāṃ jalasāmyamitarapadābhyāṃ mokṣasāmyam pīyūṣasāmyārtha śeṣapadam amṛtaṃ mokṣapīyūṣasalileṣu ghṛtepi ca  iti dharaṇiḥ mālatī atrāvasitā ṇiggamaṇimmida abbhatthedi māhavassa sirimuhā paloehi pralokaya  paraloka ṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ repi lokayātrāṃ na śithilayati tathā kuruṣva evameva priyasakhyāḥ prasādānmālatī kṛtārthā bhavati jahā tasya jīvidappadāiṇo jaṇassa avasidatti maṃ suṇia saṃdappamāṇassa taṃ tahāvihaṃ sarīraraaṇaṃ ṇa parihīadi jahā a loandaragadaṃ vi maṃ uddisia so jaṇo sumaraṇasaṃkadhāmettaparisesaṃ kālandare vi loajattaṃ ṇa siḍhiledi tahā karesu evaṃ jjevva piasahīe pasādādo māladī kidatthā bhodi makarandaḥ  hanta atikaruṇaṃ prastutam mādhavaḥ nairāśyakātaradhiyo hariṇekṣaṇāyāḥ śrutvā nikāmakaruṇaṃ ca manoharaṃ ca vātsalyamohaparidevitamudrahāmi cintāviṣādavipadaṃ ca mahotsavaṃ ca lavaṅgikā  ayi pratihatamidānīṃ temaṅgalam nātopyadhikataraṃ śroṣyāmi ai paḍihadaṃ dāṇiṃ de amaṅgalaṃ ṇe ado vi adhiadaraṃ suṇissaṃ mṛtā tathāvidhamanirvacanīyam na parihīyate na naśyati tathā kariṣyasītyanvayaḥ lokayātrā gārhasthyam sapatnīkatvaṃ vā mādhavāptipratyāśānāśādeva mevetyavadhāraṇam makarandaḥ hantānukampāyām karuṇamiti ālasyādisamutyo nirapekṣabhāvaḥ karuṇaḥ autsukyacintāsamutthaḥ sāpekṣabhāvo vipralambha ityanayorbhedaḥ ata eva nira pekṣapadopalakṣitanairāśyamāha mādhavaḥ  nairāśyetyādi nairāśyena pratyāśānāśena kātarā visaṃṣṭhulā dhīryasyā hariṇanetrāyāḥ vātsalyaṃ priyaviśleṣe prāṇatyāgecchā moho bhramaḥ sapratyāśatvepi nairāśyābhimānaḥ tābhyāṃ yatparidevitaṃ vilapanaṃ vṛttavartamānabhāvyārthacintanamatikaruṇaṃ manojñaṃ ca śrutvā cintayā yo viṣādastena vipattimudvahāmi cintāviṣādarūpāṃ vā vipatiṃ mahotsavaṃ codvahāmi cakāro mithoviruddharasayojane iha hetuphalabhāvenānvayaḥ tathā hi nairāśyakātarabuddhitvādvātsalyam tataḥ paridevanam tacchrutvā mano viṣādaḥ tathā hariṇekṣaṇatvenāpahṛtacittasya mamālābhānmanojñaparidevitaṃ śrutvā mahotsavaḥ sa punaḥ krandanaimahaiḥ pralāpaiḥ paridevanaiḥ dehāyāsābhighātaiśca karuṇābhinayo bhavet  iti bharataḥ lavaṅgikā atrāmaṅgalapratighāto vivā kālandareṇa evvaṃ de piasahī māladī sakāmā hoi vartate vasāna vasāda ido vi avaraṃ ṇa mālatīmādhave mālatī  sakhi priyaṃ khalu yuṣmākaṃ mālatījīvitaṃ na punarmālatī sahi piaṃ kkhu tuhmāṇaṃ māladījīvidaṃ ṇa uṇa māladī lavaṅgikā  sakhi kimevaṃ bhaṇitaṃ bhavati sahi kiṃ aibvaṃ bhaṇidaṃ bhodi parityamālatī  ātmānaṃ nirdiśya yena pratyāśānibandhanairvaca nasaṃvidhānairjīvayitvemaṃ mahābībhatsārambhamanubhāvitāsmi sāṃprataṃ punarmanoratho me eṣa eva yattasya devasya parakīyatvenāparāddhamātmānaṃ kṣyāmīti tadasminprayojane priyasakhī meparipanthinī bhavatu jeṇa paccāsāṇibandhaṇehiṃ vaaṇasaṃvihāṇehiṃ jīāvia imaṃ mahābībhacchārambha anubhāvidāhma sapadaṃ uṇe maṇoraho me eso jevva jaṃ tassa devassa parakeraattaṇeṇa avaraddhaṃ attāṇaṃ paricaissaṃ tti tā imassi paoaṇe piasahī me aparipanthiṇī hodu iti pādayoḥ patati makarandaḥ  saiṣā paramā sīmā snehasya lavaṅgikā mādhavaṃ saṃjñayā samāhvayati makarandaḥ  vayasya upasṛtya lavaṅgikāsthāne tiṣṭha mādhavaḥ  paiṃravānasmi sādhvasena makarandaḥ  iyameva nedīyasāṃ prakṛtirabhyudayānām mādhavaḥ svairaṃ laṃvaṅgikāsthāne tiṣṭhati mālatī  sakhi kurvanukulataya prasādam sahi karehi aṇuūladāe pasādaṃ hāditi bāhyam mādhavasannidhānādityāntaram mālatī bāhyārthamākalaghyāha  atra taccharīrāvacchinnātmā mālatī jīvanaṃ tvadṛṣṭaviśeṣakāritadehātmasaṃyoga iti jīvanamālatyorbhedaḥ jīvanasya sukhahetutayā priyatvaṃ tacceha duḥkhasaṃtatijanakamatastyājyameva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ mālatī atrānyajanetyatrānyapadena mādhavābhidhānam nandanāpekṣayānyatvāt durlabhatvena parakīyatvāropādvā bībha tsamiha nandanavivāhārthamaṅgalasyāniṣṭhasya darśanāt anaparāddhamitaṣidarthe nañ ānandanavivāhaparyantasthāyitve mahāparādho yataḥ anyasya saṃbhogāderabhāvādeṣa evetyuktam aparipanthinyavirodhinī etadātmatyāgarūpam saṃjñayā saṃketena mādhavaḥ paravānāyattaḥ sādhvasena jaḍatayā makarandaḥ atyabhīṣṭalābhādiyam nedīyasāṃ nikaṭānām svairaṃ śanaiḥ mālatī atra martu svīkurvityarthaḥ ti uddiśya anyajanapra ṭī parādhīnatvenānapa uṇa me mahābhāassa parokkhaguṇasaṃkittaṇeṇa aṇava pariccaia ṇivvudā huvissaṃ parityajya nirvṛtā bhaviṣyāmi  vayasya para svairamupasṛtya tāyaiṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ mādhavasarale sāhasarāgaṃ parihara rambhoru muñca saṃrambham virasaṃ virahāyāsaṃ soḍhuṃ tava cittamasahaṃ me mālatī  sakhi alaṅghanīya eaiva te mālatīpraṇāmaḥ sahi alaṅgaṇīo jevva de māladīppaṇāmo mādhavaḥ saharṣam kiṃ vā bhaṇāmi vicchedadāruṇāyāsakarāiṇa kāmaṃ kuru varārohe dehi me parirambhaṇam mālatī  saharṣam kathamanugṛhītāsmi utthāya iyamāliṅgāmi darśanaṃ punaḥ priyasakhyā bāppotpīḍena niruddhaṃ na labhyate āliṅgatha sānandam sakhi kaṭhorakamalagarbhapakṣamalonyāhaśa eva tedya nirvāpayati māṃ śarīrasparśa sāsram kiṃ ca mauliviniveśitāñjalirmama vacanena vijñapaya taṃ janaṃ nai mayā mandabhāgyayā vikasatpuṇḍarīmādhavasya saṃskṛtabhāṣayā lavaṅgikābhramo na syāditi bhāṣāsamāveśenāha sarala ityādi sāhasa ātmanirapekṣakārye rāgamanurāgaṃ parihara rambhoru kadalīsamorudeśe he saṃrambhaṃ maraṇe tvarāṃ tyaja jīvantyāṃ pratyāśāpi syāditi bhāvaḥ virasaṃ rasaśūnyaṃ tava viśleṣaduḥkhaṃ soḍhuṃ me cittamakṣamaṃ yataḥ atoyaṃ vallabhastvayi dattotastyaja maraṇābhiniveśamiti lavāṅgakābhiprāyaḥ ata eva sarale ajñe ṛjuprakṛtike vā mādhavapakṣe sarale ajānati he tava virahāyāsa soḍhuṃ me cittamasahamatastava samīpamāgatosmi tanmaraṇaṃ tyaja itaratsamameva tadiha saṃskṛtaprākṛtayoḥ sāmyātprākṛtasamakam kiṃ vetyādi kiṃvā bhaṇāmi tvadā rambhaniṣedhaṃ na karomītyarthaḥ he virahaduḥsahakaṣṭakāriṇi suśroṇi kāmamabhīṣṭaṃ kuru yadyevaṃ tadā mamāliṅganaṃ dehīti lavaṅgikāpakṣe mādhavapakṣe tu kiṃvā bhaṇāmi kiṃ vaktavyena kāmaṃ kāmavyāpāraṃ kuru ataḥ parirambhaṇaṃ dehi ārohaḥ śroṇikāyayoḥ  iti dharaṇiḥ ślokadvayamidaṃ saurasenyā yadāha  spaṣṭārtha lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ saurasenyāḥ prapañcataḥ lakṣaṇaṃ tvekamevāsyāḥ saṃskṛtādyadanunatā  mālatī atra utpīḍaḥ prabalībhūya nirgamaḥ utpīḍaḥ samūho vā apaścimaṃ caramam priyasparśādāhlādātsaharṣam kaṭhoramarālagarbho bījakośaḥ pakṣamalo romāñcayogāt samādhinā sukumāraḥ anyādṛśa evānubhūtasakhīsparśavidharmā śmaśānānubhūtasparśatulyaḥ nirvāpayati tāpaṃ śamayati tathā tādṛśaḥ sparśaḥ śaṅkāviṣayopyantra neti nirvedātsāśrutā atra vikasanti śataṃ patrāṇi yasya tat anyathedaṃ vyartha syāt maṇḍalapadaṃ saṃpūrṇatvārtham virasā  voḍhum eṣaḥ tvāṃ kāriṇīṃ paḍinena niruddhaṃ priyasakhyā apaścimaṃ na ṭī  pakṣmalasukumāraḥ ṭī  vijñāpāryavyāsa ṭī yathā namālatīmādhave kalakṣmīvilāsahāriṇo mukhacandramaṇḍalasya te svacchandadarśanena saṃbhāvitaściraṃ locanamahotsavaḥmudhāmanorathaiścāviratavijṛmbhamāṇadurvārodvegavyatikarodvartamānabandhanaṃ dhāritaṃ hṛdayam gamitāśca vāraṃvāraṃ saviśeṣaduḥsahārambhadāvitasakhījanāḥ śarīrasaṃtāpāḥ kathamapyativāhitā ca candrātapamalayamārutapramukhānarthaparamparā sāṃprataṃ punarnirāśāsmi saṃvṛtteti tvayāpi priyasakhi sarvadā smartavyāsmi eṣā ca śrīmādhavasvahastanirmāṇamanoharā bakulamālā mālatīnirviśeṣaṃ priyasakhyā draṣṭavyā sarvadā hṛdaye dhāraṇīyā iti svakaṃṭhādapanīya mādhavasya hṛdi bakulamālāṃ vinyasyantī sahasāpasṛtya sādhvasotkampaṃ nāṭayati kadhaṃ aṇugahīdahmi iaṃ āliṃgāmi daṃsaṇaṃ uṇa piasahīe bāhu ha ppīḍeṇa ṇiruddhaṃ ṇa lambhīadi sahi kaṭhorakamalagabhapālo aṇṇāriso jevva de aja ṇivvāvedi maṃ sarīrapphaṃso kiṃ a maulivinivesidañjalī maha vaaṇeṇa viṇṇavāha taṃ jaṇaṃ jaha ṇa mae mandabhāiṇīe viasantapuṇḍarīalacchīvilāsahāriṇo muhacanda maṇḍalassa sacchandadaṃsaṇeṇa saṃbhāvido ciraṃ loaṇamahosavo mudhāmaṇorahiṃ a aviraāviambhamāṇaduvvāruvveavaiavvattamāṇabaṃdhaṇaṃ dhāriaṃ hiaaṃ gamiā a vāraṃvāraṃ savisesadūsarhārambhadūmāvidasahīaṇā sarīrasaṃdāvā kadhaṃ vi adivāhidā a candādapamalaamārudappamuhā aṇaddhaparamparā saṃpadaṃ uṇa nirāsa utteti vipiasahi savvadā sumarīdavtrahmi esā a māhavasirīsahatthaṇimmāṇamaṇuharā vaulamālā māladīṇivvisesaṃ piasahīe danuvvā savvadā hiae dhāraṇijjā tti ciramityanena svādhīnabhartṛkātvamuktam suratādirasairyasyā baddhaḥ pārśvagataḥ priyaḥ sāmoda guṇasaṃprāptā bhavetsvādhīnabhartṛkā  nivedya duḥkhaṃ sukhī bhavediti pūrvānubhūtaduḥkhaṃ nivedayati  aviratetyādi udvartamānamunmūlitaṃ bandhanaṃ sthairya yasya tat bandhanaṃ svasthānāvasthānaṃ tasyodvartanamunmūlanārambha iti pāṭhāntaravyākhyā gamitāścetyādinā vyādhyavasthoktā ativāhitātikrāntā candrātapa iti tāpakāritvādātapaḥ eteṣāmanarthatvamāha bharataḥ   saṃbhoge ye sukhaṃ kuryuste duḥkhaṃ virahe bhṛśam  iti smartavyetyanena karuṇavyābhicāribhāvaṃ smaraṇamāha yadāha vyabhicāriṇosya nirvedo glānimaraṇavyādhidainyabhramādayaḥ nairāśyācca maraṇodayaḥ yadāha  sarvairetaiḥ pratīkārairyadi nāsti samāgamaḥ kāmāgninā pradīptāyā jāyate maraṇaṃ dunmucya pīḍaṇeṇa paccakkhaṃ ṇiruddhaṃ piasahīe apacchimaṃ kamalapahmalo  palasuumāro sadpatta sadapattapuṇḍa saṃpuṇṇa canda maṇḍalāhiramassa muhassa mahosavo loaṇāṇaṃ dūsahā āsa rambhadūmaṇāia durmanāyita ṭī  parāo hiaeṇa ṣaṣṭhoṅkaḥ mādhavaḥ  apavārya hanta ekīkṛtastvaci niṣiktaṃ ivāvapīḍya nirbhugnapīnakucakusalayānayā me karpūrahāraharicandana candrakāntaniḥsyandaśaivalamṛṇāla himādivargaḥ mālatī  svagatam aho lavaṅgikayā mālatī vipralabdhā aho lavaṃṅgiāe māladī vippaladdhā mādhavaḥayi svacittavedanāmātravedana paravyathanabhijñe iyamupālabhyase uddāmadehaparidāhamahājvarāṇi saṃkalpasaṃgamavinoditavedanāni tvatsnehasaṃvidavalambitajīvitāni kiṃ vā mayāpi na dinānyativāhitāni lava  sakhi upālambhanīyaivopālabdhāsi sahi uvālambhaṇijjeva uvāladdhāsi tataḥ  vipralambhakaruṇānantaraṃ sthāyinaḥ śṛṅgārasyopakrama māha  eṣā ceti sādhvasaṃ bhayam mādhavaḥ hanta harṣe ekīkṛta ityādi anayā mālalyā karpūrādivarga ekīkṛtaḥ sannāliṅgaya me tvaci niṣikta iva sparśasya tvagindriyagrāhyatayā tvacītyuktam nirbhinnau nirantaravalagnau pīnau stanakuṭūmalau yasyāstayā haricandanaṃ candanaviśeṣaḥ niḥsyandena dravyābhidhānam kṛdabhihito bhāvo dravyavaprakāśate  iti nyāyāt niḥsyandīti pāṭhe niḥsyandinaḥ sarasā śaivālādaya ityarthaḥ anena praśānto me kāmajastāpa ityuktam bahūpameyam ātmānurāgaprakāśanāyānubhūtavedanāmāha  ayīti uddābhetyādi etādṛśāni dināni mayāpi kiṃ vā nātikrāntāni api tvatikrāntānyeva kiṃ veti saṃbhāvanāyām yadvā kiṃ niṣedhe vaivārthe kīdṛśāni uddāma udbhaṭo dehadāha eva mahājvaro yeṣu etenodvega uktaḥ saṃkalpasaṃgamenāpanītā vyathā yeṣu anenonmāda uktaḥ yadāhabāhū prasārya gamanaṃ saṃkalpākalpite priye nivṛttiḥ sahasānyasminnunmāde hi prajāyate  yadvā saṃkalpasaṃgamenānyastrīdveṣaḥ sūcitastena ca niḥsapatnīkatvaṃ kanyāharaṇabījamāha yadāha   āsaktiṃ vā darśayetsukhamanupahata mekapatnīkatve vā varṇayet iti tvadīya snehajñānenāvalambitaṃ jīvitaṃ yeṣu tvatsnehājñāne mama maraṇameva syādityāśayaḥ  upalabdhiścitsaṃvit ityamaraḥ lavaṅgikā viṣakta nirbhinna aāhe nive vyasanā vinodana nivedita ṇijjaṃ mālatīmādhave sarasaramaṇīyatā saṃvidhānasya aho sarasaramakala  aho gīadā saṃvihāṇassa maka  mahābhāge evametat tvaṃ vatsaleti kathamadhyavalambitātmā satyaṃ janoyaṃmiyato divasānanaiṣīt ābaddha kaṃkaṇakarapraṇayaprasādamāsādya nandatu cirāya phalantu kāmāḥ lava  mahānubhāva hṛdayepyapratihatasvayaṃgrāhasāhasoyaṃ janaḥ kimidānīṃ kaṃkaṇābharaṇaṃ karaṃ vicārayati mahāṇuhāva hiae vi appaḍihadasaaṃgāhasāhaso aaṃ jaṇo dāṇiṃ kiṃ kaṃkaṇābharaṇaṃ karaṃ viāredi mālatī  hā dhik kanyakājanaviruddhaṃ kimapyeṣopanyasyati haddhi kaiṇṇaājaṇaviruddhaṃ kiṃ vi esā uvaṇṇassadi praviśya kāmandakī kaṇṭakaḥ kṣudraśatrau ca romāñcepi ca dṛśyate  iti viśvaḥ ārdrāṅgulya eva dalāni patrāṇi yasya tam romāñcitatvārdratve sātvikabhāvāt ahaṃ kīdṛśaḥ anaṅga eva grīṣmastena taptaḥ tathā ca bhagavatīvacanasaṃvidhānaiḥ kṣemeṇa gopāyito makarandaḥadya vaiyamapi nandanāvāsamupagatāḥ tato bhagavatī nandanamāpṛcchaya gatā nijāvasatham ayaṃ ca navavadhūgṛhapraveśaviracitā
